Page 23

電影專刊

逹利歐氏預言　好萊塢今年的動向（上）

— 炳賤

嘉寳將永遠脱離影壇

范朋克將重返好萊塢

關於世界大事的預言，今年我们已經見了很多，可是關於電颢界的預言，似平還不多見。

美國電影應誌"Modern　Screen"本年二月份上登載了一篇關於好萊塢的預言。預言者是在好萊塢馳名的逹利歐氏（Dareos）。逹氏在去年年初亦曾作過同樣的預言，他預言了六十八件事。在這六十八件事之中的有四十八件，卽百分之七十；猜错的有八件，卽百分之十一，無結果的是十二件，佔百分之十七。他的預言雖然不見得是百分之百的凖確，然而這百分之七十的預中也頗有可觀了。茲擇譯其中比較重要的，錄之於下：

我們先説去年最紅的梅蕙絲。逹氏預言梅蕙絲一九三四年仍舊度着獨身生活。雖然這一年她信舊地浪漫下去，可是她終於會保持梅蕙絲小姐的尊稱的。在影壇上的地位，她將更形鞏固而成爲一顆最紅的星。不過在財務方面，她在槪總要損失一些。

其次，説到瓊克勞馥。克勞馥今年的成績可謂登峯造極。可是過此以後，好將一年不如一年地失敗下去。在愛的方面，她或自己以爲滿意，可是她終於找不到眞正的愛。要到一九三五年，她才能重新爲人之妻。

説到嘉寳，那簡直是晦氣極了。她今後不能再表現列驚人的成績。假如一九三四她不放棄影壇生活，那末至遲一九三五終要退休，而且是最後的永遠的退本。她將重回她瑞典的故鄕。

珍妮蓋諾這個可愛的小鳥，今年又要做新娘了。縱然本年她不能于歸，可是至遲年底以前，她必定宣布訂婚。未來的郎君要比她年紀大，而且是一個離過婚的男人。一九三五年上她將生一個小寳寳，在影壇上她還有兩年好運。過此以後，她就該退休了。

那末克萊克寳呢？寳一定仍和她現在的丈夫白耳（Rex　Bell）繼續和好下去。她今年將舉一子。這小孩子將來一定會成名。可是究竟從哪一方面－－銀幕，舞臺，或其他？－－出名，現在却還不得而知。

琪恩哈羅今年運氣也不佳。今年將有無數的流言毁謗她在逹氏的圓光鏡上，一切的星座都和哈羅站在敵對的地位。假如她能度此難關，那末將來也有兩年的好運。

凱絲琳海嬪去年是走了好運的。今年却不甚得勢。離然本年她將遇到不少的打擊，可是她終必能够向上爬。今的她個人方面當感到一個很大的痛苦。（未完）

觀衆意見

評「熱血青年」

— 綠意

「熱血青年」是天一公司與「青春之火」個性和情調完全相反的作品。導演湯傑是進天一公司第一部作品，在技巧上，比在明星導演的「母與子」進步不少了。全劇用一種沉重滯緩的調子，更能增加悲劇（雖然熱血青年並不是完整的悲劇）的成！小聰明處也有，如用香烟灰來示李父心情的進慮：用克儉子打翻飯桶來象徵克儉父子的失業等。象徵的應用是同「飄零」裏一樣的手法，這可惜成爲天一公司的老調了。

天一公司的作品還有一個共通的缺點，那就是每部作品裏都有幾節滑稽的插穿！在「青春之火」裏是僕人的怪臉相；現在在「熱血青年」裏是那鄰婦的動作和收賬員的神情，最能破壞劇情的嚴肅空氣。製作者爲了要歡迎一般低級趣味而設此，我們實在是不敢贊同。要知滑稽的插穿在輕鬆的喜劇裏還能稍用，在悲苦的情調裏應用了反而大大的削弱了劇力的。

「熱血青年」還拖了一個大尾巴。這個尾巴完全破壞了悲劇的情緒，使觀衆帶回了一個印象：奸商終于被捕了－這雖大快人心而對于克儉父母之死的同情心却消滅了不少！我認爲在結束如果改爲克儉警察至運貨機關時因證據無着以誣告罪入獄，那末在結構上完成了完整的悲劇，于觀衆方面更加强了對奸商的憤恨，那末不更好嗎？

評「人生」

— 克洛

在技巧方面，「人生」可以説是超過了一切國產影片。攝影的清晰美妙，設置的合理匀稱，鏡頭的周轉靈活，演員的稱職盡力，都是無懈可擊，而値得令人讚賞的；尤其是這次費穆用了那新頴的導演手法－遲緩的旋律，使每個觀衆的心中都受到沉重的壓迫，而加重了悲劇的力量。

可是，在意識方面，我認爲他不特比不上「春蠶」「鹽潮」等片，却有很大的退化！牠的中心意識是「善」與「惡」的爭鬥，要使人轉「惡」爲「善」，必須用教育的力量。這樣説來，牠就有三個缺點：

（一）沒有着力描寫「惡」的成因；

（二）想用教育的力量來使人轉「惡」爲「善」，簡直是一種幻想。現社會的經濟結構未改善以前，所謂教育，結果被特權階級用來作爲栽培奴才的一種工具，不特不能使人轉「惡」爲「善」，或者還要產生多量作惡的人！

（三）把希望統統放在「未來」，而抛棄了「現實」！

然而站在人道的觀點上説來，這部颢片很有力量令人洒兩點同情之涙的！

「人生」之我見

— 越熙

「人生」之演出，雖不敢説已突過了中國影片的一切成績而躍登了世界地位，但，的確是一張不可多得而値得贊美的颢片，尤其是從技巧方面去觀察。

如以「打鐵」象徵着「人生的鍜鍊」，就是劇作者的極聰明地方。固然，這是非有藝術修養的人，不易理解；但以迎合低級觀衆的心理，而故意降低藝術的凖則，這是極不合理而且愚笨不過的事。電影本身，就是負著提高觀衆藝術理解力的使命的。

再如：圖面展示火車進行，接著就是林阮見面．這裏省去不少的不必要的圖面，是很可取的。他如由費柏青抽槍轉到入獄，等都是導演者很經濟的手法，是中國片中未曾多覯的。

光線之清晰，圖面之美妙；無疑地，是無可非難，令人滿意。

演員方面，我覺阮玲玉演得最逼眞，最努力，最成功，也最能給觀衆深刻的印象。費柏青面孔狡滑，洽合劇情，也算是成功的。鄭君里未能給觀衆以深刻印象，我們應該原諒他作戲的機會太少。其餘演員，都能稱職。此外我們那位佔據兒童演員首席的小明星－黎鏗，在這裏，成績似乎還趕不上過去的「城巿之夜」和「人道」（下略）

評「人生」

— 徐孟淦

現社會是萬惡的畸形。人生便是描摹叙述這畸形社會的一角。

在「人生」裏的主人翁；一個是從野孩子和奴婢脱胎的路柳牆花，一個是不願意理沒在粉筆灰裏的小學敎員，和他的一個在育嬰堂裏服務的妻子。在這種情形之下，於是便演成了一幕無上愴痛悽慘的悲劇。

關於導演的技術，費穆是比「城巿之夜」中更進步了。他雖然不説明劇中人的一切，但他能假借劇中人的中吻來表明，而且還叙述得有條不紊，這是他獨具特長的作風。

關於演員的表情上。那末以玩玲玉林楚楚最爲動人，黎鑑的天眞，鄭君里的英俊，均皆可取，其他演員亦各能各盡所長。至關攝影佈景及其他，均較前爲進步。

總之：在萌芽時代的國產片中「人生」是一部超特的作品。同時還能够看到中國影業是在突飛猛進着，是緊追着外國片了。

大上海映「獵艷家」

充滿着愉快情調的喜劇

「獵艷家」Facing　The　Music，是一部英國出品的音樂喜劇，主角史丹盧璧諾，是「璇宮艷史」滑稽侍者盧别麟的介弟，在歐洲銀壇上的聲譽，不亞於好萊塢的希佛萊，這個亢子，完全是運用美好的音樂，悦耳的歌曲，然後再聨合電影的技術所組合成功的，所以，不但全片滑稽有趣；而裏面所包含的歌曲，都是非常著名的，在劇壇上最有悠久歷史的「浮士德」，其中有「珠寳歌」一曲，也被搬演到膠片上來，這是很値得注意的，並且，飾演那位女角的，也是歐洲一位著名的歌星，最可喜的，就是在導演的明確的描寫之下，各個演員，均能把握着各劇中人特有的個性，喜劇能够有這樣很好的成績，確屬不易，這部片子，已定於今天（七日）起在大上海大戲院開映了。

電影小說

克利斯丁娜Queen　Chrina（六）

— 笏臣

一回客店門外，已有人馬喧　的聲音，她知道那隊西班牙人到了。她看着他們一個一個的跑進了客店。她聽見那個欽差問店主人要房間。她看見那让主人搖着肩膀，連聲道歉。店主人眼望着克利斯丁娜，好像説她就是使他沒有房间睡的原因。於是那欽差就急速地跑到她面前。他脱了帽子深深地鞠了一躬。他说：「先生，用我未得識荆，多有失禮之處，現在特地在此告罪了。」克利斯丁娜笑了，她説：「先生，用你不用道樣謙恭，那個金鎊，我是很快樂地賺來的。」那少年又説道：「先生，這眞使我惶恐無地了。克利斯丁娜道：「先生，那亦沒有理由呀。總怪我自己穿的衣服太不像樣了」，她看看自己穿的粗羊皮的上褂，「我們第一次見面，不是衣服的外表，就表示身份的嗎？」那男子看了她道：「先生，我希望你能讓我比較再深切些認識你。你可以給我一個面子，讓我請你吃晚飯呢？」克利斯丁娜道：「同吃晚飯是可惟的祗要你肯讓我作主人。你是遠來的客，我一定要略盡地主之誼。我今天請你吃晚飯，你能賞光嗎？并且你從那裹來的貴國，我是懷着深切的系念的。」那少年欽差一方面推却着，一方面表示驚異地問她：「你知道西班牙嗎？」克利斯丁娜笑道：「西班牙是深知道的。我還想從你探取一些最近的新聞。佛辣斯吉斯有什麽新的藝術作品嗎？加爾特龑臟在瑪德里近來作些什麽？」

他顯然地驚訝起來了。他問：「你上次什麽時候在西班牙的？」克利斯丁娜道：「我去是沒有去過，不過我是常常思念的。」那西班牙人的黑眼睛，透着光彩説道：「多末有趨呀！幸得相會，我心中喜悦，你是不會知道的：：：店主人！」店主人來了。那少年吩咐道：「這位先生，今天同我晚餐，你搶頂好的預備好了。」他然後回過頭來，對着克利斯丁娜道：「你曾得過思鄕病嗎？」克利斯丁娜表示着抱歉道：「我從來沒有離開過瑞典國境。」那少年道：「那你就不會知道那種損失的滋味的。那是一種念舊的傷悼。」克利斯丁娜徐徐地道：「你知道沒有到過的地方，一個人亦會因思家而悒鬰的嗎？「這尤其使他驚佩起來了。他説：「那是當然可以的。這又是第二次我失敬於你了。你是希有的青年。來吧」他拉了她的手，走到食桌前面。

那一頭店主人和他的老婆商量着：那個少年給了二十兩，可是那個外國人答應出三十兩，祇要有一張床睡覺就興。現在他看着克利斯西娜和寻個外國少年，談得很入港，於是他就走了上來。他很狡滑地沒有開口先笑着説道：「我想你們二位先生是很要好的朋友了。如果可以的話，我們可以想個法子，使這位先生亦可以得過安身之處。」他説着乎指着那西班牙欽差。（未完）

1934.02.07

Sun's Troops Violently Attack Ningyuan, Both Sides Engaged in Fierce Fighting

A Large Portion of Reinforcements Arrive

Sun Expresses No Response to Dismissal Order

He Yingqin Convenes Generals to Discuss Handling Sun's Troops

(Beiping) A large portion of the reinforcements has arrived. The battle situation in the front lines in recent days has been extremely fierce. Sun, due to the authorities dismissing him from all his concurrent positions, is determined to take risks and will not abandon his troops. He plans to capture Ningyuan in the short term and, after looting, continue westward. If the strength of Gansu, Ningxia, and Qinghai is too strong, he will proceed westward along the Mongolian border north of Ningxia. Sun has stated that even if he becomes a bandit, he is determined to move westward and will not respond to He Yingqin's telegram. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) Last night, Beiping received a telegram from Ningxia stating that the Gansu and Qinghai troops had arrived in Ningxia to reinforce the area. Ma Hongkui's troops within the city are preparing to launch a counterattack. The villages near the provincial capital are still occupied by Sun's troops, while Ma's troops surround the outside of the villages. Both sides have been engaged in fierce fighting for days. Sun's troops have prepared many scaling ladders, intending to break through after the reinforcements arrive and attack the provincial capital again. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) Military News: Ma Bufang telegraphed on the 5th, stating that Sun's troops have been besieging Ningyuan for over ten days. Fortunately, our soldiers have fought bravely with all their might, and the defenses of the provincial capital and Pingluo are solid. Fierce fighting continued in the front lines for the past two days. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) After Sun's troops defied orders and moved westward, war broke out in the Northwest. The Central Government originally advocated settling the matter peacefully and did not want the situation to escalate. The Military Affairs Commission repeatedly telegraphed to dissuade him without success. Therefore, Sun was first stripped of his position as the Qinghai Western Region Reclamation Commissioner to cut off his intention to move westward. Yesterday, he was also dismissed from his position as the commander of the 41st Army. If he continues to defy orders, the authorities of Gansu, Ningxia, Qinghai, Shanxi, and Suiyuan will be responsible for enforcing the order. Although Sun has not yet expressed his attitude, the Military Affairs Commission has already issued a final warning. Therefore, Sun's personnel stationed in Beiping have now left Beiping separately. Yan has expressed his agreement with the Central Government's opinion. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) It is rumored that the destination of Sun's westward advance is northern Shaanxi. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) The main force of Sun's troops is currently still concentrated north of the provincial capital of Ningxia, launching fierce attacks on the provincial capital from time to time. The fighting has been extremely intense for days. Zhu Shaoliang ordered Ma Bufang and Ma Buqing's two divisions to advance to Ningyuan and Pingluo for reinforcement. Ma Bufang has arrived near Ningxia, and the Gansu reinforcements are advancing towards Zhongwei and Ningshuo. Sun is very busy going back and forth between Dengkou and Shizuizi to command. Sun's troops, including Lu Fengnian's division and two replenishment regiments transferred from Baotou to Ningxia Province, passed through Linhe on the 3rd and are concentrating in Dengkou. This time, the Military Affairs Commission ordered Yu Shiming to be responsible for commanding Sun's troops to retreat and gather north of Dengkou, and to strictly reduce and reorganize the troops according to the approved number of seven regiments. The approved seven regiments are the 117th Division, the 118th Division, one special service regiment, one company each of engineers and transport troops, and one wireless telegraph team. All the rest will be dismissed. The Military Affairs Commission approved the number of Sun's troops to be 15,000, with a salary of 201,000 yuan paid by the Military Affairs Commission, a monthly subsidy of 40,000 yuan from the Central Government, and a monthly allowance of 70,000 yuan from Shanxi Province. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) He Yingqin convened the generals of North China at Jurentang last night to discuss the handling of Sun's troops. Sun himself is still in the army and has not yet expressed his position on the dismissal order. Ma Hongkui's troops plan to shorten their lines after a considerable period, and to contact Ma Hongbin, Ma Bufang, and Ma Buqing's three divisions to launch a counterattack. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

Pingluo Still Held by Ma's Troops

(Beiping) Military News: The Military Affairs Commission received a telegram from Ningxia today stating that Pingluo is still held by Ma's troops and has not been captured by Sun's troops. Sun's cavalry has been discovered in the Dingyuan Post and the Ningshuo area, where Ma Buqing's cavalry is concentrated. The main force of the Gansu army is advancing towards the Yandi Zhongwei Hongjingshan area. Wuyuan and Linhe are still defended by Wang Jingguo's troops from Shanxi. Zhao Chengzhou's cavalry originally stationed one brigade in Pingdiquan, one brigade in Suiyuan, and one brigade in Baotou. It is heard that the brigade stationed in Baotou will move into Linhe. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

Sun's Office in Beiping Closed

(Beiping) Sun Dianying's office in Beiping was officially closed today. All the staff in the office were given severance pay by Wang Shiping and dismissed. The office was emptied. Sun's representative, Hu Jie, came to Beiping three days ago and went to Tianjin this morning. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) Guihua Telegram: Sun's office in Baotou has been automatically withdrawn today. According to the representative of the Military Affairs Commission, Men Bingyue, Pingluo and Ningxia have not been captured by Sun's troops. The rumor that Pingluo and Ningxia have fallen is incorrect. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) Zhangjiakou Telegram: Yang Mingluan, the chief of the Finance Department of the 41st Army Cavalry Headquarters, returned to Baotou after completing his business in Beiping. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

Sun Directing Military Affairs in Dengkou

(Beiping) Those coming to Beiping from Baotou say that Sun's headquarters are still located in Dengkou, and Sun himself is directing military affairs there. There are no traces of Sun's troops east of the Yellow River. Most of Sun's troops are concentrated on both banks of the Yellow River. The fighting in Pingluo has been the most intense in recent days. Sun's troops, led by Bao Liansi, are launching a fierce attack on that area. The 15th Route Army's office in Beiping has not received any information from the front lines for three days, but it is heard that the fighting in the front lines has been extremely intense recently. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

Sun Can Avoid Further Investigation If He Obeys Orders

(Beiping) After the Beiping Military Affairs Commission explicitly dismissed Sun Dianying from all his concurrent positions on the 5th, no reply telegram was received from the front lines on the 6th. It is still difficult to predict whether Sun will hand over military power and leave the army in compliance with orders. However, Sun is currently still directing operations in Dengkou, harassing the vicinity of Ningxia. According to various observations, Sun's westward invasion is audacious and self-inflicted. It is feared that he may not immediately realize his mistake. The authorities here believe that if Sun leaves the army and hands over his troops to Yu Shiming, Liu Yueting, and others to command, retreating to the area north of Dengkou and implementing a reduction in force, Sun personally can be given a path to self-renewal without further investigation. Otherwise, the matter must be thoroughly resolved to maintain discipline. As for the situation in Ningxia, according to investigations, there is still no change. The rumor that Sun's troops invaded Pingluo cannot be confirmed. The troops stationed in Gansu have now arrived in Ningyuan, preparing for a counterattack. The 41st Army's office in Beiping is being closed due to the cancellation of the army's designation, and all office personnel left Beiping and scattered on the 6th. (Sixth Day Central News Agency Telegram)

Sun's Office in Nanjing Sealed Up

(Nanjing) Sun Dianying's office in Nanjing was sealed up last night by a platoon of military police dispatched by the Military Police Headquarters. The director of the office, Liu Huanzhang, his son Ruoyan, and other staff had already left Nanjing earlier. Only two messengers were left to guard the office. Also, Sun's representative in Nanjing, Lu Yuting, was summoned to the Military Police Department last night and temporarily detained, pending further instructions. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) After Sun Dianying's dismissal, the Military Police Department inspected Sun's office in Nanjing on the evening of the 5th and interrogated his representative Lu Yuting. He was released on the evening of the 6th and ordered to close the office immediately. (Sixth Day Central News Agency Telegram)

Sun Dianying Cables Military Authorities

(Nanjing) Military News: Sun Dianying sent a telegram to the military authorities on the 6th, expressing remorse and willingness to relinquish military power, handing it over to Deputy Commander Yu to lead, and awaiting reorganization by the Central Government. The authorities have always been lenient. If Sun's expression is sincere, they will not hold him accountable for the past. Otherwise, the armies of Gansu, Ningxia, Qinghai, and Shanxi will jointly encircle and suppress him. It is expected that the main force of his troops can be completely defeated within a month. (Sixth Day Central News Agency Telegram)

Taking Over Gubeikou to Start with Administration

Japanese Troops Cannot Withdraw Temporarily, Cancellation of Puppet Organization Awaits Negotiation

Sun Shutang and Yin Rugeng Discuss Details After Takeover

(Beiping) Yin Rugeng said that when taking over Gubeikou, administrative matters should be handled first. The Japanese troops stationed there cannot withdraw temporarily because there are no barracks outside the pass. As for whether the puppet tax authorities established by the puppet organization in the pass can be abolished immediately, negotiations with the Japanese side will continue during the takeover. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) Regarding the takeover of Gubeikou, Yin Rugeng has been actively preparing for days. Yin visited Shibayama, a Japanese official, to discuss the handover procedures. The Japanese side stated that as long as our side is well prepared, the takeover can be carried out. Sun Shutang, the magistrate of Ningyun County, arrived in Beiping today, and together with Wei Wen, the chief of the Security Corps, and others, visited Yin to discuss the establishment of a public security bureau and all the details after the takeover of Gubeikou. Tomorrow, Yin will make a final contact with the Japanese side to determine the date of the takeover. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) The Japanese troops in Malanyu have built a small airfield with one or two small planes parked there for transporting supplies. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) Kobayashi, the commander of the Japanese Navy stationed in the puppet state, is scheduled to arrive in Beiping from Liaoning on the 11th of this month to visit Huang He. It is heard that Kobayashi's trip is of a recreational nature and he will not stay in Beiping for long before returning to Changchun. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

Tao Shangming Arrives in Tangshan

Yuguan Approved for Takeover on the 10th

(Beiping) Tao Shangming arrived in Tangshan from Tianjin on the evening of the 5th. Tao is scheduled to go to Yuguan on the 20th with Su Yu-ke and Lin Chih-ming, the secretary of the Commissioner's Office, to negotiate and implement the takeover of Yuguan. Yuguan is approved for takeover on the 10th. The Japanese side has stated that Yuguan will be returned to our side on the 10th. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

Japanese Military Actions Increasingly Active on the Chahar Border

Military Preparations Completed

(Beiping) The actions of the Japanese army on the Chahar border have indeed become more active recently. Four roads have been built from Rehe to Chahar and Tongliao. A large amount of military supplies has been stockpiled. A certain military expert observed that the Japanese army's military preparations have been completed and are only waiting for the opportunity to realize their actions. Therefore, the situation on the Chahar border is extremely tense. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

Chen Jitang Submits Proposals for Post-Disaster Management in Fujian Province

The 19th Route Army to be Reorganized and Transferred to Jiangxi to Suppress Bandits

Guangdong Will No Longer Subsidize the Army's Expenses

Guangdong's Troops Entering Fujian Will Not Leave Fujian for the Time Being

(Nanjing) Chen Jitang submitted a telegram to Chairman Chiang regarding his opinions on reorganizing the remnants of the 19th Route Army: (1) Advocate that the army be transferred to Jiangxi to suppress bandits. (2) Guangdong Province will not continue to subsidize the army's expenses. (3) All past relations between the army and the Southwest and Guangdong Province will be completely severed after the reorganization. (4) The troops from Guangdong Province entering Fujian will not leave Fujian for the time being before the army is transferred elsewhere. (5) Senior generals of the army must be sanctioned by the Central Government to prevent any future ambitions. In addition, there are detailed opinions on various issues of preventing the remnants from fleeing and causing trouble. It is heard that Chairman Chiang has replied to Chen's proposals, generally stating that after he arrives in Fujian and convenes a meeting with the army's new and old generals, a decision can be made. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

Wang Zhengting Left Fujian After Attending Swearing-in Ceremony

(Establishment of the Fujian Provincial Government: Chiang Ting-wen Relieved of Administrative Responsibilities)

(Fuzhou) Wang Zhengting said that he came to Fujian to attend the swearing-in ceremony and has no other tasks. Wang gave a speech on construction issues at the Dongjie Theater this morning and is scheduled to go to Mawei this afternoon to take the Hairong back to Nanjing. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

(Fuzhou) Chiang Ting-wen strictly prohibits various militia groups from forcibly collecting group weapons. Chiang was previously ordered by the Executive Yuan to handle administrative affairs in Fujian Province. Now that the provincial government has been established, he has submitted a report to be relieved of all administrative responsibilities. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

(Fuzhou) Chen Jiliang did not leave on the 6th due to lung disease. The provincial land forces returned to their original defenses on the 6th. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

(Fuzhou) Sha Yong's remaining bandits have been bombarded by the air forces for days, resulting in over a thousand deaths and numerous captures. Lu Xingbang sent Chief of Staff Chen Dingyuan to the province to report on the suppression situation. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

(Xiamen) Zhang Zhen returned to Xiamen from the province on the Shanghai-Guangdong flight on the 6th. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

Shen Dexie Leads Two Planes Away From Anhui to Fly to Hangzhou to Return to the Team

(Anqing) Shen Dexie, the chief of the Military Affairs Department of the Aviation Administration, led the Anhui No. 1 destroyer and the Zhejiang No. 15 and No. 2 destroyer planes away from Anhui at 10:00 a.m. on the 6th, flying to Nanjing and then to Hangzhou to join the division's organization. The two training planes from the Aviation School flew directly to Hangzhou. People from all walks of life saw them off. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) The five planes from the Aviation Administration that flew to Anhui on the 5th to participate in the naming ceremony of the Anhui No. 1 plane were warmly welcomed by people from all walks of life in Anhui. The planes returned to Nanjing from Anhui at 11:00 a.m. on the 6th. (Sixth Day Central News Agency Telegram)

Chiang and Zhang's Travels in Hangzhou

(Hangzhou) Zhang Xueliang and Yu Dawei went to Chenglu to visit Chiang this morning. Yu left first, and then Chiang went out of the city with Zhang. They returned to their residence at 1:00 p.m. Zhang visited the downtown area in plain clothes at 2:00 p.m. and bought local products. He returned to his residence at 4:00 p.m. At 8:00 p.m., Lu Dipin hosted a banquet for Zhang at the Xileng Hotel, inviting party and government officials to accompany them. The date of Chiang's departure from Hangzhou is still undecided. Huang Shaoxiong came to Hangzhou yesterday to visit Chiang and ask for instructions on border affairs. He returned to Nanjing on the morning of the 6th. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

He Zhuguo Temporarily Stationed in Zhangde to Command

(Beiping) Zhangde Telegram: He Zhuguo left Handan at 2:00 p.m. on the 5th, passed through Cizhou at 7:00 p.m., and gave Bai Fengxiang instructions in person. He arrived in Zhangde at 9:00 p.m., met with Gao Guizi, and inquired about the bandit situation in the front lines. Due to changes in the bandit situation, He stationed at the Zhangde Railway Station that night to command. He will proceed to Xinxiang after the bandit situation in the front lines is determined. The remaining bandits who gathered in Lucoulou, 30 li southwest of Tangyin County on the afternoon of the 4th, were surrounded and suppressed by the infantry of Li Regiment and Shi Regiment, and the cavalry of Guo Division. The bandits were heavily besieged on the morning of the 6th. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) The Hebei Provincial Government received a telegram on the 6th that Liu Guitang's bandit gang of over a thousand people was chased by He Zhuguo and Guo Xipeng's troops and fled to Linxian, Henan, intending to cross the Yellow River and flee south. He and Guo's troops are in pursuit. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

Xiao and Kong's Bandits Disturb the Hinterland of Western Jiangxi

Direct Trains to Pingxiang South Resume

(Nanchang) Xiao and Kong's bandits, due to their nests being occupied by the Western Route Army, are disturbing the hinterland of western Jiangxi. Currently, the bandits in Shanggao and Gaoan have been defeated by the 1st and 2nd Columns, and the commander of the puppet 2nd Division, Zhong Biao, has been killed. The bridges on the Jiangxi-Hunan Road have also been repaired, and direct trains to Pingxiang South have resumed today. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

(Nanchang) The headquarters ordered that all exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous levies be exempted in the newly recovered areas to benefit the remnants of the Soviet area. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

(Changsha) Chen Quzhen has added Gu Jiaqi's brigade to assist in the suppression of He Long's bandits who are attacking Yongshun. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

(Changsha) Kong and Cai's bandits have suffered heavy casualties after being encircled and suppressed by the 1st and 2nd Columns and bombed by planes on the 4th and 5th. They are currently hiding in the deep mountains of Fenghuang Mountain Huangshanao area and are being tightly besieged, making it difficult for the bandits to escape. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

(Nanchang) Chiang appointed Luo Lin as the commander of the Jiangxi West Bank Defense Zone in Jiangxi. The west bank of the Gan River is his responsibility. Luo and Wang's division attacked Taihe Lujiang together, defeating the puppet Hunan-Jiangxi Independent 2nd Brigade of 4,000 men, killing a puppet regiment commander. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

Bandits on the Border of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui Have Been Cleared

(Hankou) The bandits on the border of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui have been cleared. Only one group is fleeing west of Anhui. Liu Zhenhua ordered Liu Maoen to supervise the suppression. The three provinces received 20,000 refugees each from Hubei and Anhui, and Henan has 100,000 people being received. After the remaining bandits in southern Hubei fled to Tongshan, scattered bandits were also discovered in Puchi, causing public panic. Feng Xingxian and Liu Ji immediately returned to Hankou from Puchi to search and suppress them. Xiao Zhichu came to Hankou yesterday to report to the headquarters and the Pacification Office on the situation of defeating the bandits in Henan, and returned to his defense on the 6th. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

(Hankou) The East Hubei Immigration Office has established reformation and relief centers outside Huang'an City Datangwan, each receiving 1,500 people. The remaining 30,000 refugees scattered in various villages are currently being investigated for the allocation of wasteland. The relief center also has a disaster children's school and adult vocational classes. (Sixth Day Central News Agency Telegram)

Zhu and Mao Convene the All-Soviet Congress in Ruijin

(Nanchang) A refugee from the Central Soviet Area said that all able-bodied men in the bandit area have been conscripted, even 60-year-old men. The local people in various places have disappeared. Zhu and Mao convened the All-Soviet Congress in Ruijin. The venue was set up in the Xiaojiantounao area under the Shazhou Dam in Ruicheng. The conference period was from the 18th to the 27th. Zhu De, Mao Zedong, Xiang Ying, and Zhou Enlai all participated. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

Ministry of Communications Sends Personnel to Xinjiang to Prepare for Aviation

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Communications has sent Gao Xibing and Gu Gengye to Xinjiang to consult with the local military and political authorities of the province on the resumption of the Eurasia Aviation Xinjiang Line and to request their convenience. Gao and Gu have prepared their luggage and will travel by sea to Vladivostok and then enter Xinjiang via the Siberian Railway. If there are no military affairs in the province, the route can be opened in March after negotiations. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

Ma Zhongying Repeatedly Attacks Dihua Unsuccessfully

(Moscow) News received here from Dihua reports that Ma Zhongying is currently leading Donggan troops to violently attack Dihua. The government troops are holding firm and defending it. Although Ma has received a large amount of military supplies, he has been repeatedly defeated, suffering heavy losses. Reinforcements from the provincial capital have now arrived, so it is heard that many Donggan troops are surrendering to the authorities. (Sixth Day Reuters Telegram)

(Moscow) According to a dispatch from Dihua, the Xinjiang provincial army and Ma's troops are still in conflict. Ma's troops are well-equipped with weapons, but their attempt to occupy Dihua has been repeatedly thwarted, so their subordinates have suffered heavy losses. Currently, the Hui troops in Yili and Tacheng and other places have automatically canceled their resistance to the province and have automatically surrendered their weapons. The representative of the provincial government, Liu Ping (transliteration), has been appointed as the commander of the armies in the Yili area. Liu has now arrived in Yili, and the reorganized troops in the Tacheng and Jiuli areas are under the command of General Zhao (transliteration). His troops have arrived in Suilai to reinforce the Dihua military police. (Fifth Day TASS Telegram)

The National Government Orders Approval for Rezheng to Take Charge of Tibetan Affairs

Military Affairs Still the Responsibility of the Silon Kasha

(Nanjing) Since the passing away of the Dalai Lama in Tibet, all Tibetan political affairs have been handled by the Silon Kasha. Recently, the Tibetan people publicly elected Choekyi Gyaltsen, the Reting Rinpoche, to act as the regent of Tibetan administration. In order to respect the wishes of all Tibetans, the Executive Yuan has requested the National Government to appoint Reting to take full charge of all Tibetan political and religious power. The National Government has issued an order approving it. However, military affairs are still the responsibility of the Silon Kasha. (Sixth Day Central News Agency Telegram)

De Wang's Representative Arrives in Nanjing

Reporting on the Current Situation in Western Mongolia

Applying for the Implementation of Autonomy

(Nanjing) De Wang of Silingol League has again sent Dalkhan Qunwang of Sunid Left Banner, Guoerjiazhuoerzhapu, to Nanjing. According to investigations, Guo left Silingol in late December of last year, stayed in Beiping for two months, and arrived in Nanjing from Beiping on the 4th of this month. Those who came from Mongolia include Panchen Lama Bai Yuting and five attendants. King Guo told others that this time he represents De Wang in going to Nanjing purely to report on the recent situation in Mongolian politics and to apply for the issue of autonomy. Before the various Mongolian princes convened a meeting in Bailingmiao, the Japanese sent personnel to Silingol and set up a radio station in Sunid Left Banner. It was only after negotiations that they agreed to withdraw. However, according to Japanese sources, they still need to come to Silingol this spring to set it up. Seeing their intention, it is obviously the first step in the invasion of Western Mongolia. In order to ensure the future safety of Western Mongolia, De Wang has specially sent me to Nanjing to meet with the government authorities. As for the Inner Mongolian autonomy plan, since it was passed by the Central Political Council on the 17th of last month, the Mongolian side has not been able to accept it because the content is different from the eleven articles discussed by Minister Huang in Bailingmiao. De Wang intends to have a memorandum on the above two items, which will be sent to the Executive Yuan and the Military Affairs Commission by myself. As for the recent situation in Western Mongolia, since the Manchurian Incident, the Japanese have been advancing westward step by step. Fortunately, the Mongolian people are deeply aware of righteousness and have not been tempted. Recently, a Chahar-Suiyuan League Flag Office has been established in Duolun. The Mongolian people deeply hope that the Central Government will attach importance to the border troubles and quickly find a way to save the country. They only hope that the Central Government will implement the plan agreed upon in Bailingmiao. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) De Wang's representative, Boin Dalai, came to Beiping from Silingol with King Guo earlier, originally intending to go to Nanjing together to report everything to the Central Government. Later, because Boin had a toothache in Beiping, he could not go. He is now scheduled to take the Beiping-Baotou train back to Zhangjiakou at noon on the 7th to handle the affairs of the Silingol Office in Zhangjiakou. After King Guo returns to Zhang from Nanjing, he will return to Western Sunid to report to De Wang. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) The Mongolian banner representatives in Nanjing do not accept the revised plan of the Inner Mongolia autonomy issue by the Central Political Council. The incident is still unresolved, and the opinions of both sides are far apart. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

Huang Musong Enters Tibet Via Qinghai

Attendants Go Via India

(Nanjing) Huang Musong said that only six attendants will accompany him on this trip to Tibet. The attendants will travel by boat from Shanghai to India and then enter Tibet. He will take a plane to Qinghai and then go to Lhasa from Qinghai. However, this route is inconvenient and will take about a month to arrive. Also, Huang sent attendant Gao Changzhu to the Ministry of Finance today to urge the issuance of travel expenses so that they can leave as soon as possible. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Tibetan representatives Cheng Wenyuan and others intend to prepare a written report and submit it to the Central National Government, the Military Council, the Executive Yuan, the General Staff Department, the Mongolian Association, and other institutions, stating the political and economic situation in Tibet and requesting the dispatch of a special commissioner familiar with Tibetan affairs to Tibet for appeasement. Also, Cheng received a telegram from Tibet yesterday stating that Tenzin Wangdu, a Tibetan youth, was arrested in Tibet. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

Panchen Presents to the Government

One Large Ram's Head

Sent to the Academia Sinica for Display

(Nanjing) During this trip to Nanjing, the Panchen Lama brought a ram's head from Tibet as a gift to the government. It is as big as a dustpan and three times the size of a mainland sheep, which is truly rare. The sheep's head was slaughtered a month ago, but it is still stained with blood. It was sent to the Museum of History of the Academia Sinica for display on the 6th. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

Guangdong Generals Decide to Reallocate Defenses

Armies in Southern Jiangxi Will Not Move for the Time Being

Armies in Western Fujian Stop Advancing

Remnants of the 19th Route Army Will Be Reorganized Into the 3rd Independent Brigade

(Hong Kong) As a result of Chen Jitang's meetings with Yu Hanmou, Li Yangjing, and other generals in recent days, it was decided to reallocate defenses. Zhang Ruigui's division, Deng Longguang's division in Meixian, and Miao Peinan's division in Huizhou are responsible for the eastern Guangdong Chaozhou area. Chen Hanguang's brigade and a part of Miao's division maintain Guangzhou. There will be no increase or decrease in western Guangdong, southern Guangdong, and Hainan Island. Li Hanhun's division is still responsible for the north and south Gan River areas. The armies in southern Jiangxi will not move for the time being. The armies in western Fujian will stop advancing for the time being, awaiting orders. Huang Renhuan's division will stop in Longyan Shizhong, Li Zhenliang's division will stop in Shanghang, and Chen Zhang's brigade will stop in Wuping. Huang Renhuan is responsible for the reorganization of the 19th Route Army. The Guangdong Provincial Government has decided to send personnel to inspect the police forces throughout the province. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) Chen Jitang sent personnel to Longyan to reorganize the remnants of the 19th Route Army, which will be organized into the 3rd Independent Brigade, under the command of a division group. Zhou Yuheng is designated as the brigade commander. Chiang Kai-shek appointed Xue Yue as the commander of the 6th Route Army. Chen Jitang sent military police on the 5th to nail and seal the 19th Route Army's office in Guangdong. The 7th Route will not establish an office in Guangdong because of a lack of funds. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) Huang Zhenqiu told reporters on the 6th that this trip back to China is purely for economic matters and has no other political tasks. Zhang Fakui is still recuperating in Europe and has no intention of returning to China for the time being. (Sixth Day Central News Agency Telegram)

Cui Guangxiu Attends the Southwest Political Conference

(Hong Kong) Cui Guangxiu attended the political conference on the 6th and reported on the progress of attending the Fourth Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee. There was no discussion, but it was decided to send a telegram urging Li Zongren to come to Guangzhou. (Sixth Day Special Dispatch)

Current Affairs Commentary

A Prudent Look at the Balkan Pact

The European continent is fraught with crises, with the potential for explosions everywhere. Some say that today's international relations are even more tense than on the eve of the First World War. This is hardly an exaggeration, even though diplomats from various countries are still trying their best to cover up the situation. At best, they can only temporarily alleviate the situation, but they cannot eliminate the root of the disaster invisibly. The major European powers have been suspicious of each other for a long time, but at present, none of them are willing to take the lead in war and rashly launch an attack. Therefore, a situation of armed peace has been established.

Germany, deeply resentful, is limited by its national strength and cannot easily settle old scores by force. France, enjoying the benefits of the Treaty of Versailles, is complacent and cautious in everything, not daring to act rashly. Italy, under the rule of Mussolini, is deeply dissatisfied with France, but its relationship with Germany is not very good due to its pro-Austrian policy. It is watching the situation to seek its greatest desire. The Soviet Union, due to the increasingly serious situation in the Far East, is unwilling to challenge the Western European countries, lest it be attacked from both sides. Even the Balkan Peninsula countries, known as the powder keg of Europe, have surprisingly become known to the world for drafting a peace pact. The draft of the pact has been signed by Greece, Yugoslavia, Romania, and Turkey. However, Bulgaria has not yet expressed any intention to join. However, if its ruling authorities can be farsighted and carefully consider the pros and cons, they will know that although the establishment of this pact will not help the permanent peace of the Balkans, it is enough to eliminate the dangers of Europe to a certain extent.

There are three reasons why Bulgaria is unwilling to participate in the pact this time. First, it emphasizes the solution of minority issues. Second, it advocates equality in armaments. Third, it seeks access to the Aegean Sea for Bulgaria. Although the full text of the pact has not yet been announced, the four countries including Greece are quite determined to oppose Bulgaria's proposals. We deeply feel that the minority issue is the cause of the Balkan disaster. If a relatively fair solution can be found, then there may be a glimmer of hope for peace. Equality in armaments is originally difficult to achieve perfectly without any bias. The more balance is sought, the more problems arise. Modern countries' armament preparation is all justified by self-defense. In fact, if they can be open and honest with each other, and there is no aggression, then what is so-called self-defense? Therefore, seeking peace through equality in armaments will ultimately not achieve peace. If we truly want to eliminate the scourge of war, we should start by destroying the weapons of killing. Bulgaria's desire to promote equality in armaments in this pact may inevitably repeat the mistakes of the Geneva Disarmament Conference. To go to the Aegean Sea from Bulgaria, it is necessary to pass through Greece. However, Greece will certainly not allow Bulgaria to delve deep into its territory, causing inconvenience to itself. As a result of the European War, Bulgaria lost a lot of land. Bulgaria is firmly opposed to the proposal to maintain the status quo of the Balkans. It is certainly reluctant to comply rashly and work for others if the issue of access to the sea cannot be satisfactorily resolved.

As for the impact of the Balkan Pact on countries outside the contracting parties, it can be summarized in one sentence: Italian imperialism will be severely hit, and the secret door between France and Italy will become even more intensified. Italy has always regarded invading Yugoslavia as one of its national policies, and France is quite wary of this. If the Balkan Pact is successfully established, Yugoslavia can deal with Italy calmly without worrying about its rear. Seeing the frustration of Mussolini's eastward policy, the French will certainly boast of their diplomatic victory. Whether the result can improve German-Italian relations, or even promote the cooperation of the world's two major pan-nationalist countries, is still uncertain, but the far-reaching significance is generally recognized by those who are aware of the situation.

Rumors of Coups and Revolutions Abound

Tens of Thousands of Military Police Suppress Paris

Dismissal of the Police Commissioner Creates a Stir

The Outcome of the House Meeting is Still Uncertain

The New Government is Overwhelmed and Difficult to Sustain

(Paris) Today, the Daladier government will fight for its survival in the parliament. 30,000 police, gendarmes and soldiers are ready to suppress any riots. Rumors are rife throughout the city, with some even saying that a "coup" and a "revolution" will occur. According to the French Action newspaper, machine guns have been installed in the parliament, and traffic within half a mile of the parliament has been temporarily suspended. Therefore, machine guns may not be used. The Paris garrison is currently preparing in the barracks to be ready to move out at any time. Currently, a cavalry team has been transferred from Senlis, and many tanks have been transported from Compiegne. It is believed that the police force can maintain order and will not use force lightly. The Minister of Interior warned the new Police Commissioner Sipriot that if there are any demonstrations, he will be dismissed. At the same time, this intention was conveyed to police officers at all levels. Therefore, in order to maintain their positions, police officers will definitely work hard to maintain public order. On the other hand, the National Veterans Federation announced that it will send 30,000 people to demonstrate, and the Young Patriots League, the Communist Party, the Fascist Party, and the Royalist Party are also gathering. German newspapers have commented a lot on the recent events in Paris, believing that the Daladier government can still control the overall situation and that the royalist coup is impossible. People from all walks of life in Germany have speculated a lot on the impact of the French Prime Minister's reliance on the issue. The dismissal of former Police Commissioner Chiappe has caused a lot of unease among police officers in Paris. When Mr. Chiappe handed over his office, the crowd cheered to send him off. Paris is indeed in a dangerous state. Currently, there is a lot of controversy over the dismissal of Mr. Chiappe. There are now two questions: If Mr. Chiappe is indeed involved in the Bayonne municipal bond fraud case, then why was he promoted to the position of Governor of Morocco? If there is no relationship, then why was he dismissed? (Reuters, 6th)

Daladier's Declaration Thoroughly Investigates No Corruption

(Paris) Daladier's cabinet's declaration of major policies will be decided by today's State Council. The main idea is that the government is determined to thoroughly investigate the recent fraud case and intends to organize a parliamentary investigation committee. Secondly, it asks the parliament to re-discuss the budget and pass it. Mr. Daladier also said that he intends to quickly rectify finances and implement economic policies that meet modern needs. Mr. Daladier's major policy is a concise plan that includes everything. Regarding diplomacy, Mr. Daladier still advocates continuing France's consistent policy, which is to respect treaties and consolidate peace. According to responsible sources, the parliamentary investigation committee for thoroughly investigating the fraud case is planned to be composed of representatives elected by the parliamentary political party groups in proportion to the number of seats occupied by each party, rather than directly appointed by the Presidium of the House of Representatives. The committee will enjoy all the powers necessary for investigation. Regarding this point, Daladier and his cabinet members have all agreed. (Havas, 6th)

The House Meeting is Very Noisy

Unique in the History of French Constitutionalism

The Government's Life May Not Last Long

(Paris) Today's House meeting was full, and the gallery was also crowded. Premier Daladier had only read his declaration of major policies for ten minutes when the meeting was very noisy, so that the Premier's words could not be heard, so he had to suspend the meeting temporarily. This scene is unique in the history of the French Parliament. The suspension of the meeting had the effect of restoring order. Daladier returned to the meeting and completed his declaration. The Premier then proposed a method: only four opposition parties would be allowed to speak and question today. Mr. Daladier decided to take this as a matter of confidence, so the members engaged in voting.

(Paris) It is expected that the Daladier government, relying on the support of the Socialist Party, can survive after a long and fierce debate in the House of Representatives. However, although Mr. Daladier used his wisdom and published an article urging the people of Paris to be calm, it is feared that even if he wins in the parliament, the life of his government will not last long. Currently, in addition to the danger of street riots, the government is also opposed by the stability side. This can be seen from the cancellation of the Thursday banquet by the Paris City Council. The banquet is an annual event, and the President and new cabinet members are invited. Now it has been suddenly cancelled. It is said that the city councillors refused to share a table with the new cabinet members. It is even rumored that the city council plans to refuse to pass the police budget to resist the newly appointed Police Commissioner Sipriot. Today, the authorities prohibited civilian aircraft from flying over the sky of Paris, except for commercial aircraft. (Reuters, 6th)

Cabinet's Major Policy Declaration Maintains the Free System

Sincere Unity Respects the Law

The Diplomatic Policy Remains Unchanged

Administrative Taxes are Thoroughly Reformed

(Paris) The cabinet held a State Council meeting at the Presidential Palace this morning, presided over by President Lebrun. The cabinet's major policy declaration was passed. The declaration will be read in the Senate and House of Representatives in the afternoon. In the House of Representatives, it will be read by Premier Daladier himself. The declaration briefly stated that the new government, which is now attending the parliament, should ask the parliament to judge it based on its actions. The government believes that some public agencies have neglected their duties and lack a sense of responsibility, so it will make changes to their personnel and office methods. As for this year's budget, it must be passed before March 31. After the budget is passed, we must find ways to reduce unemployment and rectify the national economy. Our country's tax system must be thoroughly reformed, abandoning the old, chaotic and complex system, and replacing it with a simple and modern institution, so that taxes can be put on the right track without causing excessive harm to the people. In terms of diplomacy, it is said that Europe is now fragmented and uneasy. Our law should reaffirm the aspiration of peace and security. All French policies can be included in two words: international cooperation and national defense. The ideal of peace cannot be realized only by advocating and promoting it. We must pursue it practically with all our strength, with sincerity, and avoid empty and arrogant actions. But to achieve this goal, the government must have the support of the majority and have strong authority. This is what we hope for from your trust. We must now protect the current system, so that the law and the parliament are respected. Our French ancestors fought bravely in times of crisis to maintain the order of democratic politics. All of us republicans must now unite sincerely and follow the example of our predecessors to maintain the only remaining free system in the world. The free system is the system of human progress. For the sake of national interests and people's welfare, what we want to call for now is the unity of republicans. (Havas, 6th)

Representatives Express Maintaining the Sanctity of the Constitution

Officials' Appointments and Removals Should Have Standards

(Paris) The House of Representatives members have organized groups to study the issues of administrative reform and the improvement of the working methods of the parliament. The group recently issued the following three hoped-for events: (1) The authority of the government must be maintained. The duties of the parliament are to pass laws and supervise the executive power within the scope of the constitution. The parliament should not exceed these duties. (2) It is right for members of parliament to intervene when they see actions that are unreasonable or beyond the law. However, it is harmful to disturb the principle of equality of all citizens under the law by relying on their power. Therefore, the group hopes that in the future, any intervention by members of parliament in the government and various administrative agencies that is sufficient to destroy the principles of equality and justice should be considered invalid. Equality and justice are the sacred basis of the constitution. (3) When the government selects personnel to appoint the heads of various agencies, it should be based purely on academic knowledge and experience. (Havas, 5th)

(Paris) The Rules Committee of the House of Representatives held a meeting this morning to discuss the organization of an investigation committee to thoroughly investigate the Stavisky case. This matter has been fully approved by the committee in principle. However, it has not yet been determined whether this investigation committee will enjoy judicial power, be able to conduct searches and arrests, according to the precedents of previous years. (Havas, 5th)

Right-wing Groups Demonstrate in Front of the Presidential Palace

Panic Arises in the Stock Exchange

(Paris) The right-wing "Fiery Cross" group held a demonstration near the Ministry of Interior and the Presidential Palace, and was dispersed by the police and the Republican Guard. In order to prevent disturbances from occurring tomorrow, the government has specially placed the Republican Guard and the guerrilla Guard under the command of the newly appointed Paris Police Commissioner Bonnet-Foy Chaupeau to maintain public order in the capital. The defenses around the Presidential Palace, the State Council, the Ministry of Interior, and the House of Representatives are particularly strict. (Havas, 5th)

(Paris) Before the political storm broke out, although there was temporary tranquility, the Paris Stock Exchange was in a state of panic today. The price of the pound and the US dollar rose, while the price of the franc fell. Everyone is scrambling to buy international first-class securities, and the prices of French first-class securities have all fallen. (Reuters, 5th)

Taxpayers' Declaration Demands the Dissolution of the House of Representatives

Dismissal of Officials Damages the Dignity of Paris

(Paris) The Seine Provincial Taxpayers' Federation issued a declaration, saying, "National interests are now seriously harmed." The Federation rejects all party prejudices and asks all members to participate in various demonstrations in Paris tomorrow. The National Taxpayers' Federation recently sent a letter to President Lebrun, asking me to dissolve the House of Representatives and form the Senate into a "Supreme Court" to uphold morality. (According to the French Constitution, presidents and cabinet members who commit serious political crimes, as well as others who commit crimes against the state, are tried by the Supreme Court composed of the Senate.) (Havas, 5th)

(Paris) Thirty of the fifty-eight members of the Seine Provincial House of Representatives recently sent a joint letter to the Minister of Interior Frot, protesting the replacement of Paris Police Commissioner Chiappe, saying that the government "sacrificed the responsible official in charge of maintaining public order to appease the troublemakers" for political motives. This kind of move is obviously unfair, and the residents of Paris are extremely dissatisfied. In addition, fifteen members of the Paris City Council issued a letter to the citizens, saying that as a result of the measures taken by the government, Police Commissioner Chiappe and Seine Provincial Governor Reynaud have resigned one after another. This matter is sufficient to damage the independence and dignity of the city of Paris, and a protest is raised. (Havas, 5th)

League of Nations Prepares

To Handle the German-Austrian Issue

A Special Meeting Can Be Convened on the 15th

A Disarmament Conference Will Be Convened on the 19th

(Geneva) According to important sources, after the League of Nations discusses the special meeting on the Austrian issue, the Disarmament Conference may be held in Geneva immediately. It is said that if Austrian Prime Minister Dollfuss submits a protest to the League of Nations this week regarding Germany's interference in Austria's internal affairs, the League of Nations can meet on February 15. At the same time, the Disarmament Preparatory Committee will prepare in London first, and the General Assembly will be formally convened in Geneva on the 19th. France is currently promoting to all parties, hoping to convene the meeting as soon as possible, but its attitude is still opposed to the proposals of Germany, Britain and Italy. According to the opinions of the French representatives, it is planned to still follow the previous resolutions, and countries are not allowed to increase armaments. (National Electricity, 5th)

(Geneva) It is believed here that the Austrian representative to the League of Nations, Pflügl, will ask the League of Nations to convene an extraordinary meeting of the Executive Yuan on Monday to discuss the German-Austrian issue. Unexpectedly, news was suddenly received this evening that although the Austrian government still insists on seeking justice from the League of Nations, it plans to submit the case to Geneva after Prime Minister Dollfuss goes to the Hungarian capital. The deadline should be after Friday. There are different explanations for the Austrian government's cautious self-control. Some say it is due to internal affairs changes, and some say it is due to the advice of the British. However, the State Council unanimously insists on seeking justice from the League of Nations, and a thick booklet of files on German-Austrian relations will soon be sent to the major powers to clarify the truth. (Havas, 5th)

Vienna Austria's petition to the League of Nations for protection against German interference in internal affairs was decided after a five-hour discussion at today's cabinet meeting. Prime Minister Dollfuss was authorized by the cabinet to prepare everything and submit the petition to Geneva. However, opinions on this matter in the cabinet are not consistent, because some people feel that this move is inappropriate, one is to increase domestic panic, and the other is to worsen the relationship between Germany and Austria. Moreover, the general public knows that this move is strongly disapproved by the British, while France is traditionally pleased. After Dollfuss was granted special privileges by the cabinet, he immediately sent a telegram to Austria's permanent representative to Geneva, Mr. Pflügl, instructing him to visit Secretary-General Avenol and request the Council to convene an extraordinary meeting to consider Austria's request. At the same time, he sent a telegram to Polish Foreign Minister Beck, making the same request, with Beck being the chairman of this year's Council. It is also heard that the Council may convene a meeting within this week. (National Electricity, 5th)
