Soviet Russia Promulgates New Orders

Important Steps for War Preparation

Increase the Salaries of the Red Army in the Far East

Benefit Farmers by Exempting Taxes for Six Years

(Moscow) According to the order announced today by the authorities and signed by Communist Party Secretary Stalin and People's Committee and Labor Defense Council Chairman Molotov, this is indeed one of the most important orders in recent years. The order stipulates that the monthly salaries of the Red Army in eastern Siberia and Outer Baikal will be increased, and the monthly salaries of office personnel will be increased by 10% to 30%. Collective farms and their farmers will be exempted from paying harvest to the state for the next six years, and individual farmers will be exempted for three years. According to the authorities, this plan aims to improve the situation of workers and improve the economic situation of residents in these areas and the Buriat-Mongol Autonomous Soviet Socialist Republic. However, some parties regard this as an important step for war preparation. Because the situation within the territory bordering Manchuria is good, people will be happy to live there. The more migrants there are, the more natural resources can be greatly developed and can greatly benefit the country. (Reuters, 6th)

(Moscow) The Soviet Union's People's Committee and the All-Union Communist Party Central Committee's order on special treatment for residents of eastern Siberia has been announced. The meeting was signed by Molotov and Stalin. The text says, in view of the increasing number of people moving to the Buryat-Mongol Autonomous Soviet Socialist Republic and the Outer Baikal and East Siberian regions, and in view of the fact that we must facilitate their economic settlement and improve the working conditions of manual workers and agency staff who are far from the Soviet Union's cultural center, Therefore, the Soviet Union's People's Committee and the All-Union Communist Party Central Committee ordered that collective farms and collective farmers in the area be exempted from paying grain to the state for six years, and private farmers be exempted for three years. At the same time, it stipulates that certain areas can be exempted from paying other agricultural products, while the remaining areas can reduce the amount of payment. This order also increases the wages of manual workers and agency staff in the area by 10% to 30%, and increases the supply of food to the troops in the Outer Berga region inside and outside the East Siberian region. (TASS, 6th)

Russian Border Military Preparations

Japan Feels Threatened

Hishikari Sends Private Individuals to Russia to Ease the Air

Speeches by Important People in Moscow

Tokyo Compares It to a Weak Dog Barking Easily

(Dalian) Hishikari claimed that Soviet Russia obviously cannot understand Japan. He hopes that Soviet Russia will not cause unexpected incidents by making military preparations in the border area of "Manchukuo". Now it is appropriate to send private individuals unofficially to Moscow to ease the tension between the two countries. Soviet Russia seems to have military installations in most of the border area of "Manchukuo". Vladivostok, Spasskaya, Hailanpao, Boli, and Dayouli all have military bases. Is the construction of this kind of military installation for self-defense or for offense? Is Soviet Russia really plotting something? There is no way to know. But we must be very careful at this time and not start a war lightly. Soviet Russia has many misunderstandings about Japan, which is very regrettable. The fact that Soviet Russia has great defense projects in the border area of Siberia is enough to prove that Soviet Russia cannot understand Japan's policy. (Reuters, 5th)

(Tokyo) Important figures such as Soviet dictator Stalin, Prime Minister Molotov, Foreign Minister Litvinov, and Land Minister Blokhilov have recently made frequent speeches attacking Japan. The comprehensive opinions of the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs and Army on this matter are as follows:

(1) Soviet Russia uses its tough foreign speeches to agitate the minds of ignorant nationals and vigorously publicizes the Communist government as a powerful government. (2) There are now more powerful factors of war in Europe than before the World War in 1913, and in a crisis that is on the verge of breaking out, they secretly hope that a war will break out in the Far East because of the lack of economic strength. Soviet Russia is instigated by European countries and makes tough remarks against Japan. (3) After the United States recognized Soviet Russia last year, Soviet Russia's attitude became even more blatant. (4) Weak dogs bark easily. Soviet Russia's second five-year plan has not achieved much. When they scold abroad, there must be unavoidable events in the country. This is their usual diplomatic tactic. (United Press, 6th)

Chinese Eastern Railway Issue

Tense Relations Between Japan and Russia

Russia Accuses Japanese Troops of Not Paying Debts

And Illegally Arresting Russian Workers

Pseudo Police in Heihe Open Fire and Injure People

Pseudo Apologizes to the Soviet Russian Consulate

(Moscow) The situation between Japan and Russia has been quite tense recently. Today, the Russian Foreign Ministry issued two reports, one accusing Japan of refusing to repay the 20 million rubles owed for the expenses of transporting troops in Manchuria by the former Chinese Eastern Railway, and the other accusing Japan of interfering with the Chinese Eastern Railway and imprisoning a large number of Russian workers, all of which are illegal. Last year, Japan paid Russia 435,000 rubles to repay international debts. Japan's management of the Chinese Eastern Railway is still smooth, but recently, goods transported by the Siberian Railway from Germany and other European countries have been delayed, the reason is that the number of freight cars is restricted by Japan. (National Electricity, 5th)

The Japanese and Manchukuo customs and police authorities at the Boli Suifenhe station are wantonly destroying the freight transport between the Chinese Eastern Railway and the Ussuri Railway. They have arbitrarily limited the daily export freight to 50 vehicles, with the aim of deliberately reducing transportation to this amount. At the same time, it is stipulated that each freight vehicle shall not exceed three vehicles. Their explanation for this method is all attributed to insufficient staff. Seeing that foreign exporters are constantly transporting goods to Vladivostok, the police have prohibited vehicles from connecting to the Ussuri Railway, arrested the staff on the vehicles, and taken other repressive measures. Recently, 24 railway workers came from the Ussuri Railway and were arrested. After being searched for three hours, they were released. These illegal steps by the Japanese and Manchukuo authorities are nothing more than openly destroying the export freight of the Chinese Eastern Railway. (TASS, 6th)

Boli According to news from Heihe, a Chinese city across the Heilongjiang River from Hailanpao, a police officer there suddenly fired his continuous-fire pistol and injured three other police officers. He was arrested and fled. Another team of police opened a volley of fire at him. A car from the Soviet Russian Consulate in Heihe happened to pass by at this time. Consulate staff member Usov was in the car and was injured in the shoulder. The local Manchurian authorities immediately expressed regret and apologized to the Soviet Russian Consulate. (TASS, 6th)

Upper House Questions on War

Concentrated on Sino-Russian Problems

Relaxing Relations Between the Two Countries

Hirota Holds It as a Diplomatic Creed

Akaike Publishes Absurd Arguments

Attempting to Interfere in Our Fujian Province's Internal Affairs

Sino-American Aviation and the Development of Soviet Areas

Believed to Violate the Non-Cession Treaty

(Tokyo) The focal point of today's parliament is concentrated in the Upper House. The plenary session of the House convened at 10:10 AM today. After Minister Nagai and Mr. Seki Naohiko conducted a question-and-answer session regarding the South Seas Development Company issue, Viscount Okouchi Teruhiko took the stage to question:

Regarding diplomatic issues, I would still like the Foreign Minister to provide an explanation. Currently, there are quite a few people discussing the impending occurrence of a world war. Furthermore, regarding issues such as Japanese-Soviet relations and Sino-Japanese relations, I would like a detailed explanation of the diplomatic policy.

Foreign Minister Hirota replied:

Judging from the current situation, it can be said that there is absolutely no danger of such a war. I am absolutely certain of this. As for Japanese-Soviet relations, I feel there is no cause for pessimism. I believe there will be appropriate policies to deal with it. As for Sino-Japanese relations, so-called anti-Japanese movements are merely temporary phenomena. Sino-Japanese relations must be amicable, no matter what. I am using

this creed to deal with the current situation.

Viscount Okouchi asked:

Although the Foreign Minister said that war will not occur, the Army and Navy authorities said that they can explain this in a way that the people can decide. What is the meaning of this?

Naval Minister Osumi and Army Minister Hayashi both made simple replies:

This matter should be carried out in conjunction with diplomatic work, and it is also necessary to strengthen national defense.

Next, Mr. Akaike Nou rose to ask:

Regarding the current situation of the three major countries surrounding Japan, we must consider it carefully. A gloomy atmosphere pervades, and people feel the same way. We must not blindly deal with this kind of international situation. First of all, we should carefully observe the actions of Soviet Russia. Recent reports from Manchuria say that Koreans working in Manchuria have recently been returning to Korea in batches. The reason given is that war between Japan and the Soviet Union is imminent. The reason is that Soviet Russia has 150,000 to 190,000 troops stationed on the border of Manchuria and has built permanent fortresses. In addition, based on Stalin's remarks and combining the above-mentioned situations, it can be seen that the people of Manchuria can hardly live and work in peace. Therefore, it is felt that "Manchukuo" must now seek security outside the country. What kind of diplomatic work should the Foreign Minister implement for the sake of "Manchukuo's security"? I would like Foreign Minister Hirota to answer in detail.

At noon, the parliament announced a recess.

(Tokyo) The plenary session of the House of Peers continued in the afternoon. Regarding Mr. Akaike's question, Foreign Minister Hirota replied:

I feel that the points Mr. Akaike mentioned deserve great attention. I feel that my relationship with Soviet Russia is extremely important, so I continue to negotiate with various people related to Soviet Russia, working day and night to avoid any mistakes. Regarding the positions of "Manchukuo" and Japan, we should seek understanding from the world. I will continue to work hard in the future.

Mr. Akaike asked again:

Fujian must not be ceded to any country. This is clearly stated in the treaty and has now been violated. These items are stated below. First, the China National Aviation Corporation, most of whose capital is provided by the United States, is nominally a commercial flight, but in essence, it is used for military purposes. This clearly violates the said treaty. If Xiamen is used as a base for flights, Taiwan can be reached in the shortest time. This is a fact that is extremely worrying for Japan's national defense.

Second, the Soviet area in China is expanding greatly, and therefore it has been violated. The development of the Soviet area, in other words, is a secession. Areas within China under the guidance of the Third International may create a new republic. Even if there is no major problem now, there will inevitably be a problem in the future, so it is inconvenient to treat it as if we are watching a fire from across the river.

Foreign Minister Hirota replied:

Regarding the Sino-Japanese relationship in the Fujian treaty, it can be divided into two items: one is the non-cession of land, and the other is matters related to military affairs. If the China National Aviation Corporation is indeed of a military nature, as Mr. Akaike said, it violates the second item of the treaty. However, it is necessary to investigate in detail whether the aviation company is of a military nature. As for the claim that the United States and China have a secret agreement, we will cooperate with the military authorities to pay as much attention as possible to this point. Regarding the communist bandits in China, if we talk about the theories and claims of the Communist Party, they have a consistent point of view, but the current Chinese

communist bandits are not in the situation that Mr. Akaike said, because their organization is also very weak. (Nippon Rengo Electric, 6th)

British Newspapers Reveal

Secrets of the Naval Conference

Rumor That the United States Purchased British and French Islands in the South Pacific

Intended to Encircle Japanese Mandated Islands

To Connect With the Philippines

Purchase Cost to Be Paid With a Portion of War Debts

London Dispatch: The Daily Express published a headline in large letters on the 28th of last month, "Secrets of the Pacific: The United States is Discussing Methods of Outflanking Islands Under Japanese Rule." The content stated that the British Far East Naval Conference convened in Singapore this time discussed the issue of Britain and France selling islands in the South Pacific to the United States, such as the United States buying the Marquesas Islands from France, and buying Nauru, the Bismarck Archipelago, and other islands from Britain, in order to outflank the southern part of the Japanese mandated islands and connect with the Philippines. As for the purchase cost, it will be roughly offset by a portion of the war debt. The United States plans to build ports and airfields on these islands after purchasing them, using them as commercial bases in peacetime and as bases for warships and aircraft in wartime, etc. Although this news is not entirely credible, at a time when the Singapore Conference is giving people an impression of extreme secrecy, this unexpected article has caused great shock in all quarters. (World News Agency)

The British Government

Attention to Far East Trade

Some People Advocate Forming a Manchuria Commercial Investigation Team

Australian Dignitaries Plan to Seek a Compromise on Trade With Japan

(London) In the House of Commons today, there were suggestions to organize a British Chamber of Commerce delegation to "Manchukuo" and to investigate the dumping of Japanese cement in Hong Kong. The person who raised the issue of the commercial delegation to Manchuria was Captain Dowell of the Conservative Party. Mr. Colville, Minister of Overseas Trade, replied that a trade official was stationed in Harbin in 1930, but was soon transferred to Peiping because the position in Peiping was more urgently needed than in Harbin. The British commercial interests in Manchuria are adequately represented by the British Consulate. However, he is well aware of the importance of Mr. Dowell's proposal, and the government will pay close attention to this situation. Conservative Mr. Hamsley raised the issue of Japanese cement dumping in Hong Kong. Malcolm MacDonald (son of the British Prime Minister) replied on behalf of the government that the Colonial Secretary had contacted the Governor of Hong Kong about this matter. After considering various circumstances and Hong Kong's trade preferences, the Governor felt that it was not appropriate to interfere with such imported goods. The Governor is now doing his best to promote the use of British cement as much as possible within the colony. A Reuters dispatch from Melbourne stated that Mr. Latham, who holds the three important positions of justice, diplomacy, and industry in the Australian government, will go to the Far East on March 7 for a three-month tour. Mr. Latham will visit China, Japan, Hong Kong, the Dutch East Indies, and Malaysia, and plans to go to Vietnam and the

Philippines. According to Melbourne official sources, the purpose of Mr. Latham's trip is to enhance friendship between Australia and its northern neighbors, and his mission is not limited to trade. Although the official arena released this news, according to general speculation, one of the main purposes of Mr. Latham's trip is to negotiate a compromise in order to eliminate the possibility of a commercial war between Australia and Japan. Recently, with the low value of the Japanese currency, Australia has proposed increasing taxes to restrict the entry of Japanese goods. Japan replied that Japan purchases more from Australia than it sells to Australia. If Australia raises tariffs on Japanese goods, Japan will abandon Australia and turn to other places to purchase the wool it needs. (Reuters Dispatch, 5th)

Molotov's Report

The Second Five-Year Plan of Soviet Russia

(Moscow) Mr. Molotov, Chairman of the Soviet Union's Council of People's Commissars, made a lengthy report to the Communist Party Congress on the Second Five-Year Plan, stating that

the first basic political task of the First Five-Year Plan was to completely eliminate capitalist components and (generally speaking) classes, completely eliminate class divisions and exploitation, overcome the remnants of capitalism in the economy and people's minds, and transform all the working people of the Soviet Union into active creators of a classless socialist society. The second task was to improve the well-being of workers and collective farmers. The consumption standards of the working masses will increase five to three times. The third issue was to complete the technical transformation of the entire national economy, such as industry, transportation, agriculture, etc.

These three are united and indivisible, and at the same time, they determine the essence of socialist construction in the Second Five-Year Plan. They can be proposed today on the basis of the successful and victorious completion of the First Five-Year Plan. At the beginning of the implementation of the First Five-Year Plan, capitalist components in the Soviet Union still occupied an important position. By the end of the First Five-Year Plan, the capitalist components in the industrial sector were no longer significant. Cooperative and state trade have taken a dominant position. Therefore, during the implementation period, private business was almost completely excluded from trade. The struggle to eliminate capitalist components in rural areas was far more difficult. However, at the beginning of the implementation of the Second Five-Year Plan, the adoption of the collective farming system has been effective in the most important agricultural areas. At the same time, the rich peasant class has been destroyed. "To this day, collective and state farms have occupied 84.7% of the area under grain cultivation. Therefore, we can say that the collective farming system has achieved complete victory. The remnants of the rich peasant class will inevitably be eliminated rapidly and finally. At the same time, the only way for private farms to gradually transform into collective farming."

Mr. Molotov then stated that when the Second Five-Year Plan is completed, socialist forms will occupy a monopoly position in all sectors of the economy. After the completion of the tasks of the Second Five-Year Plan, the Soviet Union will become a solid socialist republic.

Mr. Molotov further elaborated on the various issues of the Second Five-Year Plan, such as eliminating the factors that generate class differences and the relationship of exploitation between people, and overcoming the remnants of capitalism in the economy and people's minds. He said that if we want to complete these tasks, we must strengthen the dictatorship of the proletariat with all our strength, strengthen its power and combat effectiveness, and consolidate the alliance between the working class and the working peasants. When Mr. Molotov mentioned the improvement of the material and cultural level of the workers, he said, "The phenomenon of unemployment in the Soviet Union has disappeared. Workers have full confidence in the future. At the same time, with the elimination of poverty in the countryside, the phenomenon of farmers being divided into rich and poor peasants has also disappeared. The constant improvement of the material level of the working masses and the rapid increase in the welfare of the peasant masses are proved by their increased demand for culture and other needs. "Therefore, the Party and the government have shouldered this task, that is, to expand the food industry and the general light industry to improve the consumption standards of the working masses."

The main economic task of the Second Five-Year Plan is to completely complete the technical transformation of the national economy and, on this basis, greatly expand our country's productive forces. This task requires its complete completion in all sectors of industry, agriculture, and transportation. Although the Soviet Union is lagging behind the United States in some economic sectors, it will surpass all European countries in terms of technical level and total industrial products. All this will fundamentally change the Soviet Union and the capitalist world, and at the same time, make the conflict between the two systems of socialism and capitalism enter a newer and higher level. The industrialization policy expressed in the Second Five-Year Plan further increases the proportion of industrial production in the total national production, that is, almost to 80%. In this way, the Soviet Union will be on par with the countries with the highest degree of industrialization in the world, such as Germany and the United States.

Industrial production must increase by 2.4 times compared with the First Five-Year Plan, and will increase by 9 times compared with the pre-war level. During the First Five-Year Plan, the industry that manufactured production tools developed relatively rapidly, and during the Second Five-Year Plan, we have been able to accelerate the development of both heavy industry and light industry at the same time, and we have been able to make it develop particularly rapidly in the production of general consumer goods. Mr. Molotov also pointed out the necessity of developing local and handicraft industries, and listed the tasks of the most important industrial sectors. He said, "By the end of the Second Five-Year Plan, 80% of the total industrial production must be manufactured by factories newly built or completely rebuilt during the First and Second Five-Year Plans. At the same time, 50% to 60% of the production tools used in the national economy at that time will be manufactured during the Second Five-Year Plan. We have shouldered this task, that is, to complete the technical transformation with tools made in our country." Mr. Molotov detailed the achievements of the machine industry. This industry has manufactured various machines for various sectors of industry, and its production quantity in the world's machine production has increased from 4% in 1928 to 21.4% in 1933. When Mr. Molotov mentioned electrification, he said that the Soviet Union will rank second in the world in terms of the amount of electricity produced. He also listed the expected development status of petroleum, coal, peat and chemical industries, as well as steel and other metallurgical industries in the Second Five-Year Plan. When Mr. Molotov mentioned light industry, he said that the Second Five-Year Plan will increase the production of general consumer goods by three times. At the same time, when the Second Five-Year Plan ends, the Soviet Union will rank first in the world in terms of the level of technical equipment. In terms of food industry production, it will rank first in Europe. He particularly emphasized that various industries must focus on improving the quality of production.

Mr. Molotov discussed agricultural production, saying that there were indeed huge difficulties during the organization period, and now the process of changing private management to collective farming has been largely completed, so agriculture has incomparably superior conditions for rising. The total agricultural production in the Second Five-Year Plan will increase greatly. In 1937, it will reach 110,560,000 tons, while in 1932, it was 69,870,000 tons. The Second Five-Year Plan does not stipulate a sharp increase in the sown area. The main issue is to increase crop yields. Animal husbandry also has very important issues. The Second Five-Year Plan stipulates that the number of livestock must increase greatly. "In order to make agriculture rise rapidly, we must consolidate the economic foundation of collective and state farms."

Molotov then described the most important tasks of the transportation industry. Compared with 1932, the freight volume in 1937 increased as follows: railways by 178%, river transport by 245%, and sea transport by 280%. In order to complete this extreme increase, the technical transformation of the transportation industry, especially the railway, must be regarded as the central issue. He also mentioned the work stipulated in the plan in the transportation industry, such as the double-tracking of the Ural-Kuznetzk-Donets coal area, Outer Baikal and Ussuri railways, the adoption of automatic block signal methods, the increase of vehicles and the increase of railways, etc. (The trunk line project from Baikal to Amur is extremely huge and important). All this is intended to eliminate the phenomenon that today's transportation industry is lagging behind the general development of the national economy. Mr. Molotov then mentioned the work of developing waterways. He said that the canal from the Volga River to Moscow (127 kilometers long) is being dredged, and the canal from the Volga River to the Don River (100 kilometers long) will also be built during the Second Five-Year Plan. By then, the European part of the Soviet Union will have a great waterway system. Mr. Molotov also listed the plans for overhauling and rebuilding river and sea transport,

developing automobile and air transportation, building new highways, and developing radio communications. Mr. Molotov emphasized that the implementation of technical transformation must have a struggle to win production technology. Mr. Molotov mentioned labor issues, saying that by the end of the Second Five-Year Plan, the efficiency of industrial labor will increase by 63%, the production cost will decrease by 26%, and the factory-affiliated schools will graduate 2.7 million skilled workers. Agricultural vocational schools will train 1.5 million agricultural workers. Within five years, 5 million new workers participating in industry will be trained. The number of experts graduating from universities will also increase, and scientific and technical work will continue to develop. Mr. Molotov said, "We have learned a lot from foreign technology and foreign experts. We have not forgotten these lessons. Therefore, we have a large number of new talents in science and technology. During the Second Five-Year Plan, we will rely more on the achievements of Soviet technology in the technical transformation of our national economy. All this will be able to make the Soviet Union's productive forces develop rapidly. This kind of development has never been seen in any capitalist country. When the Second Five-Year Plan ends, the Soviet Union's position among the world's powers in terms of production will change greatly. Before the First Five-Year Plan, the Soviet Union's production accounted for the fifth place in the world. Before the Second Five-Year Plan, it has accounted for the third place in the world, and the second place in Europe. When the Second Five-Year Plan ends, the Soviet Union will jump to the second place in the world in terms of production, and will rank first in Europe. The task of catching up with and surpassing capitalist countries in economics and technology will be realized in practice."

When Mr. Molotov mentioned construction work and the redistribution of productive forces, he pointed out that a more accurate distribution of the Soviet Union's productive forces, a more even distribution of factories throughout the country, and making industry close to raw material supply areas and electricity sources, etc., are the characteristics of the investment plan in the Second Five-Year Plan. The total investment in various sectors of the national economy will reach 133,000,000,000 rubles, while it was only 50,000,000,000 rubles in the First Five-Year Plan. The investment in the industrial sector will reach 69,000,000,000 rubles, and the investment in the agricultural sector will increase from 900 million rubles in the First Five-Year Plan to 1.5 trillion rubles. Within these five years, 94 newly established machine manufacturing plants will start construction.

Mr. Molotov mentioned the improvement of the material and cultural living standards of the working masses. He said that the status of workers has improved dramatically during the First Five-Year Plan. The elimination of unemployment and the fact that our country's workers do not have to worry about tomorrow are of the greatest value. At the same time, the status of farmers has also changed significantly. In the past, the poverty level of rural areas deepened like a river going downhill, but today its status is increasing day by day. We no longer have the danger of unemployment. On the contrary, the number of employees has increased by 29% within five years, and workers are not threatened by excessively long working hours every day. On the contrary, the daily working hours have been reduced to seven hours, and under more difficult working conditions, they have been reduced to less than six hours." When Mr. Molotov discussed the income of workers and employees, he paid special attention to the increase in real wages. In the plan, this kind of wage will increase by one. The total wage fund will increase from 320 billion rubles to 510 billion rubles within five years. The average wage of workers and employees will increase by 22%.

The Second Five-Year Plan stipulates that illiteracy must be completely eliminated, and the implementation of compulsory vocational education will be universally adopted. The total number of teachers and students will increase greatly. All young children will be able to enter kindergartens. Other facilities such as clubs, libraries, radio stations, scientific research institutes, and scientific workers will also increase sharply. Mr. Molotov also detailed the improvement of health services, the expansion of living areas, and the increase in the supply of urban and rural workers. The average per capita consumption of major items will increase by 2.5 to 3 times within five years, and the average consumption of industrial goods will also increase.

Mr. Molotov then compared the position of the Soviet Union with that of capitalist countries, saying, "From 1928 to 1932, the national income of the United Kingdom decreased by 16.9%, but the national income of the Soviet Union increased by 32% during the same period. Capitalist countries have no five-year plan and no clear goals. Their leaders can never try to restore the level of 1928 even after five years. The position of the Soviet Union is different. We have a clear vision, just as the Second Five-Year Plan has stipulated. We will constantly and sharply increase our total national income, that is, we must carry out this task, so that this income will increase by 138% compared with 1932, and by 332% compared with 1923." (TASS Dispatch, 6th)

Britain Builds

New Military Aircraft

(London) According to the "Daily Mail", the Ministry of Aviation has just ordered the construction of a twin-propeller aircraft with two rudders. Its style is larger than that of the Lacierva (the Spanish inventor, the inventor of the twin-propeller aircraft). According to the newspaper, this aircraft is considered by the army and navy to have important strategic value, because on the one hand, this aircraft can stay in the air, almost motionless, which is very useful when conducting reconnaissance, and on the other hand, its flight speed is almost equal to that of ordinary aircraft. (Havas Dispatch, 6th)

International Train Robbery Suspects

Two Leaders Arrested

(Changchun) Two leaders of the bandits who robbed the Siberian train near Angangxi on December 15 last year have been arrested near Qiqihar. In addition, four other bandits have been captured and may be sentenced to death. This time, it was jointly cracked by the local police and the Heilongjiang army. According to reports, when the bandits robbed the train on that day, they kidnapped many Chinese people and waited for ransom, and killed several passengers. (Reuters Dispatch, 5th)

Balkan Pact

Nature Belongs to Defense

Athens newspapers enthusiastically approve the initial signing of the Balkan Peninsula Consultation Pact, saying that according to the pact, the signatory countries only mutually guarantee their common borders in the Balkan Peninsula, and its defensive nature is very obvious. The pact will be formally signed at the Athens Academy of Sciences on Thursday afternoon. (Havas News Agency, 5th)

(Geneva) After the initial signing of the Balkan Consultation Pact, the Turkish government immediately conducted negotiations with the Greek government, intending to establish a customs union between the two countries to supplement it. It is reported that the Turkish Minister of Economy will go to Athens soon to organize the draft customs union treaty, and it is hoped that other signatory countries of the Balkan Consultation Pact will also follow suit. (Havas News Agency, 5th)

Sofia, this semi-official source has announced Bulgaria's attitude towards the Balkan Pact concluded by Greece, Turkey, Romania, and Yugoslavia. It is said that Bulgaria is willing to join non-aggression treaties within the League of Nations framework and in accordance with the Kellogg-Briand Pact, as this is the best way to consolidate Balkan peace. Informed sources now say that the reason why Bulgaria did not join the Balkan Pact is because it could not obtain certain concessions, such as a corridor to the Aegean Sea, which caused dissatisfaction. However, the hope that Bulgaria can be persuaded to sign to consolidate the effectiveness of the pact has not yet been abandoned. Informal talks are now underway to achieve this goal. It is reported that the new pact stipulates economic and political cooperation among the countries, and opposes the revision of the Treaty of Versailles, so it is no less than a Locarno Pact for the Balkans. (Reuters, 6th)

(Paris) The news of the initial signing of the Balkan Consultation Pact has been warmly welcomed here. Responsible parties said that the pact is in line with France's consistent policy. Before now, the Balkans were the most chaotic area in Europe. With the completion of the pact, the situation in the peninsula can be considered stable. It is also said that the reconciliation of the Balkan Peninsula countries is out of their own free will, so the signing of the pact is out of the countries' own initiative, which is in line with France's consistent principle of respecting the sovereignty of all countries. (Havas News Agency, 5th)

Although people in London are pleased about the imminent signing of the Balkan Consultation Pact, they remain silent about Bulgaria's non-participation in the so-called "Eastern Locarno Treaty." At the House of Commons meeting this afternoon, someone asked the government how to instruct representatives stationed in foreign countries to express their attitude towards this pact. Foreign Secretary Simon said, "The government has ordered representatives stationed in the relevant countries to notify the governments of the respective countries that the British government supports the pact concluded by the countries of the Balkan Peninsula for the sake of general peace, but only on the condition that this pact does not oppose any country or any group of countries. Therefore, it is hoped that the articles of the Balkan Consultation Pact will be carefully considered so that Bulgaria can also join." (Havas News Agency, 5th)

Executive Yuan Passes

Regulations for the Organization of Administrative Inspectorate Offices in Jiangsu Province

Appointment of Xie Zhongfu as a Member of the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission

Appointment of Yan Wei as Director of the Education Department of Suiyuan Province

(Nanjing) The Executive Yuan held its 146th meeting at 9:00 AM on the 6th. Attendees included Wang Zhaoming, Kong Xiangxi, Chen Shuren, Wang Shijie, Zhu Jiahua, Chen Shaokuan, Chen Gongbo, Liu Ruiheng. Attendees by special invitation included Cao Haosen, Gan Naiguang, Xu Mo, Zou Lin, Zhao Pilian, Zheng Tianxi, Guo Chuntao, Zeng Zhongming, Duan Xipeng, Tang Youren, Chu Minyi, Peng Xuepei. Wang Zhaoming chaired the meeting.

(A) Review of Reports

(1) Minister of Interior Huang, Minister of Finance Kong, and Minister of Education Wang reported on the case of educational subsidies for Beiping City. As a result, it is proposed to restore the original annual amount of 600,000 yuan starting from the 23rd year. The resolution was to pass.

(B) Appointments and Removals

(1) Resolved to appoint Xie Zhongfu as a member of the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission. (2) Resolved that Pan Xiuren, a member of the Suiyuan Provincial Government and concurrently Director of the Education Department, has been absent from his post for a long time. He should be relieved of both positions. Yan Wei is appointed as a member of the Suiyuan Provincial Government and concurrently Director of the Education Department.

(3) Minister of Justice Luo submitted a request to appoint Liu Yun as the President of the Jiangsu Rehabilitation Institute. The resolution was to pass.

(4) Minister of Navy Chen submitted a request that due to the death of Du Xigui, the principal of the Naval Academy, Zhu Tiansen be appointed to succeed him with simplified appointment procedures. The resolution was to pass.

(5) Minister of Navy Chen reported that the Naval Torpedo Guerrilla Command has been ordered to be abolished, and Commander Wu Shouting has been appointed to another position. Please approve the dismissal. The resolution was to pass.

(6) Minister of Navy Chen reported that Yuan Jin, the Director of the Naval Mawei Shipyard, had left his post without authorization, and Han Yuheng, the Director of the Naval Xiamen Shipyard, had been appointed to another position. Please approve the dismissal. The resolution was to pass.

(7) Minister of Military Affairs He requested the appointment of Han Xihou as the Major General Chief of Staff of the 97th Division. The resolution was to pass.

(8) Minister of Military Affairs He requested that Chen Jinglie, Secretary of the Ministry, Jiang Shouqian, Fan Xinzhi, Lu Linchang, and Cai Yuan, Chief of the Document Section of the General Affairs Department, be relieved of their posts as they have been appointed to other positions. The resolution was to pass.

(C) Matters for Discussion

(1) Minister of Interior Huang reported that the Jiangsu Provincial Government had submitted revised regulations for the organization of the Administrative Inspectorate Offices in Jiangsu Province, general rules of procedure, and a zoning table. It is proposed to approve the record for future compliance. The resolution was to approve the record.

(2) Minister of Finance Kong submitted a draft of the rules for the custody of the Xiang Province Construction Public Bond Fund for the 23rd year of the Republic of China. The resolution was to pass and order the Hunan Provincial Government to quickly establish the fund custody committee and submit the charter for review.

(3) Minister of Foreign Affairs Wang requested that the term of office of the ministry's inspection commissioner be extended for another six months. The resolution was to pass.

(4) Minister of Finance Kong submitted the list of members of the Committee for the Custody of the North China Relief War Zone Short-Term Public Debt Fund for the 22nd year of the Republic of China, and signed and noted the revised detailed rules for the fund custody regulations. The resolution was to approve the record in accordance with the ministry's endorsement and revision. (Central News Agency, 6th)

Ministry of Finance Sends Telegram to Provincial Governments

To Assist in the Implementation of the New System of Weights and Measures

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance has issued a general order to all salt districts that, in order to unify the system of weights and measures, starting from January of this year, the new market scale must be used uniformly to weigh and sell salt, and taxes will still be collected at the old rate. However, merchants and the people in various places are clinging to old habits and are mostly hesitant to adopt the market scale. The ministry sent a special telegram to the provincial governments, stating that the implementation of the new system of weights and measures is a key policy of the central government. The hesitation of merchants and the people will affect salt tax revenue. Therefore, it is requested that they instruct the county governments under their jurisdiction to vigorously assist in persuading merchants and the people to enthusiastically comply with the new system without delay, so as to benefit the salt administration. (Special Dispatch, 6th)

Tangshan

Qixin Factory Strike Wave

(Tianjin) Zhao Xun, the newly appointed Director of the Special Public Security Bureau of Tangshan, took office on the 6th. On the 6th, workers at the Qixin Cement Factory in Tangshan demanded a share of the bonus. The factory stated that its business was poor and it lost tens of thousands of yuan last year, so it could not pay the bonus. The workers believed that their interests were being exploited and went on a general strike. The Public Security Bureau is currently mediating. (Special Dispatch, 6th)

(Tianjin) A labor dispute occurred at the Qixin Porcelain Factory in Tangshan. The reason is that the factory intends to reduce wages by 12 yuan per hundred yuan for all employees this year in order to maintain operations due to business losses. The workers were dissatisfied and gathered more than 400 people on the afternoon of the 5th to surround the office and announced a strike at the same time. The situation is serious, and all parties are now mediating. (Central Telegram, 6th)

Two Huai Salt District Revitalization Plan

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance learned that the Two Huai Salt District, from Tongzhou in the south to Ganyu in the north, covers more than 800 li. Due to the deterioration of waterways in recent years, the salt industry has been declining. In addition, waterlogging, drought, and the proliferation of smuggled goods have caused more than 30 companies to close down. The salt administration authorities have formulated a reorganization and revitalization plan: (1) building salt ponds, (2) dredging rivers, (3) facilitating transportation, (4) eliminating malpractices, and (5) abolishing bad rules. These will be implemented step by step. The Yushi Office and the business group will first build two salt ponds in Xiba Town, which are nearing completion. It is estimated that the salt production this year can increase by about 200,000 dan. (Special Dispatch, 6th)

Xiao Ke

Two bandit lairs have been destroyed.

The remnants of the two bandits are fleeing in disarray.

The First and Second Columns are still pursuing and suppressing them.

Changsha Dispatch: He Jian, the Commander-in-Chief of the Western Route Bandit Suppression Army, considered Xiao Ke and Kong Hechong's bandit gangs in the western region to be the largest. Recently, he specially dispatched Liu Jianxu, the commander of the First Column, to station in Lianhua, Jiangxi, to command the 15th Division (Wang Dongyuan), the 16th Division (Peng Weiren), and the 63rd Division (Chen Guangzhong), among others, to suppress Xiao's bandits. He also sent Liu Yinggu, the commander of the Second Column, to station in Wanzai, Jiangxi, to command the 18th Division (Zhu Yaohua), the 50th Division (Yue Sen), and the 62nd Division (Tao Guang), as well as the Tao-Liu Brigade of the 19th Division (Li Jue), to suppress Kong's bandits. On the First Column's side, after two or three months of using the "blockhouse advancement method," building blockhouses step by step towards Xiao's old lair, Yongxin, scores of battles, large and small, occurred. In the middle of last month, Peng Weiren's division braved the snow and occupied the natural stronghold of the Meihua Mountains. Xiao's bandits, knowing that Yongxin could not be defended, abandoned their lair and fled, crossing the Rui River through Anfu and heading towards Gao'an and Shanggao, attempting to join up with Kong's bandits. Liu Jianxu, in addition to ordering Wang Dongyuan and Chen Guangzhong's divisions to handle the post-banditry affairs in the bandit areas and clear out the remnants of bandits in the Yongxin Meihua Mountains area, also sent Peng Weiren's division to track and pursue them. On the evening of the 31st of last month, they had already pursued them to Shangfen, and it is expected that they will catch up in two or three days this month, as the 18th Division (Zhu Yaohua) is blocking their path ahead. At that time, they will be attacked from both sides, inflicting a major blow on Xiao's bandits. On the Second Column's side, the various units only completed their deployment on the 27th of last month. At dawn on the 28th, they launched a four-pronged attack on Kong's bandits' old lair, Xiaoyuan. It is found that Xiaoyuan was the place where the pseudo-Soviet government of the Hunan-Hubei-Jiangxi border area issued orders, called Little Moscow by the bandits. Located northwest of Wanzai, surrounded by towering mountains and ridges, it has always been a bandit den. In the Ming Dynasty, there was the bandit Li Daluan, and in the Qing Dynasty, there were the "shed bandits" Zhu Yiwu, who used it as their nest.

Page 10

They caused trouble for decades before they were finally suppressed. Kong's bandits had also occupied it for six or seven years. The National Army restrained by them numbered as many as five or six divisions. This time, Liu Yinggu personally stationed in Wanzai to launch a major suppression. The original plan was to prepare for at least a week of major battles. Unexpectedly, because the important points near Xiaoyuan were lost early, and the nest had been blockaded for too long, lacking both rice and salt, Kong's bandits did not resist once the Western Route Army launched its suppression, and immediately abandoned their nest and fled. At 5 PM on the 28th, the Tao-Liu Brigade of the 19th Division was the first to occupy Xiaoyuan. It was heard that Kong's bandits led their troops around the mountain roads from Zaoqiao and Ganfang, rushing towards Fengxin and Gao'an, attempting to join up with Xiao's bandits. Liu Yinggu, in addition to leaving the Tao Brigade stationed in Xiaoyuan to clear out the remnant bandits and handle the aftermath, also sent Zhu Yaohua and Yue Sen's divisions to track and pursue them. Therefore, both Xiao and Kong's bandits have lost their lairs and are fleeing everywhere. This is the biggest victory since the bandit suppression. The two columns are now preparing for a major encirclement, hoping to wipe them out in one fell swoop. Appended below is the news of victory:

Telegram from Liu Jianxu, Commander of the First Column: "According to telegrams from Division Commander Peng Weiren on the 30th, based on reports from various sources, Xiao's bandits have passed through the Jiebu border (located between Shanggao and Gao'an) and crossed the Rui River. The entire group crossed the river after dusk and arrived near Tongan in the forenoon of the 31st. The 18th Division is blocking their path there. Also, the bandit Gao Yongsheng (a division commander in Kong's force) secretly fled to Ganfang (southwest of Fengxin). It appears that Xiao and Kong's bandits are planning to join up. My division arrived in Shangfen on the 30th evening and will continue to advance tomorrow. We have been traveling at least 70 to 80 li per day, and morale is very high. We are determined to disregard everything and pursue bravely to annihilate these bandits. I have ordered a fierce advance to detect and suppress the bandits, aiming to achieve merit and annihilation. Respectfully reported, your subordinate Liu Jianxu, Eastern Seal."

Telegram from Liu Yinggu, Commander of the Second Column: "Kong and Xiao's bandits are hoping to join up. At this moment, Kong's bandits are fleeing from Zaoqiao and Ganfang, harassing the Fengxin area, while Xiao's bandits are heading towards Jiebu and Huayang, attempting to cross the river northwards between Gao'an and Shanggao. However, it is not easy for the bandits to move in safe areas, and the Xiaoyuan bandit lair has been destroyed. I have no worries about the rear. I have already ordered the various units to relentlessly pursue and suppress the two bandits, Kong and Xiao. The deployment is in place. I expect to be able to annihilate these bandits and eliminate the major problem in the near future. Respectfully presented, your subordinate Liu Yinggu, kowtowing, world seal." (February 3rd)

Large-Scale Rural Pacification in Southern Hubei

More than 20 bandit lairs destroyed, dozens of bandit leaders captured and killed.

More than a thousand remnant bandits fled from Yangxin into Tongshan territory.

Hankou Dispatch: The remnant bandits in southern Hubei, including the pseudo-3rd Red Division, the Northern Jiangxi Division, and the Guard Division, led by bandit leaders Ye Jinbo, Zhang Shou, etc., previously besieged Tongshan and Chongyang counties one after another, attempting to occupy the Hunan-Hubei road and disrupt transportation. After being jointly defeated by the National Army units led by Feng Xingxian, they fled south to the Mushigang and Dawushan areas in Yangxin territory, remotely contacting the Jiangxi bandits in Xiaoyuan and seeking opportunities to disturb the Yangtze River. Upon receiving the report, Chen Jicheng ordered Guo Rudong, Liu Peixu, and Li Zongjian's units to jointly suppress them, repeatedly defeating the remnant bandits. The lairs in Mushigang and Dawushan were all recaptured. Initially, when the bandits invaded Chongtong, their strength was no less than four or five thousand men, and their momentum was huge. Pu and Xian counties were all threatened. After fleeing south, their momentum declined daily. Guo, Li, and Liu's three units engaged in battle for weeks with fresh troops, and the main force of the bandits completely collapsed. Three pseudo-division commanders were killed in battle, and the bandits also suffered losses. Afterwards, the National Army was victorious everywhere it went. Only a little over a thousand remnant bandits remained, unable to resist. Recently, they fled north again to Tongshan, hoping to prolong their lives. Chen Jicheng, believing that the main force of the bandits had been eliminated, decided to launch a large-scale rural pacification to eliminate the remnants. He had already organized a rural pacification corps, divided into districts to search. In a few days, he would separately destroy and recover the total sub-offices of the remnant bandits and their bases, totaling 21 places, including Tiantai Mountain, Baishuitai, Chengmi Gong, Jiangtang Fort, Shitoutan, Zhu Jia Shan, Longjiao Shan, Xiang Jia Shan, Liu Zhong Shan, Dong Qing You Mountain Village, Guo Jia Shan, Song Jia Zhai, Hua Jia Shan, Nanchang Fort, Dong Jia Houshan, Beishantou, Jinpen Shi, Daqin Yan, Wu Ba Chong, Yu Jia Gang, and Chuan Jia Shan. Among them, Tiantai Mountain was the main base, and the general office was located in Chengmi Gong. Xiang Jia Shan and Liu Zhong Shan were the general offices of the bandits' eight agencies, including (1) the pseudo-rising district Soviet government, (2) the pseudo-Communist Party district committee, (3) the pseudo-Young Communist district association, (4) the pseudo-district labor union, (5) the pseudo-mutual aid society, (6) the pseudo-pro-Soviet grand alliance, (7) the pseudo-district work group, and (8) the pseudo-district team headquarters. The remaining places, such as Guo Jia Shan, were all important bandit dens. The bandit leaders who were beheaded or captured, in addition to the pseudo-Jiangxi Northern Division Commander Yang Xicheng, the pseudo-Deputy 3rd Division Commander Liu Yonghong, the pseudo-Hebei Independent 2nd Division Commander Liu Jihui, and the pseudo-Regimental Commander Wu Yingrui, who were killed in battle during the suppression by Guo's division, the remaining bandit leaders who were captured and beheaded by the rural pacification corps included the pseudo-Young Pioneer general commander and county committee member Song Zhangde, the pseudo-trial department head and political security bureau special envoy and county committee member Zuo Lihu, the pseudo-military commander and county committee member Huang Zhongshi, the pseudo-Young Communist county committee member Huang Meiyun, the pseudo-farmers' association president Song Qixun, the pseudo-rising district committee members He Shenming, Xiang Xiangzhi, Hu Qiyun, Li Yufu, and Song Qizheng, the pseudo-liaison officers Yang Qijiang and Wan Zhengli, the pseudo-mutual aid society chairman Xiao Dafa, the pseudo-cadre training class instructor Ke Xugui, the pseudo-Young Women's Pioneer captain Wu Yu Shi, the pseudo-Youth Women's Group leader Xiang Xiao Shi, the pseudo-Youth League leader Zou Hezhen, the pseudo-Red Labor Union Committee member Huang Dequan, the pseudo-Youth League leader Liu Yunli, the pseudo-Women's Department Minister Xu Yu Shi, the pseudo-branch secretaries Zhang Zhaokai, Fang Xiangde, and Fang Xiangda, the pseudo-confiscation section chief Liu Zhengbang, the pseudo-gray organization executive committee member Dong Ruizhi, the pseudo-town Soviet chairmen Xiang Fuchen, Luo Zhengde, Hu Yunfa, and Yin Benlu, the pseudo-village representatives Cheng Qixian and Xiang Liangxing, the pseudo-general liaison office chairman Cheng Gongfu, the branch office chairman Yuan Yiping and Yuan Yichen, the pseudo-mutual aid society member Ye Kaiqi, the pseudo-gray group leader Yu Junzhi, the pseudo-sentry Cao Maopu and Chen Sima, the pseudo-worker organization minister Chen Jingkun, the pseudo-Young Communist executive committee member Li Fushen, the pseudo-comfort team leader Chen Shi Shi, the pseudo-Youth Worker Minister Xiao Shili, the pseudo-county Soviet committee Chen Guangxin, the bandit-colluding Baozhang Xiang Longyu, and the bandit-colluding Jiazhang Liu Xianxing and Yuan Fuping, totaling more than fifty people, have all been executed separately. There are also the pseudo-Labor Union Standing Committee member Ke Dashu, the pseudo-Beishan Work Group Chairman Tian Tianshun, the pseudo-Young Communist Committee member Yuan Huicheng, the pseudo-County Soviet Government Inspector Qin Guangming, the pseudo-Battalion Deputy Liu Jiayu, and the pseudo-Eastern Hubei Provincial Committee Member Duan Qichun, etc., who surrendered and turned against the communists, remaining in the corps to work. As for the refugees from various places, because the bandit areas have just been recovered, they are returning one after another, lacking both clothing and food, and suffering greatly. Upon receiving the report, Chairman Chiang telegraphed the provincial government on the 5th, ordering them to quickly accept and resettle them in order to save the survivors and cultivate vitality. (February 5th)

Post-Disaster Issues in Fujian Province

Chairman Chen Yi Convenes Meetings of Various Committees

Dividing Various Tasks such as Military Demobilization, Bandit Suppression, Civil Administration, and Finance

Major Bandit Suppression War in Northern Fujian to be Launched Soon

Fuzhou Dispatch: The new provincial government chairman Chen Yi and committee members Zheng Zhenwen, Chen Ticheng, Lin Zhiyuan, Li Shijia, and Xu Fu have arrived in the province. The committee members are scheduled to take office on the 5th. Wang Zhengting, the central government's supervisor, arrived in Fujian from Shanghai on the 2nd aboard the Hai Rong warship, expected to arrive on the 3rd. The seals of the provincial committee and various departments are also being brought by Wang. The government departments are all being taken over by the new appointees on the 3rd. The old personnel have all been dismissed and will be reappointed later. However, the repair costs for the provincial government and various departments were recently discussed and decided by the provincial committee, and a letter was sent to the finance commissioner's office requesting the allocation of 5,000 yuan for use. However, Xu Fu, citing insufficient income, has not yet allocated the funds after several days, so many necessary appliances have not been purchased. Moreover, many documents have been lost after the chaos. It is expected that they will not be able to start working immediately after the establishment without major replenishment and reorganization. The first priority of the new provincial government should be the post-disaster problems of the region. On the 2nd, provincial government chairman Chen Yi and Eastern Route Commander-in-Chief Chiang Ting-wen convened provincial government committee members Li Shijia, Lin Zhiyuan, Chen Ticheng, Zheng Zhenwen, and Xu Fu, as well as military commissioners Du Qiyun, Tan Shuqing, Song Yuanyuan, and Zhang Zhen, to discuss the demobilization of local troops, bandit suppression, civil administration reorganization, and financial unification. The discussions touched on all of these. It is heard that the content of the provincial government meeting mainly concerned the salary issues of the troops stationed in the province, which are all allocated by the central government. However, the local troops recruited by the various military commissioners are all being reorganized into provincial security teams, with a maximum limit of 10,000 men, divided into five brigades, with a security commander to oversee them. (The post of security commander has been appointed by the military commission to Xiao Qian, who will soon arrive in Fujian.) The salaries will be borne by the local government. Regarding the division of financial management in the province, local taxes will still be managed by the finance department, and national taxes will be managed by the finance commissioner's office.

The plan for suppressing the Red bandits in northern Fujian is still being undertaken by Eastern Route Commander-in-Chief Chiang Ting-wen. Currently, the Red bandits in northern Fujian are still entrenched in Shunchang, Jiangle, Sha County, and Yong'an counties, and have kidnapped Liu Qiming, the Sha County magistrate. They are also dividing their forces to spy on Youxi, Yanping, and Shaowu counties. They are currently in a stalemate with the divisions of Lu Xingbang, Liu Heding, and Zhou Zhiqun. Once the main force arrives, they will be able to encircle the bandit forces. Therefore, the large-scale bandit suppression war in northern Fujian is expected to begin soon. (February 3rd)

Jiangxi Province

Rapid Progress of the Banking Industry

All Trades and Professions in Decline, Market Stagnant

Eight Banks Alone Reap Huge Profits

Nanchang Dispatch: Jiangxi is suffering from the national economic decline and the spread of banditry everywhere. All industries are in decline. Even in the case of commerce, due to rural bankruptcy and low social purchasing power, the market is stagnant and unbearable. However, the banking business is thriving. It is found that there are eight banks in this province. The branches from Shanghai are the Central Bank, the Bank of China, the Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank, and the China & South Sea Bank. The provincial banks are the Yumin Bank, the Construction Bank, and the Municipal Bank. There is also the Jiangxi Branch of the Farmers Bank of Henan, Hubei, Anhui, and Jiangxi Provinces, whose sole purpose is to provide relief to the rural areas affected by banditry. Among them, the Central Bank has the most developed business. Because Chairman Chiang was stationed in Jiangxi last year to supervise the suppression, the troops that directly or indirectly received salaries from the military headquarters numbered no less than fifty or sixty divisions. Each division was paid 150,000 yuan per month, totaling six or seven million. Most of this was remitted through the Central Bank. In addition, the military headquarters and various agencies' incoming and outgoing funds were entirely handled by this bank. The monthly business volume was around ten million yuan, and the annual volume was around one hundred million yuan. Therefore, the Central Bank's Jiangxi Branch made a profit of between 100,000 and 200,000 yuan last year. The Bank of China, in addition to government funds, surpassed the Central Bank in commercial terms. The Shanghai-Jiangxi exchange and local lending were dominated by this bank. Last year's profits were also over 100,000 yuan. The Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank has seen its business grow daily since its establishment. Small and medium-sized merchants and retail depositors are happy to do business with it. In particular, the savings department absorbs the floating capital of the middle class. The turnover is quite flexible. The China & South Sea Bank, due to its smaller size, has not been able to develop its business and is not worth mentioning. The Yumin Municipal Construction Bank all had surpluses in their business last year. The dividends were about 10,000 to 45,000 yuan. The Farmers Bank of the Four Provinces was established to provide relief to rural areas. It has now established warehouses for the consignment and mortgage of agricultural products and has lent small amounts of money to cooperatives in various places. Its business should be considered separately. According to people in the financial sector, the business of various banks has been thriving in recent years, which is in inverse proportion to the daily decline of various industries. Although there are many reasons, they do not go beyond the following: (1) Rural bankruptcy, financial capital is gradually concentrating in the cities, with banks being the final destination. (2) The middle and upper classes from other counties have abandoned their properties and brought their money to the province to take refuge, preferring to deposit it in large banks at low interest rates for the sake of stability. (3) Banks deposit funds at low interest rates and lend them to small and medium-sized merchants at high interest rates, earning a lot of profit on interest. (4) Due to the disappearance of export goods in this province, the financial system has lost its balance of circulation. Those who handle goods in Shanghai have no export goods to offset, so they buy drafts and banknotes from various banks. The income from the exchange rate is quite considerable, and the banknote price, except after December, is higher than the silver dollar. (5) Banks have relatively strong capital and can manipulate and control everything. However, the fact that various banks are making profits in the midst of the decline of all industries is probably an economically abnormal development and not a good phenomenon. (January 31st)

Suzhou

One Hundred Yuan Forces a Person to Death

In recent times, rural areas have gone bankrupt. Even Suzhou, which is known as paradise, where villages were once well-fed and well-clothed, is now often unable to make ends meet. Tragic scenes have occurred repeatedly. Yesterday (the 5th), Shi Guoxing, a villager from Nanzhou Village, Weiting, 31 years old, with a wife and three children, the eldest being eight years old and the youngest only two years old, whose family was originally well-off, has been suffering losses due to the low grain prices over the years. This past spring, he entrusted Shi Heqing to guarantee a loan of one hundred yuan from the Yitai Rice Shop outside Loumen, using a farming boat as collateral. The loan was supposed to be repaid with eighty yuan in the summer and forty yuan in the winter. The latter payment had not yet been made, but Yitai continued to lend the boat for use. Unexpectedly, on the afternoon of the 4th, Shi Guoxing followed eighty or so villagers to the city to load firewood. Yang Tai asked him about the repayment date, but Shi remained silent and left. Yesterday (the 5th) morning, it was suddenly discovered that Shi had hanged himself with the boat rope in front of Yitai's river pier. The local court was notified to come and inspect the body. At the same time, Yitai went to summon the deceased's family to the city to handle the aftermath. It is heard that more than ten rice shops in Suzhou, including those outside Kuatang and Loumen, and on North Street in the city, have loaned out a total of about three to four hundred thousand yuan to villagers as farming capital. This year, less than thirty or forty percent of the villagers have repaid on schedule. Now that this incident has occurred, the rice merchants are even more worried. This is also an important issue amid the sounds of the New Year's drums.

Jailer Suspended from Duty for Custodial Care

Jiang Mengxiong, the county government's jailer, was found to have been corrupt in his handling of prison administration. The Judicial Yuan and the High Court have repeatedly sent commissions to investigate. Shen Jiayi, commissioned by the Judicial Yuan, came to the county on the 17th of last month to investigate. The Ministry immediately ordered the county government to suspend Jiang from duty and investigate him. The official document arrived on the 24th of the previous month. Former County Magistrate Feng was about to leave office and did not have time to deal with it. The new County Magistrate Xu Cixuan only took office on the 1st of this month. Lin Biao, President of the High Court, came to the county on the 3rd to reinvestigate. That day, Jailer Jiang went to Shanghai again to socialize and was not found. It is heard that after the investigation, President Lin took away certain account books from the prison. That evening, County Magistrate Xu ordered the First Section Chief Zhang Zhaoxi to temporarily serve concurrently as jailer. He went to take over on the 4th. Jailer Jiang returned from Shanghai and immediately handed over, and was placed under custody and investigation on suspicion of serious crimes. It is now known that the High Court has separately appointed Huang Ruyuan as the jailer of this county, and he will arrive in the coming days.

Small Steamer Service Launched Between Chonggu and Baihe

Qingpu Dispatch: There has been no small steamer service between Baihejiang and Chonggu, which has been very inconvenient for travelers. Now, local resident Qian Jun has raised funds to purchase a small steamer to run between Chonggu and Baihe. The steamer passes through Zhangyan and cooperates with the Zhuan and Tongji companies, which run between Zhujiajiao and Anting. If travelers from Shanghai want to go to Chonggu or Zhangyan, they only need to take the Shanghai-Nanjing Express train to Anting at 9:00 AM or 12:15 PM every day, transfer to the two steamers, disembark at Baihejiang, and transfer to the newly opened Chong-Bai small steamer to arrive safely.

Three years ago, they adopted the daughter of Feng Jinshi from Qingyang South Street, Jiangyin, as their daughter-in-law. However, Fuquan's wife was extremely shrewish and often abused the adopted daughter-in-law in every possible way, beating her mercilessly, causing her to be covered in bruises, with head injuries and bleeding. Upon the adopted daughter-in-law's death, Fuquan and his wife secretly buried her that day and reported to Feng Jinshi the next day that she had died suddenly from a disease. Since the construction department and the Shanghai Municipal Government actively planned the Wuxi-Shanghai highway, the section from Changshu eastward to Shanghai is now open to traffic. The Dingfeng Grain Distillery under the Dashi Bridge was established with funds raised by local residents Tang Hanzhou and others. Subsequently, the creditors of the distillery elected representatives to add shares and continue the business. However, it still went bankrupt in the fall, losing 16,000 to 17,000 yuan. Afterwards, Tang sold the distillery's site and assets to a certain drug store for 1,500 yuan. The creditors learned of this and sent four representatives, including Zhu Jianqiu, to negotiate with Tang and retain the funds to be distributed publicly. Unexpectedly, the four representatives, believing that they also had more than 6,000 yuan in claims, refused to hand over the 1,500 yuan for distribution. The other creditors were panicked and went to Tang Hanzhou's house yesterday to negotiate. Because Tang avoided meeting them, they dragged Tang's wife, Zhuang, to the Public Security Bureau's First Sub-bureau. The sub-bureau stated that the matter concerned the judiciary and advised them to file a formal lawsuit with the court.

Twelve-Weir Salt Workers' Petition Causes Trouble

Due to the increase of six additional quota tickets for the wheel transport of edible salt on the Hunan bank by the salt workers and the labor and management sides of Twelve-Weir, and the fact that Taihe, Hengji, and An two wheel companies are also lowering prices to attract business, the sailboat transport is severely impacted and its livelihood is endangered. Therefore, the Twelve-Weir Eighteen Gang Sailboat General Company elected directors Duan Zhizhou, Wu Songping, Xie Zhaojia, Zheng Xinru, Tang Yuefeng, Xie Zizhen, and more than 20 representatives, including Chen Zhensheng from the Salt Pu Workers' Union, to come to Yangzhou to petition all parties. After arriving in Yangzhou, Twelve-Weir received news that Anhui bank had added 400 quota tickets for wheel transport, and Hunan bank had added more than 30 quota tickets for transport. All the workers were extremely panic-stricken. They immediately went to the salt affairs inspection branch to petition. One person was stabbed to death and more than ten were injured by the bayonets of the tax police regiment. On the other hand, they telegraphed all the representatives in Yangzhou, saying that more than 3,000 salt workers were preparing to come to Yangzhou on the 6th to petition. At the same time, the Jiangdu County Government received the above news. Considering the importance of local public security during this winter defense period, it immediately sent the chief inspector of the Public Security Bureau, Lang Huizhang, to advise the representatives to proceed according to the proper procedure and not to come to Yangzhou for the time being. Therefore, the representatives telegraphed the salt workers of Twelve-Weir, etc., to postpone their arrival in Yangzhou. The representatives scheduled to petition Shen Yintang, the deputy of Yunfu at the Four Banks Public Office, who came to Yangzhou to receive the Yunfu file, and Taihe, Hengji, and An two wheel companies on the 6th.

Bandits Rob and Injure a Person on the Road

Zhu Jian, a bill collector from Dayuan Cloth Store on Jiaochang Street in Yangzhou City, went to the Leitang Bridge area in the western countryside at the end of last month to collect bills. Yesterday, he arrived at Dayi. Because he had already collected more than 300 yuan and was afraid that it would be inconvenient to carry the money far, he happened to meet a familiar rickshaw puller named Xiao Feng. So he asked Xiao Feng to deliver the money to the city this morning (the 4th). Unexpectedly, Xiao Feng was ambushed by three bandits on the road about eight miles from the city at Xiaomaoshan. In addition to robbing all the more than 300 yuan in cash and scattered items, Xiao Feng's head was cut with a knife on the spot. Xiao Feng struggled to stand up from the pool of blood and walked with difficulty. He arrived in the city with injuries at dusk and was admitted to Datong Hospital for treatment.

The Linpu Wheel, which runs from Shipu to Sizhoutou, Xiangshan, was sailing back to Shipu from Xiezhentou, Sizhoutou yesterday when eleven pirates disguised themselves and boarded the ship. When the ship sailed to Hejingdu, the pirates began to rob. They first fought with the four escort police on the ship, resulting in one escort police officer being killed and one being injured. Two pirates were shot dead by the police, and one was injured. One passenger and one squad leader of the defense regiment were also killed by stray bullets. All the guns and ammunition of the escort police were robbed by the bandits. Five or six passengers on the ship, including Yang Bangcai, the manager of Shipu Yudanan Goods Store, Yan Xianlin, the owner of Longtai Nan Goods Store, and a young girl, were kidnapped by the bandits. The clothes and silver dollars carried by the passengers on the ship were all robbed. Then the pirates forced the helmsman to steer the ship towards the Fengyang sea. Later, at Chong'ao, Beian, the pirates took the stolen goods and hostages ashore. The total loss is about seven or eight thousand yuan.

Financial Sector Investigates Shanghai Business Community

Still Able to Barely Maintain

Rumors of Large-Scale Closures

Believed to Be Overstated

Central News Agency reports that with the approach of the Lunar New Year, some businesses in Shanghai are facing closures due to financial difficulties. It is even said that dozens of large stores on Nanjing Road will close at this time. According to inquiries made by the Central News Agency reporter with the local financial sector yesterday morning, these rumors are exaggerated. The economic panic in recent years is not unique to China, nor is it limited to Shanghai. Financial and industrial sectors in various places routinely close their accounts every winter. Naturally, a very small number of stores may experience debt disputes or even close down due to financial reasons. This is common. During the Lunar New Year this year, such events will certainly occur in Shanghai. According to a survey by the financial sector, the economic panic in Shanghai's financial and business communities this Lunar New Year is slightly better than last year, and most businesses are able to barely maintain.

Income of Eight Million Only Covers Expenses

Japanese Rice Dumped in China

Extremely Difficult in Practice

Chinese People Should Pay Attention

Central News Agency reports that there were previous rumors in this city that a large amount of domestic rice was being shipped to the Northeast, and recently there have been rumors that Japan will ship a large amount of food to China to dump it. Because this matter is of great importance, the reporter specially inquired about the truth from various related parties. The information obtained is as follows:

News from Rice Merchants According to information obtained from food merchants, since the domestic bumper harvest the year before last, there has been a surplus of rice stored in the interior. Although the harvest last year was not as good as the year before last, the accumulated rice from previous years is not easy to sell at once, resulting in a sharp drop in rice prices, which has only been seen in recent years. The suffering of farmers is deep, and merchants also feel very distressed. In view of this, the government has levied import taxes on foreign rice. The dumping of foreign rice in the country over the years has been a major reason for the sharp drop in rice prices. Since the government began collecting foreign rice taxes, the import of foreign rice has indeed decreased. As for Japan shipping a large amount of rice to China for dumping in recent days, it is also an extremely difficult matter in practice. Chinese merchants also have no ability to sell Japanese rice on their behalf.

News from Authorities The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau has also sent personnel to investigate the matter of selling domestic rice to the Northeast, but has not been able to confirm it so far. With the current sharp drop in domestic rice prices, in order to raise prices, in addition to paying attention to domestic rice regulation, efforts should also be made to sell rice abroad, so that rice prices may rise. As for the dumping of Japanese rice in China, because Japan is not a rice-producing country, and its domestic rice prices are usually higher than those in China, with the current sharp drop in Chinese rice prices, there is no profit to be made from dumping Japanese rice in China. However, the Japanese side may have other plans, and the Chinese government and rice merchants should pay attention to it in order to stabilize the rice market.
