Silk Sales Gradually Picking Up, Prices Rising

Silk Factories Are Preparing to Start Work

More than Ten Factories Have Resumed Work in Recent Days

Cars Will Be Started Successively After the Lunar New Year

The Dagong News Agency reports that there are a total of 108 single and double cocoon reeling factories in this city. Since the autumn of last year, due to the sharp drop in the silk market and sluggish sales, the factories have been unable to maintain operations, and almost all of them have stopped work. Now, silk sales in Europe and the United States are gradually picking up, and spring cocoons will also be on the market, so the silk factories will start work successively after the Lunar New Year. The details are recorded below:

Increase in Work Resumption

In Shanghai, there are more than 50 single cocoon reeling factories and 5 double cocoon silk factories in the Chang'an Road area of Xinzha Bridge in Zhabei District, 17 single cocoon silk factories and 2 double cocoon silk factories in the Tiantong Road Xiangyan Bridge area of Hongkou District, 8 single cocoon silk factories in the Caojiadu area of the West Shanghai District, 5 single cocoon silk factories in the Route Albesert area of the Concession District, and 4 silk factories in the Dapuqiao Rihuigang area of the South Shanghai District. In total, there are 108 single and double cocoon silk factories in the city. More than 60 factories were operating in the spring and summer of last year. Since the autumn, due to the sharp drop in silk prices and sluggish sales, it has been difficult to maintain operations, so they have successively stopped work. Only three or four factories are barely operating. Now, silk sales are gradually picking up, and prices have also risen slightly, so Yongheng, Xiangsheng, Fulunheng in Hongkou District, and Yuanxin, Jiyu, Chuxin in Zhabei District, Jingwei in the Concession District, and Baotai in the South District have successively started work and resumed operations.

Slight Increase in Silk Prices

The white spun silk produced by the factories could be sold for more than 900 yuan per package in May and June last year. Yellow factory silk could also be sold for about 800 yuan, and Sichuan factory silk could be sold for more than 700 yuan. Since the autumn, the prices have gradually declined, and each package is only sold for about 500 yuan, so each package must lose more than 200 yuan. The factories had no choice but to deposit the produced goods in the bank. Now, European sales are gradually picking up, and silk prices have also increased slightly compared to before. The current highest-priced white factory silk can be sold for about 600 yuan per package, and other types of silk, such as Sichuan factory silk, can also be sold for more than 500 yuan, so the factories are quite optimistic about the future of silk sales and will gradually start work to maintain their business.

Factory Preparations

Yesterday, the Dagong News Agency reporter visited people in the silk industry to inquire about the opening dates of the silk factories in this city. According to them, after silk sales have picked up, the factories in this city have prepared to start work successively. However, due to the approaching Lunar New Year recently, the money market is extremely tight, and it is inevitable that capital turnover is difficult. Therefore, after the New Year, the factories will start work one after another. However, the silk industry crisis is deep, and it is hoped that the Silk Industry Control Association will seek fundamental relief measures as soon as possible, so that China's only silk industry will not be on the verge of bankruptcy and have the hope of revitalization.

The Yangtze River Water Level Is Decreasing Again

Navigation Is More Difficult

The Yangtze River water level has suddenly decreased since January 15. The water level at Madang was 8 feet 9 inches. By the 5th, the Jianghan Customs lifted the ban on the new port to open the navigation route. Unexpectedly, yesterday, the water level receded again, and the river ships still had difficulty navigating. The details are recorded as follows:

The Water at the New Port Receded Again

When the Yangtze River is at its shallowest near Xiaogushan in Madang, it recedes to 8 feet 9 inches, and all Yangtze River ships are obstructed. Jianghan Customs closed the new port there and prohibited ships from traveling. Until the 5th of this month, after the Jianghan Customs measured the results, the water level at the new port in Madang was 10 feet 4 inches, which was larger than the old port. Ships with a draft of about 10 feet can pass through. Unexpectedly, yesterday afternoon, various shipping companies in Shanghai received a telegram from Hankou saying that the new port in Madang had just been unblocked and opened for navigation, but the river water had receded again. Yesterday, it had dropped to 9 feet 8 inches, and larger ships could not transport goods. It is still necessary to use barges to drag the bottom to pass.

Longping Also Reports Shallow Water

The water level above Jiujiang is originally larger than the upstream. During the period of water reduction in Madang, the Yangtze River near Longping Dayanshan is often about 10 feet 5 inches. Unexpectedly, yesterday, Shanghai received a report that the water in Longping has suddenly dropped in the past two days, only 10 feet. Jianghan Customs has issued a notice restricting the transportation of goods by upstream river ships not exceeding 10 feet. Therefore, the Yangtze River ships of the six companies in this port can only load one-third of their capacity. If they transport a little more, they must use barges to transfer and unload, which is very troublesome.

Stranded Ships Are Difficult to Escape Danger

The Sanbei Changxing ship, which ran aground at the old port in Madang, has been there for a week. Repeated dragging has been ineffective and has not escaped the danger. Yesterday, the company connected two telegram reports, saying that the coal and food in the ship are complete and requested the company to quickly provide relief. Because the ship has no hope of being towed out of the shallow water, the ship is currently guarded by military police. As for the ships stranded on the Upper Yangtze River, news was received from Xindi yesterday that the water level is still only 5 feet, and most of the ships are trapped in the sand and mud, and it is difficult to rescue them for a while. Fortunately, imports and exports from the upper and lower reaches of the Yangtze River have been extremely scarce recently, and there is no large-scale cargo loading.

Revision of the

American Cotton Loan Contract

Since the cotton and wheat purchased by our government from the United States with loans began to be loaded last winter, one-third of the American wheat has arrived in full, and only one-sixteenth of the cotton has arrived. Now, because there are very few outlets for cotton, it is inconvenient to load and transport it to China. Compensation for warehouse rent has led to requests to the American authorities to amend the contract. The information obtained by the reporter is described as follows:

Twelve American Wheat Ships Arrive

Since December 18 last year, American wheat has been transported to China by Norton Lilley Co, entrusted by the China Merchants Bureau, one after another through Portland. In seven weeks, a total of twelve ships arrived (including the Hubble Rodney ship of 8,900 tons that arrived yesterday). In total, 93,772 tons have been transported, accounting for one-third of the total of 300,000 tons. Among these twelve ships, one ship carried 7,200 tons, which was unloaded to Nanjing and purchased by Yangzi Flour Mill. The remaining eleven ships were unloaded in Shanghai. The average selling price per ton is 70 yuan. The value of the wheat that has arrived is 6,564,000 yuan.

Flour Has Not Been Shipped Yet

It was agreed that part of the loan of American wheat would be flour, with an amount of 60,000 to 70,000 tons. Since the promulgation of the new tax, the Ministry of Finance has set the import tax at 3 yuan per dan for wheat and 75 yuan for wheat flour, equivalent to more than 1.9 yuan in national currency. According to the current flour price in Shanghai, each package sells for about 2.2 yuan. If American flour is imported, including tariffs, the cost will be at least 2.67 yuan. Because it does not match the market price, the loaned flour has not been telegraphed to start shipping. Only a small batch was brought in by the Milverdale ship last month. It has now been decided to continue shipping American wheat first, because the import cost per dan, including various expenses, is only 4.23 yuan, which is easier to sell. There are still 200,000 tons of goods that must be shipped within 140 days.

Cotton Contract Amendment

The total amount of loaned American cotton is 800,000 pieces, accounting for 400,000 tons, worth 40 million US dollars. According to the original loan contract, all of them must be shipped before June 30 this year. Since the first batch arrived on November 17 last year, only 50,000 pieces have been shipped to Shanghai so far, accounting for only one-sixteenth of the total. Our country advocates selling a batch and shipping a batch, and is unwilling to ship to Shanghai first and bear heavy warehouse rent and other expenses. Recently, because the outlets for domestic cotton are not smooth, and the contract period will expire in June, it will be difficult to sell them all within the limited time. Therefore, our country has decided to propose amendments to the American cotton loan contract to the American authorities, extending the deadline by half a year or several months to facilitate sales. At present, this matter has been requested to the American government, and it is heard that the United States has agreed and is discussing amending the contract.

National Chamber of Commerce Telegraph Request

National Government to Consider Reducing Match Tax

And Limit Time to Clear Existing Stock

The National Federation of Chambers of Commerce yesterday sent a telegram to the National Government, the Ministry of Finance, and the Ministry of Industry, stating: "To the esteemed Nanjing National Government, the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Finance, and the Ministry of Industry: Recently, we received a joint letter from Gao Songfu, representative of Shanghai Dahua Match Factory, Sun Runzhai, representative of the Shanguo China Match Factory, Xi Jianqing, representative of Nantong Tongsui Match Factory, Cai Keming, representative of Shanghai Huaming Match Factory, Xu Huisheng, representative of Ningbo Zhengda Match Factory, Bao Zhen, representative of Wenzhou Suichang Match Factory, Shao Xiushan, representative of Shanghai Daming Match Factory, and Xu Guangji and Wu Yihua, representatives of Linhuai Huai Shang Match Factory. The letter roughly stated: 'The match industry involves foreign merchants using machinery for manufacturing, while our country uses manual imitation. The labor costs and production differ by a ratio of one to fifteen. Recently, due to foreign merchants dumping goods and fierce competition among domestic companies, the supply exceeds demand, and prices have fallen from 40 yuan per case to below 30 yuan. Manufacturers are struggling to maintain operations and are in a precarious situation. This year, we suddenly received a notice from the Ministry of Finance that the unified match tax, originally 7.5 yuan per case, has been increased to 17.4 yuan. Upon hearing this, manufacturers felt like they had been struck by lightning. To levy a tax of 17.4 yuan on goods worth over 20 yuan per case is equivalent to a tax rate of 70%. This increased tax could originally be compensated for in the price of the goods, with manufacturers only bearing the responsibility of collecting and remitting the tax. However, the manufacturers are all undercapitalized and cannot cope with such a sudden increase in the tax amount. Moreover, before the tax increase, foreign merchants and large factories had tens of thousands of cases in stock. The market price cannot be averaged due to the tax increase. It will take at least five or six months for their inventory to be cleared. The manufacturers are unable to sustain operations and have been forced to request your association to forward our request to the central government, asking it to consider the difficulties faced by small factories and provide support by appropriately reducing the tax rate and setting a time limit for clearing existing inventory as a form of relief. We eagerly await your assistance.' The representatives were also allowed to present their case in person at the meeting. Upon approval, it was found that matches are daily necessities, and a tax rate of 70% will affect all the people. Furthermore, the uneven distribution of inventory among factories has led to uneven market prices, creating an opportunity for large factories to overwhelm small factories. Based on the information in the letter, we hereby telegraphically submit this matter to your esteemed Yuan and ministries for review and approval. We earnestly request that you approve a reduction in the tax and set a time limit for clearing existing inventory to provide relief. Respectfully, Lin Kanghou, Chairman of the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce, (Seal)."

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Cables Executive Yuan Again

Requesting Release of Confiscated Local Sugar from Qinzhou and Lianzhou

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday sent a telegram to the Executive Yuan and the Ministries of Finance and Industry, stating: "On the 5th of this month, we received a letter from Pang Songhui, a representative of the sugar merchants of Qinzhou and Lianzhou in Guangdong, stating: 'Various groups have risen up to provide relief, and our representatives have repeatedly described the plight of the sugar merchants and requested assistance from your association. They have also petitioned the relevant ministries and departments in Beijing. We are grateful that you have understood our difficulties and accommodated our requests. Everyone was eagerly awaiting the reversal of this unjust case and striving to resume business. However, before the government's protective measures could be implemented, the Jianghai Customs intensified its destruction of local sugar. On January 23rd of this year, our colleague Henghelong transported 92 bags of 'K' marked local white sugar from Beihai on the Hubei steamer, which were received by Fu Tianshen firm in Shanghai. They reported the sugar to the Beihai Customs for inspection. The sugar was produced by the Lunchang sugar workshop in Wulixu, Lingshan County, and was certified as purely local produce. However, upon re-inspection by the Jianghai Customs in Shanghai, it was claimed that the sugar had a polarization reading of 92.8 degrees and contained more than 50% foreign sugar, and should be confiscated. Upon hearing this, we were shocked and perplexed. The Central Industrial Testing Institute was ordered last month to test type C local sugar from Qionghai County's Shizilu, which had a polarization reading of 92 degrees, while type B local sugar reached 93 degrees. The local sugar from Qinzhou and Lianzhou is even better than that of Qiongyai. Now, the Jianghai Customs' test results show a reading of less than 93 degrees, yet they claim that it contains more than half foreign sugar. What is the basis for this claim? Since last September, our sugar merchants have suffered from fines and suspensions imposed by the Jianghai Customs, and have been unemployed for several months. Fortunately, the government has agreed to provide protection, and we are just starting to resume business when we are subjected to this even more violent destruction. What hope do we have for the future? We are compelled to earnestly request your association to provide assistance again and truthfully forward this matter to the relevant ministries and departments of the central government for immediate relief measures: (1) Order the Jianghai Customs to immediately release the local sugar in this case. If it is absolutely impossible, please retain it pending a public re-inspection and absolutely prohibit its sale at auction. (2) Send personnel to the sugar-producing areas of Qinzhou and Lianzhou for on-site inspection. If it is inconvenient to send personnel, please order the Qinzhou and Lianzhou Sugar Industry Guangyitang to collect samples of local sugar with public certification from local party and government agencies, mass organizations, and send them to Beijing for testing to establish standards for distinguishing foreign sugar, in order to reverse the previous erroneous handling of cases and ensure the safety of future transportation. We are in urgent need of assistance.' Upon receipt of this letter, we found that eight or nine cases of Guangdong's entrepot local sugar being accused by customs of being mixed with foreign sugar and being detained and punished have occurred. The duration has been seven or eight months, ranging from Qiongyai to Qinzhou and Lianzhou. Our association has repeatedly received letters from the representatives of the sugar merchants there, as well as from local chambers of commerce, and has repeatedly petitioned your Yuan and ministries to seek redress, but no resolution has been reached to date. According to the aforementioned, the sugar shipped from Beihai to Shanghai was certified as purely local sugar produced by the Lunchang sugar workshop in Wulixu, Lingshan County, but the Jianghai Customs again detained it, claiming it was mixed with foreign sugar and planning to confiscate it. It should be known that the value of foreign sugar is higher than that of local sugar, and there is no need to pay taxes on the entrepot of foreign sugar according to regulations. Sugar merchants would never mix foreign sugar into local sugar to increase the quantity,"

Page 12

"and pay an additional entrepot tax. Our association has clearly stated this in previous telegrams and petitions. However, the Jianghai Customs officials continue their destructive actions, which will leave Guangdong's local sugar with no foothold and contradict the Ministry of Industry's announced plan to revitalize national sugar. Therefore, we respectfully submit this telegram to your esteemed Yuan and ministries for review and approval. We earnestly request that you consider the long-standing requests for relief made by our association and the two points raised by the sugar merchants this time, and provide remedies to alleviate the sugar merchants' plight. This would be the most fair and convenient solution. The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce respectfully pleads."

Social Affairs Bureau Instructs Municipal Chamber of Commerce

All Salt to Be Weighed Using New Market Scales

And Verification of Reductions in Regular and Additional Taxes

The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau yesterday instructed the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, stating: "According to the Municipal Government Instruction No. 8467, 'Regarding the Ministry of Finance's directive on the implementation of unified weights and measures, a general order has been issued to all salt-producing areas, starting from January 1st of this year, to uniformly use the new market scales for weighing salt, while the tax collection will remain at the old rate. Currently, according to the verification report of the General Inspection Office, merchants and citizens in various regions are accustomed to old habits and are hesitant about adopting the new market scales, etc. The promotion of the new system of weights and measures is a key policy of the central government, and the hesitancy of merchants and citizens will affect salt tax revenues. It is proposed that your Municipal Government instruct its subordinate agencies to provide assistance and encourage merchants and citizens to enthusiastically comply without delay, in order to benefit salt administration. This has been communicated by telegram and is hereby relayed for your information and strict compliance. Please also provide feedback.' Upon receiving this instruction, while processing it, we received Municipal Government Instruction No. 8474, which stated: 'Regarding the Ministry of Finance's Order No. 2022 on the implementation of the new system of weights and measures, a general order has been previously issued to the subordinate agencies to expedite preparations and implement it by a deadline. Currently, the salt affairs and tax agencies under the Ministry only use weighing instruments for inspecting and collecting goods, making preparation easier. Therefore, the new system should be adopted as early as possible to promote it. The date of January 1st, the 23rd year, is set as the date for the salt affairs and tax agencies to implement the new system of weights and measures. All goods subject to inspection and collection will be calculated using the new weighing instruments at that time to achieve uniformity. As for the tax amount to be collected, it will still be collected according to the legal tax rate, based on the market standard of jin and dan. Furthermore, in order to rectify salt administration and equalize the burden, all central regular and additional salt taxes and local surtaxes, totaling more than 10 yuan to 13 yuan per dan, have also been instructed by telegram to be reduced to 10 yuan starting from January 1st of the 23rd year. The central regular and additional taxes and local surtaxes will be reduced proportionally. Those below 10 yuan will be improved gradually after assessing the situation, so that the plan for equalizing taxes can be gradually realized. The salt affairs agencies have been instructed by telegram to comply, and it has been reported to the Executive Yuan, which issued a directive stating, "This case has been submitted to the 141st meeting of the Yuan and the resolution to approve the record has been passed." This has been communicated by telegram and is hereby forwarded for your information.' Upon receiving this instruction, we hereby instruct your association to take note. This instruction is hereby issued."

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and Jiaoji Railway Joint Transportation

To Be Implemented Starting March 1st

Tan Shukui and Others Who Went to Guangdong for Inspection

Returned to Shanghai Yesterday and Will Return to Qingdao Soon

According to a report from a news agency, after the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and the Jiaoji Railway signed a detailed contract to handle water and land joint transportation, the Jiaoji Railway specially dispatched Tan Shukui, Deputy Director of the Transportation Department, along with Wang Xichang, Deputy Director and Senior Consultant of the Qingdao Municipal Port Authority, to Shanghai and then to Shantou and Guangzhou to inspect matters related to joint transportation. They returned to Shanghai the day before yesterday. Yesterday, they met with Liu Hongsheng, General Manager of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, He Molin, Head of the Business Department, and Zhou Fengtu, Director of the Joint Transportation Division, and decided to return to Qingdao by the Shanghai-Nanjing train in the next few days. It is reported that the date for the Jiaoji Railway's joint transportation has been set for March 1st.

Two Railway Bureaus

Dredging Coal Wharf and Dock in Nanjing

Gao Yuji Contracted at 1.4 Yuan per Cubic Meter

Due to silt accumulation caused by river tides, the coal wharf and dock at the Nanjing Riverside Station of the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway are periodically filled. Traditionally, the bureau undertakes dredging to facilitate transshipment. Recently, further silting has been discovered. The Public Works Department contracted Gao Yuji to dredge the area. A contract was signed on December 15th of last year, with the following key points: (1) The railway bureau will supply the coal-dredging machine and mechanics, while the contractor will be responsible for providing the mud barges and loading/unloading workers. (2) The price is 1.4 yuan per 28.317 cubic meters (i.e., per cubic meter). (3) Payment will be made in three installments: 2,500 yuan after completing 2,000 cubic meters, 2,500 yuan after completing 4,000 cubic meters, and the remaining balance 14 days after completing the entire project. (4) The entire project must be completed within 75 days from the date of approval of the contract by the railway bureau, excluding two days. A penalty of 10 yuan per day will be imposed for any delays. The dredging project is currently underway.

Two Railways

Establishing Model Stations at Major Stations

According to the Central News Agency, the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administrations have decided to establish model stations at major stations along the lines in order to improve all stations. Then, this improvement will be extended to other stations. The Shanghai, Suzhou, Changzhou, Wuxi, Danyang, Zhenjiang, and Nanjing stations on the Shanghai-Nanjing line, and the Songjiang, Jiaxing, Xiashi, and Hangzhou stations on the Shanghai-Hangzhou line have been designated to proceed with this plan first. The order has been communicated by the two railway administrations to the aforementioned stations, and preparations have already begun.

Two Railways Hold Material Procurement Review Meeting

The Two Railways Bureau held a Material Procurement Review Committee meeting a few days ago. Zhong Guidan, Rong Qiwen, Zhang Yuandong, Chen Shaobai, Mao Wenzhong, Xiao Weiguo, Wang Yunyuan and others attended and discussed the following cases: (1) The review time for material procurement should be limited to expedite the procurement case, with the proposed review time set as follows: (A) The Materials Department shall prepare the price comparison table after the bidding, with a maximum limit of two days. (B) The representative of the using department shall review the price comparison table, with a maximum limit of three days. (C) The representative of the Chief Auditor's Office shall review the price comparison table, with a maximum limit of one day. (D) The chairman of the Material Procurement Review Committee shall review the price comparison table, with a maximum limit of one day. The resolution was passed as is, except for items B and C, which will not be limited if the purchased materials require special testing or review or the quantity in the comparison table is excessive. (2) If the using department has any objections to the value and quality of the material after the bidding, how should it be resolved? The resolution was that before the material standard is determined, the committee shall jointly review and resolve it. (3) After the review of the material list, the signatures or seals of each member should follow the bureau's order and use Chinese characters to respect the national system. The resolution was that the case was passed as is, and the use of foreign characters for signatures and seals will be invalid in the future. (4) How should the scope of authority of the committee to handle affairs be determined? The resolution was to promote committee member Xiao to draft the detailed rules for handling affairs, submit them to the committee for approval, and then submit them to the bureau for record. (5) How should the review work be accelerated? The resolution was to handle it in the following ways: (A) The Materials Department shall stipulate the unified bidding standard of weights and measures and notify all merchants to comply. (B) The Materials Department shall organize the standard of the bidding materials. (C) If the using department cannot immediately decide on the materials in the price comparison table, the undetermined items should be submitted separately, and the determined items should be handled in accordance with the regulations. (6) Each using department should keep a copy of the material comparison table for future reference. The resolution was that the case was passed as is.

After the Disaster in Hua County

Organizing Immigration to Find Food Elsewhere

First Batch Set at 50,000 People to Be Moved to Counties Along the Pinghan Railway

Xi Dejiong Returns to Shanghai After Inspection, Establishes Reception Center at Daokou

According to Xinsheng News Agency, the Yellow River flooded last autumn, causing a particularly severe disaster in Hua County, Henan Province. The flooded area reached more than 5,500 square miles, more than 14,000 people were drowned, and 300,000 people were affected by the disaster. Although the Disaster Relief Group of the National Government's Yellow River Disaster Relief Association and local disaster relief associations have provided relief, the funds were too small and the disaster was too severe, and the disaster victims have not yet settled down. Unexpectedly, during December of last year, ice floes surged and water receded in various places, but were re-submerged, and disaster victims were in the cold ice, and boats could not cross. Besides a small number of those rescued, there were many deaths and injuries. Liu Zhi, Chairman of Henan Province, Xi Dejiong, Director of the Disaster Relief Group of the Yellow River Disaster Relief Association, and Yang Zigong, Director of the Henan Disaster Survey Office, successively went to inspect and decided to immigrate out to find food elsewhere. Now, a reception center has been established at Daokou Station. Mr. Xi Dejiong returned to Shanghai a few days ago, and Mr. Yang Zigong is in Daokou Town, together with the Henan Disaster Relief Association and the North China Charity Federation, requesting to handle immigration matters. The details are recorded as follows:

Immigration Area

The disaster area in Hua County, especially the fifth, sixth, and seventh districts, was the most severe, with 473 villages flooded, and 140,000 disaster victims who could not survive without relief. The Henan Provincial Government decided to transfer disaster victims from Hua County to neighboring counties along the Pinghan Railway, from Zhangde (now Anyang) in the north to Yancheng in the south. Anyang, Tangyin, Lin County, Wu'an, She County, Ji County, Hui County, Jun County, Huojia, Xinxiang, Qinyang, Bo'ai, Jiyuan, Xiuwu, Yuanwu, Yangwu, Qi County, Yanjin, Zheng County, Mi County, Yu County, Xuchang, Yan County, Xinzheng, Lin Ying, Fugou, Yanling, Weishi, and Weichuan and other counties were designated as resettlement locations, with the number of people to be resettled allocated according to the size of the county: 1,000 to 2,000 people in large counties, 800 to 1,500 people in medium counties, and 500 to 1,000 people in small counties. The first phase is temporarily set at 50,000 people, and more will be transferred in the second phase depending on the situation.

Resettlement Measures

According to the measures set by the Henan Provincial Government, the transfer of disaster victims from Hua County to various counties is for the purpose of temporary food aid. Good lodging should be provided in each county. The county government, together with the local gentry, should allocate resettlement to various districts, villages, and towns, and supervise and protect them. The county magistrates should be responsible for resettlement and prevent people from starving to death or being displaced. Each county should provide disaster victims based on household size, with approximately 30 to 60 households required to support one disaster-stricken household. Temporarily, the county government gentry will allocate it according to the number of disaster victims and the local poverty and wealth. The period of food aid is temporarily set at half a year to one year, and at that time, the situation will be re-evaluated and sent back to the original origin, or if any of them can make a living on their own and are willing to go elsewhere, they will be allowed to go. The county government should cooperate with local agencies to organize a disaster victim supervision committee to be responsible for supervision and protection. The local people must not entice, abduct, sell, abuse, or antagonize them. Disaster victims must not coerce, cause trouble, incite, or conspire secretly. If either party violates the regulations, the county government will handle it impartially.

En Route Provision

When immigrating, from the date of assembly to the date of arrival, daily allowances shall be provided, with one jiao per day for adults and five fen per day for children (or converted to japonica rice). For the required trains on each route, the Yellow River Disaster Relief Association of the Government will request the Ministry of Railways to telegraph each railway bureau to approve the allocation of trains free of charge at each station for transportation. The Disaster Relief Group of the Yellow River Disaster Relief Association has received a reply from the Ministry of Railways a few days ago to proceed with the free transportation. Regarding immigration expenses, in addition to the 50,000 yuan already raised by the Henan Provincial Government, the North China Charity Federation donated 10,000 yuan, and the World Red Swastika Society donated 2,000 yuan, which were handed over to the Henan Travel Agency to send personnel to Hua County to handle the matter. However, the transfer of 50,000 people only accounts for one-sixth of the disaster victims, and the majority are still in dire straits. It is hoped that people from all over the world will do their best to rescue them.

Free Transportation

According to the Central News Agency, the Yellow River Water Disaster Relief Association of the National Government issued a message yesterday that due to the large number of disaster victims in Hebei Province, three more porridge factories have been added in the areas where the disaster is most severe in Changyuan, Puyang, and Dongming, each of which can accommodate more than 5,000 people. In addition, the association stated that there are still more than 300,000 disaster victims in Hua County, Yu Province, and that they are trapped in a watery land and are crying out for relief. The association has previously telegraphed the Ministry of Railways to find a way to transport disaster victims free of charge. Yesterday, the association received a reply from the Ministry of Railways agreeing to transport them free of charge immediately. The association immediately telegraphed the Disaster Survey Office of Yu Province to quickly handle immigration to save the people in distress. In addition, the association has recently received a report that Ling Water in the disaster area of Hebei has suddenly increased and the ice flow is rapid. The most severely affected areas are the more than 50 villages of Yangsai Erlangmiao Kou, Cuizhai, Lei Dian Zhai Tuan of the fifth district, and Shitou Village. The lighter areas are the more than 50 villages of Jiu Ji of the second district and Zhi Village of the fifth district. After hearing the news, the local Disaster Survey Office immediately dispatched personnel to knock on the ice for relief and distribute steamed buns, and set up porridge factories separately to arrange the work in a very tense manner.

Fujian Red Cross Telephones Request to Quickly Remit Donations

Rescuing Many Wounded Soldiers Every Day

Huge Need for Funds, Difficult to Maintain

The Fujian Fellowship Association received a telegram from the Fujian Red Cross Society stating, "To the Public Appraisal of the Fujian Fellowship Association: The correspondence and plans have been delivered. For several days, we have been rescuing wounded soldiers, reaching 400 people. The association set up temporary hospitals to treat them, and accommodated more than 1,300 wounded soldiers in three locations, provided meals, and buried more than 200 dead soldiers. The need for funds is huge, and it is difficult to maintain. At this time of year-end, if no measures are taken, they will be scattered in the city, which is no small problem. We have previously requested donations, but have not received a response. This matter concerns our hometown, and we sincerely request your utmost support. If the amount is certain, please remit it quickly. Hoping for a reply, the Fuzhou Red Cross Branch bows deeply."

Sino-Foreign Relief Association News

ShaanxiAccording to the Sino-Foreign Relief Association at 12 Renji Road, this port, Wu Jun, the president of the Shaanxi branch of the Western Association, arrived at the association the day before yesterday to personally describe the recent situation in the province. He said that the Shanghai Association is responsible for the second and fifth major branch canals of the Jinghui Canal. They have long been completed and are now only in the finishing stage of setting up gates and reinforcing bridges. The farmland irrigated by the Jing River, such as millet, beans, grains, and cotton, are all as high as the waist. Compared with those that have not benefited from the rain, they are only knee-high. The harvest in the last autumn was excellent and far beyond expectations, more than three or four times higher. The export of cotton is indeed higher than in any other year. The report also said that the western part of the province is higher in terrain, such as Xingping, Wugong, Qianxian, Fufeng, Qishan, and Fengxiang, which are not covered by the Jinghui Canal. Only a dozen wells can be drilled in each county, and each well can irrigate about 400 mu, and gradually promoted, with the goal of equitable distribution of benefits. Unfortunately, the land is high and the water is low, and each well must be drilled to a depth of 450 feet, resulting in work that is slightly difficult and slightly delayed.

Gaoyou

During the Jiangbei floods of the 20th year of the Republic of China, dozens of breaches occurred in the Yun Dyke, and the towns of Gaoyou and Shaobo were completely submerged, and the people sighed their fish. The association undertook the repairs, and the largest of them, Tangjun Tower, Qigong Temple, Miaoxiang Kou, Yuma Head, Thirty Mile Shop, Twenty Mile Shop, and Six Major Breaches, were built quickly due to time and economic reasons, and were completed last spring. Fortunately, the harvest last year was deeply dependent on the protection of the dam. However, the association has deep considerations, strengthens and seeks to strengthen, and strives to permanently eliminate disasters, so as to avoid repeating the tragedy. It has been discussed and decided to rebuild the stone works. A few days ago, Mr. Wang Shuxiang, Deputy Director of the Dyke Repair, came to Shanghai to report that all the cement, steel bars, yellow sand, stones and all kinds of miscellaneous materials required for this project are all specially sold cheaply by merchants who maintain public welfare, which is very gratifying. As for the construction, the progress is also quite smooth. During the busiest period, 4,000 to 5,000 workers were hired every day. Now, on average, there are more than 1,000 workers every day. It is also said that the reconstruction of the stone works was originally intended to block the traffic on the canal. In order to maintain the lives of boat owners, it had to be rebuilt over the dam, so the construction costs exceeded 10,000 yuan, but the benefits received by the boat owners were more than ten times that. At this time when the weather is cold and the ice is frozen, the work is inevitably slow, but it can be said with certainty that it can be hidden before the Peach Blossom Flood. According to this, once the dam is completed, the lives and property of 4 million people in the eight counties under the wrapping river and the neighboring Huaian and Jiangdu counties will be guaranteed, and Anlan will be celebrated forever.

Huai'an

The Fougong Dyke in the county was washed away by water the previous year, and it has been repaired by the association since last summer because it involves 8,000 acres of fertile land and the lives of 100,000 people. Because the local people know the righteousness and are willing to help with their efforts, according to the original estimate, there is still a surplus of several thousand yuan in foreign currency. It is reported that the association has decided to raise several thousand yuan more and dredge the Yongji River connected to the dam to discharge the flow and irrigate it.

Huaiyin

The Pu Hui Porridge Factory in the county suffered from severe funding shortages and was difficult to maintain this year due to the large number of refugees after the disaster. It is reported that the association has allocated 3,000 yuan and cotton clothes to provide assistance.

Public Concession

Public Works for the Last Year

Private Buildings More Developed Than Last Year

Application for License Started 2778

The Director of Public Works, Happier, reported on his work last year: Private buildings were more developed than the previous year. The amount of construction for which licenses were issued in the district was estimated to be 25,324,100 taels, while in the previous year it was only 18,181,900 taels, an increase of 39 percent. In addition, the total amount of miscellaneous projects is about 1.195 million taels, and the application was filed

Building Permit

A total of 2,778 cases were filed (including 2,154 Chinese and 624 foreigners). The approved cases totaled 1,480 cases. The houses approved for construction include 3,545 Chinese-style houses, 257 Western-style houses, 13 Western-style apartments, 13 offices, 204 Western-style shops, 4 theaters, 27 factories, 20 warehouses, and 784 others. 263 permits were granted for sanitation construction. The busiest month for construction was July and August, with 479 sites under construction at the same time. The smallest was in February, with 342 sites. The old houses demolished in the district included 1,714 Chinese-style houses and 63 Western-style houses. Most of them were demolished and rebuilt. After deducting the demolitions and constructions, 1,831 Chinese-style houses were added this year.

Violation Cases

Due to violations of construction regulations, 906 cases have been given warnings by the Public Works Department. Therefore, inspections must be carried out at any time. In addition, there are as many as 1,105 cases of construction without permission for which warnings have been issued. In a certain area, there are 190 houses of the Hua family, which were not built long ago, and there are 100 places where additions have been made without permission. Adding wooden sheds on the sun deck is the most common offense. In one case, a family added three stories on top of a two-story kitchen, turning it into a five-story building. An even greater danger is the conversion of Chinese-style houses into factories, adding roofs to courtyards, piercing walls, and removing handrails, all of which can lead to danger. Regarding the steel bars used in construction, contractors tend to only consider the price and not the quality. It has been discovered that the load-bearing capacity of steel bars and concrete is insufficient. Therefore, the Public Works Department sincerely hopes that homeowners, designers, and engineers will cooperate with the department to avoid danger. Last year, the department's material testing laboratory conducted 1,267 tests on building materials for public buildings under the bureau, while private individuals only requested 352 tests, indicating that the public has not fully utilized this facility.

Public Buildings

Many large public buildings of the Public Works Department were completed last year, including the police station on Pingliang Road and the married Chinese police officers' residences, the Chinese police officers' residences on Baoding Road, the slaughterhouse and animal pens on Dixiwei Road, the nurses' home on Daxi Road, the Western children's school on Yuyuan Road, the Chinese children's middle school on Jingzhou Road, and the office, two prison cells, a hospital, and a residence for Indian guards at the Huade Road prison. In addition, the police station on Chengdu Road was completed and put into use in January 1934.

Road Works

The Public Works Department currently manages roads with a total length of 182 miles of various pavements. In 1933, repairing road surfaces due to the installation of underground pipelines, etc., covered a length of 5,281 miles, with an area of ​​over 110,000 square yards. To widen and extend the roads, 86 plots of land were acquired, totaling 34 mu, 8 fen, 3 li, and 4 hao, costing 820,725 taels.

Bridges and Wharves

The Public Works Department currently manages 77 bridges, including 8 steel bridges, 18 concrete bridges, and 51 wooden bridges. A new reinforced concrete bridge is currently being built on the Jiading Road Hongkou Creek, with a width of 51 feet. A similar bridge is being built on the Kulun Road Shajing Port, with a width of 41 feet. The deep-water wharf built on Qiwupu Road has been completed and put into use. The pier on Zhaofeng Road has been extended.

Drainage Works

Since the new drainage plan began to be implemented in 1921, a total of 65 miles of ditches have been built to date, with 25 miles of connecting branches, and 72 miles of rainwater sewers and branches. In the past year, 62 sewage pits were abolished, and 187 houses were connected to the drainage pipes. A total of 3,712,646 gallons of disinfectant are applied to sewage in ditches every day.

Cleaning Work

This year, a total of 299,399 tons of household waste were collected, of which 161,620 tons were handed over to contractors to be shipped out by small boats, 89,659 tons were sent to incinerators for incineration, and 50,120 tons were transported to the eastern and western districts to fill in depressions. This year, a total of 52,957 tons of road sweeping and ditch cleaning were carried out, and a total of 42,972,000 gallons of water were used for flushing and watering roads. The Binlang Road and Maohai Road incinerators worked day and night throughout the year. With accumulated experience, the amount of incineration has gradually increased. In the summer, when watermelons are abundant, the moisture content of garbage reaches 45%, making incineration extremely difficult, so 3% of fuel must be added. This is not necessary in autumn and winter. It is now quite effective to preheat the air entering the furnace.

Other Undertakings

The Pingqiao Stone Quarry managed by the Public Works Department produced more than 21,183 cubic meters of material last year. The cement factory produced 177,822 pieces. The foreign poor people's shelter accommodates a total of 210 people at any time, including 1 American, 2 Austrians, 1 Belgian, 1 Briton, 2 Danes, 2 Estonians, 4 French, 5 Germans, 1 Greek, 2 Italians, 6 Latvians, 24 Poles, 156 Russians, 1 Serbian, and 2 Spaniards.

Preliminary plan to order fishing boats from the UK

The Sedimentation of Suzhou Creek Has Been Cleared

Inland Water Vessels Operate as Usual

All Cargo Ships Will Be Suspended Starting From the 9th

The inland river steamship bureaus of the city, such as Lao Gongmao, Tai Dong, and Xie Xing, which operate small cargo steamers to Wuxi, Suzhou, and other places, were previously blocked due to siltation in the area of Laozha Bridge, Sampan Factory Bridge, and Yidaikou of Suzhou Creek. The round trips of ships were appropriate because the end of the year was approaching, and various places were coming to Shanghai to purchase New Year's goods for the market. Therefore, it was very crowded, and when the tide receded, they were all stranded on the accumulated silt and could not travel. Although the water patrol team tried their best to resolve the passage, it was not enough to solve the urgent need. The various steamship bureaus changed the trips to Suzhou and Wuxi to transship goods through Waihuangpu, detouring through Minhang, etc., in order to facilitate freight transportation. At the same time, the inland river steamship companies jointly petitioned the city chamber of commerce to request the Dredging Bureau to find a way to dredge the river in order to reassure travelers. The Dredging Bureau has now sent several dredgers to work, and the river has gradually been dredged. However, the Lunar New Year is approaching, and most merchants have already closed their business, so freight transportation has also decreased in recent days. The previously silted sections can now be connected unimpeded, and the small inland river ships traveling to Suzhou and Wuxi have resumed operations from Wusong River, without having to detour through Waihuangpu. However, as the settlement period is approaching, the amount of freight has sharply decreased, and the shipowners of various cargo ships have to return home to celebrate the Lunar New Year. Therefore, starting from the 9th, all passenger and cargo ships from various places will be suspended until around the 29th, when they will resume sailing.

Foch Road, Rue Amiral Courbet

Tenants Demand Rent Reduction Dispute

Landlord Has Asked the Court to Attach

Tenants Provide Guarantee to Lift the Seizure

There are seventy or eighty houses on Foch Road, Rue Amiral Courbet, which is adjacent to the French Concession and the British Concession. The land was rented by Shen Shumei, the Chinese comprador of the French Water and Electricity Company, to build houses. The tenants held a meeting last month and publicly elected representatives to send a letter requesting the landlord to reduce the rent by 40%. The landlord initially ignored it. Later, the tenants organized the Rue Amiral Courbet Branch of the Second District and Third Branch of the Citizens' Association to actively carry out the rent reduction movement. They also invited Mr. Wang and Mr. Lu to negotiate a rent reduction with Shen Shumei in order to resolve the matter peacefully. As a result, the landlord only agreed to reduce the rent by five yuan per room and made the payment of arrears a condition of the exchange. The tenants then held a plenary session at the Second Special District City Federation to discuss the matter. After the mediator Lu Jingshi reported on the process, the whole body believed that the rent reduction of five yuan was far from the requested 40% and could not be accepted. It was decided to temporarily stop paying the rent and deposit 60% of the monthly rent in the bank for safekeeping. Unexpectedly, the landlord learned of this and specially hired lawyer Ai Zhenlin to first provide a guarantee for the Xin Wanyuan Sauce Garden opened by Wang Nengzu, who served as the representative, and implemented the attachment. The Second Special District Court sent personnel to the premises yesterday afternoon, together with the litigation agent of the owner, to seal it up and recover the rent of 618 yuan. After receiving the news, the manager, Mr. Wang, immediately raised 618 yuan in cash, provided the court to lift the seizure, and also asked the tenant's agent lawyer, Chen Bingxing, to file a counterclaim with the court, claiming that the owner had damaged his business and demanded compensation for the loss. When the tenants heard the news, they became even more angry. In addition to continuing to carry out the rent reduction movement, they also organized a delegation, issued a declaration, and requested assistance from all walks of life to stop the landlord's illegal actions, so as not to affect the city's rent reduction movement.

City Ferry

Adding the Chuntong Line

Officially Opens Tomorrow

One Departure Every Seven Minutes

The City Ferry Chuntong Line, which is being planned by the City Public Utilities Bureau, is ready and has been scheduled to officially open on the 8th of this month. The planning process is recorded as follows:

The Spring River Wharf's Terrain The Spring River Wharf is in a straight line with Nanjing Road, about 400 meters (about 1,300 feet) from the Bund, which is equal to the Bund of Nanjing Road to Henan Road's throwing field, and the land price is dozens of times different. The shape of the Huangpu River, from the Five Horse Central Bund to the Lihong Bridge in Hongkou, is a circle, and the Spring River Wharf is located in the center of the circle, and its radius with the major streets is almost equal. It is connected to Pudong Avenue in the east, and telephones and lights are fully equipped. The New Spring River Wharf Built by City Ferry in Pudong

Water can be organized soon, and the land price is extremely low. Since City Ferry built a wharf here, there have been land developers who have gone to collect land and prepare to build houses. After the City Ferry opens, it will only take three minutes to directly reach the Bund of Nanjing Road. In the future, those who serve in the Bund area will want to move to the area, and the house prices will be lower than in any area in Puxi. Its development can be guaranteed.

City Ferry Equipment The place is commonly known as Lujiazui. Puxi is shallow, and the cost of building the wharf is several times higher than that of other cross-river ferry wharves. The office building is located next to the wharf to facilitate nearby command and management. The floating wharf is all made of steel with steel roofs. The first-class cabin panels dismantled from the Changdu ferry are used around it, and there are cabin doors to avoid wind and rain. Those waiting for the ship are no different from being at home. Entry and exit are separate, and the ticketing and inspection procedures are simple. The ship uses the City Ferry's latest No. 16 to operate. From 5 am to 8 pm, there is one departure every seven minutes. The ferry fare is five copper coins per passenger between 5 am and 7 am, and between 5 pm and 7 pm, and eight copper coins at other times. It is stable, convenient, and cheap, and it is a shallow blessing for the citizens.

The People's Ferry Suspends Operation The original People's Ferry in the area has outdated equipment. It takes no less than twenty or thirty minutes to cross the river if there is a slight wind and wave. The danger is even more so. It should have been eliminated long ago. It is said that the ferry users have voluntarily closed down.

Measures to Restrict Rickshaw Licensing

Shanghai French Concession Board of Directors Issued a Notice:

For the purpose of notice, the Board is aware that the traffic in the Concession is congested, and therefore, the Board of Directors adopted the policy of restricting public rickshaw vehicles implemented by the Public Concession Works Bureau at the regular meetings on March 6 and December 22, 1933, and the number of vehicle licenses for 1933 and 1934 is limited to 17,000. (The Public Concession only issued 10,000 vehicle licenses) The number of vehicle licenses applied for in the past has never exceeded the above-mentioned quota as of January 1933. Only 16,610 licenses were taken in January 1933, 16,624 in February, 16,789 in March, 16,906 in April, 16,955 in May, 16,574 in June, 16,757 in July, 16,786 in August, 16,856 in September, and 16,996 in October. Later, the number of applications for licenses slightly exceeded the limit, and the restriction measures set by the Board began to take effect. It has been decided that only those who hold old licenses will be issued new licenses according to the number of old licenses they hold. This method of exchanging licenses is the only fair way to protect the rights of vehicle owners. According to this standard, all requests can be satisfied. In order to avoid any disputes, the Board has decided to implement the registration method of public rickshaw owners in January 1934 and issue temporary registration certificates. The vehicle owners who hold this certificate can come to the Board to exchange it for a new vehicle license in January. According to the regulations of the Board, all public rickshaw vehicle licenses are not allowed to be transferred. Vehicle owners must not lend, transfer, or sell their licenses. If the number of vehicles prepared by the vehicle owner is reduced, they should immediately report it to the Board. This is hereby announced.

Shanghai National Products Company

The First Voice of the Women's National Products Year

Astonishing Statistics of Purchasing Power in January

The Shanghai National Products Company, located opposite the Hong Miao Temple on Nanjing Road, is the earliest established and most important stronghold for promoting national products on Nanjing Road. Its location is conveniently surrounded by strongholds for promoting foreign goods, which, according to common sense, makes competition difficult. The company, aware of this, specially established a design department in April of last year, appointing Mr. Ren Jinpin as the director. Mr. Ren, based on his "Operational Plan for Building National Products" written in 1930 and the principle of "Chinese People Buy National Products with Reason," carefully studied the various facts of the company and formulated a first plan for developing business. This plan began to be implemented on September 1st of last year, and a monthly standard total business target was set to observe the results of the plan, with a completion period of six months. It was found that from January to August of last year, the monthly business was lower than this standard by 14.66%. Since September, no month's business has failed to exceed the standard. Subsequently, due to the success of the first plan, the company prepared to trial a second plan from December of last year, which was earnestly implemented from January of this year. Before the implementation, it was jointly agreed with Mr. Lu Qisheng, the concurrent acting manager of the company, to aim to exceed the previously set standard by 150% in the monthly total business within six months as the goal of completing the second plan. Therefore, Mr. Lu and Mr. Ren invited the general manager, Mr. Qiu Zhihao, to gather all the staff on New Year's Eve last year, held a fun fair at the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, and encouraged all male and female staff to work hard to serve the Women's National Products Year with the slogan of promoting the Women's National Products Year. It is now known that the company's business in January of this year totaled more than 84.94% above the previously set standard, which is better than any month last year. According to common practice, this month was both the end of the lunar year and the weather was extremely cold, coupled with the economic impact of the war, the society showed a clear phenomenon of economic downturn, and various businesses were all facing a sharp decline due to the shrinking purchasing power. However, the company was uniquely able to create this abnormal achievement, which is enough to amaze people and shows the value of its efforts.

Impersonation

Negotiations regarding the name of Bingxun Shorthand

The Bingxun Shorthand School on Hainin Road in Shanghai, founded in 1927, has established a unique position in the academic world. Thanks to the inventor, Yang Bingxun, continuing to study diligently, his aspiration has finally been realized. Today, his students serve in various organizations in society, and the number of people writing to the school from various places for correspondence and face-to-face teaching is increasing daily. Unfortunately, the First Zhonghua Vocational Tutorial School in Shanghai thought that this practical new skill was a great opportunity. Without obtaining Mr. Yang's consent in advance, they included in their charter that the Bingxun shorthand method would be taught by experienced teachers to attract students. Mr. Yang believes that this kind of imitation is a lack of moral concept and is unreasonable. He has had serious negotiations with the school. It is now heard that the school has cancelled the subject and published an apology to Mr. Yang in the newspaper.

Sentencing for Trademark Forgery

Tang Lianji, a native of Ningbo living at No. 70 Xiangfen Lane in the Public Concession, who runs a broker business, took 28,000 counterfeit cardboard boxes with the trademark of the American merchant Every Ready Battery to the Zhenxin Printing Factory opened by Chen Honggao at No. 10 Xinle Lane, Puyang Bridge, in the French Concession for cutting on the 21st of last month. When he arrived at the entrance of the lane, he was discovered by Detective Lu Changsheng and others from the French Police Department. Tang was arrested and taken to the police station, and Chen Honggao, Li Xuan-san and Bai Zefang, employees of Luoyang Zhongxing Shenzhuang at No. 50, Lane 20, Tiantang Street, and Wang Xiajin, a broker from Zhenhua Lamp Shop at No. 32 Jixiang Street, were also arrested and sent to the Second Special District Court for public prosecution on charges of trademark forgery. Details have already been reported in previous newspapers. The interrogation has already been concluded. Yesterday, Judge Qiu Huan-ying sentenced Tang Lianji in the Eighth Criminal Court to two months' imprisonment and a fine of 60 yuan for jointly forging trademarks. Wang Xiajin and Chen Honggao were sentenced to one month's imprisonment and a fine of 30 yuan each for helping to forge trademarks. Li Xuan-san and Bai Zefang were each fined 50 yuan for committing fraud. The fines can be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two yuan per day. The number of days of detention before the judgment is determined shall be counted as two days of imprisonment or one day of fine for every day of detention. During the appeal period, only the three defendants Wang, Chen, and were detained in the detention center. The two defendants Li and Bai were allowed to post bail and wait for instructions.

Victim Injured and Came to Shanghai for Medical Treatment

Xu Xingen, a 35-year-old farmer from Xujiazhai Township, more than 20 miles from Qingpu County, was suddenly invaded by more than ten bandits at about 9 o'clock last night (the 4th). Establishment of the Joint Association

Factory Staff Bookkeeping Tutorial School

The Shanghai Machinery National Products Factory Joint Association yesterday notified its member factories as follows: "Esteemed sirs, the progress of a business depends on the availability of suitable talents. Now that business is evolving and changing with each passing day due to the evolution of science, the need for talent is the most important issue for entrepreneurs. In particular, the various accounting aspects of factories are complicated. If there are no applicable talents, it is difficult to understand the detailed figures accurately. In terms of accounting, the standard of calculation is lost early, and all plans are bound to fail. In view of the fact that member factories must have the pain of someone unsuitable for the job or a job unsuitable for the person, this association decided at the 22nd meeting of the 7th Standing Committee today to establish a factory staff bookkeeping tutorial school in the association's premises (and hire personnel from the Lixin Certified Public Accountants Office to provide training). This will allow staff members to take advantage of the tutorial opportunity to add service functions, enhance the knowledge of individual staff members, and enrich the content and develop the business due to the application of staff members, so that both are suitable for common use and both can be announced. In order to give preferential treatment to members, the fees are halved. All the detailed measures are detailed in the constitution. The date of commencement is set for February 20. Reports will be started from now until the eighteenth of the month.

Oil Cart Wharf Robbery Last Night

Police Officer Shot and Captured a Thief

Recovered a Portion of the Original Loot

A Handgun Was Found in the Garbage Can

Yan Baolin, a native of Ningbo, is nearly seventy years old. He is married to Cai, who is forty-five years old, and has a daughter named Xia Xiang, who is sixteen years old. Yan works as an old clerk in the Changhe Pig Shop on Youche Road in the South City. His family lives at No. 22 Youche Road, and their life is still sustainable. For some reason, he was noticed by bandits. At about 7:30 last night, Yan happened to be out and had not returned home. Cai was taking care of chores at home when four bandits suddenly came, speaking in the Jiangbei accent. Each of them had a handgun. When they entered the door, they closed the main door tightly and forbade any noise. Cai was stunned and allowed them to search the house. Unexpectedly, when the bandits entered, Yan's young daughter, Xia Xiang, happened to be standing outside the door. She witnessed the bandits breaking in and knew they were robbers. She ran to report to Police Officer Zheng Chen of Post No. 20 nearby. Upon hearing the report, Officer Zheng blew his whistle frantically. Liu Xueqing of Post No. 18, Wang Jiyuan of Post No. 24, and off-duty police officers Zhang Yinian, Liu Shucheng, and Liu Shutang all rushed to help with the arrest. Just as the bandits were coming out after having looted enough, the police officers chased them desperately. Unfortunately, because the area was very dark, the five bandits took the opportunity to escape. Only one bandit in a gray striped cloth shirt was chased closely by the police officers. He went west along Youche Lane to Ping'an Street, then west to Meiji Lane in Xibuhama and reached the Youche Wharf. Then he turned back to Ping'an Street and entered Tangguan Lane. He was held by the hands of off-duty police officers Liu Shutang and Wang Luoyuan near the south end of Yuanxing Lane and a portion of the original loot was taken back. The bandit surrendered. When he was chased along the way, Officer Zheng fired six shots, and the bandit returned two shots. Officer Liu fired one shot, and the bandit returned one shot. When the bandit was taken to the station, he was interrogated by the chief of the station, and it was learned that his name was Li Xueshu, 29 years old, from [missing information], living in a small boat on Baidu Bridge. He admitted without hesitation that he had conspired to rob. When asked where the handgun was discarded, he hesitated. Just as the interrogation was in progress, the police chief had already found the handgun in a garbage can at the south end of Youche Wharf. There were still two bullets in the chamber. The gun was a 6-inch Brown Lymm-style gun with serial number 8881.9. Among the original stolen goods recovered were a green velvet shirt, 16 yuan in banknotes, a piece of blue floral cloth, a child's schoolbag, and a piece of ham. The owner identified them as correct. After the interrogation by Chief Yi, he ordered that the bandit be temporarily detained and reported to the General Bureau for verification.

Unified Tax Clerk

Deng Darong Admits to Embezzlement and Misappropriation

The Facts Are Now Clear, Debate Begins Yesterday

Verdict Announced in Court on the 9th

Deng Darong, a native of Guangdong, was working as a clerk in the audit section of the First Section of the Zhejiang-Anhui Unified Tax Bureau on Chengdu Road. He was discovered by the bureau chief, Wang Zongzhu, for forging seals and embezzling a large amount of tax money, and ordered a strict investigation. However, it was the end of the Western calendar year at that time, and Deng Darong asked for leave to return to his hometown. Later, he learned that Deng was coming to Shanghai on the Asia Queen ship. The ship arrived at the port on January 6, and he immediately sent someone to wait at the dock. When the ship arrived, Deng was arrested and temporarily detained in the Municipal Public Security Bureau for investigation.

The definite number of Deng's embezzlement has been reported in this newspaper. After Bureau Chief Wang Zongzhu's detailed verification with various parties in recent days, it was learned that Deng had fraudulently withdrawn tax money, amounting to a total of 84,321 yuan and 21 cents. He then sent a letter to the Public Security Bureau, requesting that Deng Darong be transferred to the First Special District Court and sent to the detention center for custody. At the same time, he hired lawyer He Qingyun, along with evidence, to submit a statement to the First Special Court, accusing Deng Darong of violating Article 234 of the Criminal Law, forging the seal of Bureau Chief Wang Zongzhu, Article 363, fraudulently obtaining materials, and Article 366, breach of trust, etc.

In addition, a civil lawsuit was filed requesting a judgment to repay the embezzled tax money of 84,321 yuan and 21 cents. In the indictment, he recounted how the defendant used various means to design and fraudulently withdraw tax money, totaling more than 10,000 words. He also stated that he had found a stone seal with the seal script of the name "Zongzhu" privately engraved in the defendant's residence, as well as evidence such as the stub of the Central Bank's checkbook and a silver deposit book, and asked Deng strictly where the seals and other items came from. The defendant admitted that in April 1932, he privately engraved the bureau chief's name seal in advance because he needed money urgently at that time and planned to secretly withdraw tax money from the Central Bank. When filling out the check for the withdrawal, he secretly obtained the check receipt form in the checkbook and obtained a checkbook from the Central Bank

by deceiving them. He filled out two checks, used fake seals, and personally withdrew the tax money from the bank. After the defendant was arrested, he handed over 212 Shanghai banknotes and 750 Hong Kong banknotes, and it was found that the defendant had deposits of 13,001 yuan, 1 cent and 2 cents in the Shanghai, China, and Kenyee Banks under the name of Duaji, etc. However, it was feared that there was still concealment, and he should be ordered to confess truthfully, etc. The Special Court accepted the statement and summoned him from the detention center by Judge Liu Yugui to the Second Criminal Court at 2:30 yesterday afternoon. Because the plaintiff Wang Zongzhu did not arrive, his agent lawyer He Qingyun stood up and described the case in detail, and presented

various evidence, stating that the defendant's deposits in Kenyee Bank had not been withdrawn because they had not been through the court, so the court should order the bank not to allow others to withdraw these deposits. When questioned, the defendant Deng Darong stated that he entered the Unified Tax Bureau in May 1931 as a clerk in the audit section of the First Section, specializing in reviewing the tax money reported by various organs. All the money to be paid by various branches was collected by the local Central Bank on behalf of the Bureau, transferred to the Shanghai Head Office, and the bills were sent to the Unified Tax Bureau for my review. After the collection bills from various places were collected, I would fill out the checks, which would be signed and sealed by the bureau chief and sent to the Unified Tax Administration. He admitted without denial all the points of the plaintiff's accusation against the defendant for malpractice and

the amount of misappropriation. The fake seal of the bureau chief was privately engraved in Wangping Street in mid-April 1932 for a few cents. The checkbooks were also obtained by me from the bank in the name of the Unified Tax Bureau, totaling three books, two of which have been used. I filled out the amount of money, stamped it with the bureau chief's fake seal, and personally withdrew the money from the bank, etc. Judge Liu ruled that the facts of the case were clear and ordered the debate to begin, so the lawyers from both parties stood up and debated for a long time. The court ruled that the debate on the case was over, and the verdict would be announced on the 9th of this month, and the defendant was returned to custody.
