Correspondence

The Current Cigarette Tax Rates Are the Same for the Government and Chinese Merchants

A Request for Careful Reconsideration and Forwarding of Loss Claims

A Letter for Swift Governmental Improvement (Part 2) - Huang Ziping

The tax bureau's letter focused on three main points: (1) whether tax revenue is affected, (2) whether opinions within the industry are consistent, and (3) whether there are practical obstacles to implementation. I, Ziping, have discussed these points in detail and offer the following answers: (1) Whether tax revenue is affected: as mentioned before, the failure of the two-tier tax system lies in the tax reduction on high-grade cigarettes. Therefore, the revenue gained from increasing taxes on low-grade cigarettes must still compensate for the loss from reducing taxes on high-grade cigarettes. Although the burden on Chinese merchants is heavy, the government does not benefit, as British and American companies enjoy over 10 million yuan in annual tax reductions. If the idea of tax benefits for foreign interests is discarded, the tax rates on high and mid-grade cigarettes can be increased appropriately. Then, the benefits previously enjoyed annually by British and American companies due to tax reductions would be returned to the government, leading to an increase in tax revenue. How can it be said that tax revenue is affected? (2) Whether opinions within the industry are consistent: people's views differ as much as their faces. Complete consensus within the industry is practically impossible. To illustrate, many Chinese people do not support the establishment of Manchukuo, yet collaborators like Zheng Xiaoxu and Shi Yousan are also Chinese. The world cannot conclude from Zheng and Shi's collaboration that Chinese people are inconsistent and should recognize Manchukuo. Therefore, when discussing cigarette tax rates, one should only ask whether they align with the principles of fairness and whether they harm domestic agriculture, industry, and commerce, not whether industry opinions are consistent. If a tax rate aligns with fairness and does not harm domestic industries, it should be adopted; otherwise, it should be abolished. Industry consensus is not crucial. If consensus is required, the current two-tier tax system is already opposed by 24 Shanghai companies and the general public, with cigarette companies in Hebei, Shandong, Shanxi, and Henan provinces also protesting. It should have been abolished long ago. Therefore, this point does not require further discussion. (3) Whether there are practical obstacles to implementation: this likely considers the opposition of British and American companies. However, this is not a significant concern. Before the establishment of the National Government, customs duties were limited to a 5% ad valorem rate. After customs autonomy, this unequal treaty was broken. Consolidated taxes are domestic taxes, and even during the diplomatic failures of the late Qing Dynasty, domestic taxes were never interfered with by foreigners. China is a sovereign nation, and no matter how powerful foreign merchants are, they cannot interfere with domestic taxes. Even the agreements between the tax bureau and British and American companies only state that they should receive the same treatment as Chinese factories, with no preferential clauses. If a fair tax rate is set, applying an ad valorem tax consistently to both Chinese and foreign companies, there is no need to worry about foreign companies making excuses. The above points were thoroughly researched and discussed by Ziping and others, with unanimous agreement. As the tax bureau is currently seeking the opinions of cigarette merchants and the general assembly is studying tax rates, it is appropriate to prepare a written opinion and submit it to the general assembly. We hope for careful reconsideration and a reply to the tax bureau, striving to improve the tax rate as soon as possible, relieving the Chinese merchants of their plight. The industry would be deeply grateful. Respectfully submitted to the general assembly of the Shanghai Chinese Cigarette Manufacturers Association by Huang Ziping, representative of the People's Public Company.

Appendix: Original Letter from the Ministry of Finance's Tax Bureau to the Trade Association: We are writing to inform you that twenty-four cigarette companies, including the People's Public Company, have jointly submitted a petition stating that the current cigarette tax rates unfairly treat Chinese and foreign companies and request a prompt revision of the tax brackets for relief. Regarding the second-tier cigarette price, this bureau agreed to your association's request to raise the limit to 300 yuan to avoid restricting business. If the proposed tax bracket changes do not affect national tax revenue, if the entire industry agrees, and if there are no practical obstacles to implementation, this bureau will forward the request for instructions. Enclosed is a copy of the original petition for your reference. Please study it carefully, discuss it properly, and reply with your opinions. Respectfully addressed to the Shanghai Chinese Cigarette Manufacturers Association.

Q&A on Learning

On Learning Languages (Part 2)

From Mr. Cheng's letter, we believe there are two important points that need to be discussed with Mr. Cheng: First, should one read classical Chinese when learning the language? Second, can learning a language be effective solely through reading and studying texts?

Indeed, without language, we cannot express our own thoughts or understand those of others. However, the use of language is still just a tool—a tool for thought. Therefore, the purpose of learning a language is to make the use of the medium for communicating thoughts more flexible, which is what Mr. Cheng hopes for.

There is a difference between "language" and "writing." What is indispensable for the medium of communicating thoughts is not "writing" but "language," because there are many places where there is only "language" but no "writing," yet thought still exists. (See Chen Wangdao's "Some Questions About Literature" in the inaugural issue of Literature Magazine. However, Chen discusses the relationship between "language," "writing," and literature. We are extending his argument to generally discuss "thought.")

Writing emerged after language, but writing must be consistent with language. If it is not consistent, then such writing is definitely not a living language and is bound to be unintelligible. Because we usually think about things in the language we are familiar with, if we see a friend going somewhere and want to ask where they are going, the question that comes to mind is "Where are you going?" But if we are not asking verbally but using a letter—that is, writing—if we want to use "classical language" at this time, then we must translate this question into something like "Whither do you go?" From this, we can know that if "writing" and "language" are not consistent, then turning thought into writing must go through three steps: thought—the language of the time—the ancient language. This means that if we use classical Chinese, the communication of thought requires an extra step: we must translate the common language we think in into the ancient language, unable to directly write on paper the language we are thinking in. Those who are proficient in classical Chinese naturally do not need to go through such cumbersome procedures; they have learned the "ancient language" so well that they can think in the ancient language. But how much effort does their learning require! So, in the past, after learning everyday language, people did not just write but had to learn the ancient language as well. In reality, it seems like learning two languages. But if vernacular Chinese is used, this difficulty probably would not arise. Because what we want to say can be immediately written on paper. From a learning perspective, this is the first reason why we do not advocate reading classical Chinese.

Now, many people say that we certainly advocate using vernacular Chinese, but learning vernacular Chinese must start from reading classical Chinese. Don't you see that many people who write vernacular Chinese extremely well have a foundation in classical Chinese? This is a specious view. What are we learning when we learn classical Chinese now? Are we learning to write classical Chinese? Of course not. Are we gaining some writing skills from classical Chinese? This is also nonsense. Yao Nai believed that what one should learn from classical Chinese is nothing more than "structure, tone, spirit, reason, and taste." Are we now learning "structure and tone"? Since we are not writing classical Chinese, what is the use of learning this "structure and tone" that can only be applied to classical Chinese? Since modern grammar and structure are different from classical Chinese, what is the use of learning the tone of classical Chinese? There is also no need to learn the "spirit, reason, and taste" of classical Chinese. "Spirit, reason, and taste" are not exclusive to classical Chinese; our modern Chinese also has spirit, reason, and taste. Why insist on learning and studying them from classical Chinese? In short, the beautiful qualities of literature, such as what Yao Nai called vigor and tenderness, are what all articles should have. Classical Chinese has them, English also has them, French also has them. If we study with this purpose, then what is the difference between studying classical Chinese and studying French?

Another group of people, though not making the above argument, advises people to read ancient books and classical Chinese such as "Zhuangzi" and "Wen Xuan" to increase the vocabulary of beginners. This is also a prescription that does not fit the symptoms. Such arguments have been published extensively in this newspaper's "Free Discussions" section last year, and readers can refer to them for themselves to see the pros and cons. No need to repeat them. Now, let's point out the shortcomings of this argument. It is indeed necessary to expand the vocabulary of students at present, but not by looking in ancient books. In this respect, students should diligently consult dictionaries and use the living vocabulary in them. At the same time, foreign words, newly coined scientific terms, and terms that are trending in social life but have not yet "become established" should be added to expand the modern, living vocabulary. This is the real way out. The characters in Zhuangzi and Wen Xuan do have a lot that ordinary people do not recognize now, but even if these characters are recognized, what use are they in language and writing? Therefore, from the perspective of training writing skills, we also do not need to read classical Chinese, but only to be able to express my meaning as desired. Learning classical Chinese is absolutely unnecessary. (To be continued)

Letters to the Editor

To the Editor: We are writing regarding a news item in your newspaper's local news section on February 6th, reporting that the Jiangjing vessel of the Dada Company returned to Shanghai yesterday and (omitting the beginning) that the main perpetrators of the incident, Cai Yunsheng (from Wuling), Zou Caigao (from Yancheng), Zhang Yucun, and Liu Guangcheng, were handed over to the authorities and that a business card and main certificate of Wang Zemin, a shareholder in the Xiaobao District Nitratin Mine, were found on them. The Xiaobao Sub-Bureau's transport and sale of nitrate mines is limited to Xiaobao territory and does not extend to other areas. Zhang Yucun and his accomplices are suspected of being private nitrate traffickers who are using this method to avoid searches en route. The incident of smuggling and causing trouble not only harms the bureau's reputation but also violates laws and regulations. We are therefore writing this letter to clarify this matter, hoping that you will publish it in the letters to the editor column to clarify the truth and avoid confusion. Sincerely, Wang Zhixiang, Director of the Xiaobao Special District Nitrate Mine Sub-Bureau, February 6th.

To the Editor: I am writing on behalf of Ms. Zheng Yu Jingxiu, who stated that she read the news report in your newspaper's local news section on February 6th about the lawsuit between the brother and wife of the deceased Zheng Mingshan. The report stated that the Rongyang Work Socks Factory was founded by the brothers Zheng Fengshan and Zheng Mingshan, which is not entirely accurate. Both factories were solely founded by the late Mingshan before changing ownership to a partnership. Zheng Fengshan was only given a portion of shares due to the late Mingshan’s brotherly affection. Therefore, we have been specifically commissioned to write this letter to request a correction to reflect these facts. We thank you sincerely for your assistance. Sincerely, Lawyers Chen Tingrui and Sun Zuji, February 6th.

Random Thoughts

Protecting Children is Our Responsibility

— Hu Chenzhou

That is truly good news for the children of China! Someone has proposed, "Protecting children is our responsibility!" Slogans that are colorful and green are plastered on the streets, walls and telegraph poles, and it has been decided that this year will be "Children's Year".

"Children's Year"! This reminds me of my childhood! I--no, not just me alone, but most of us--lived a dark, hungry, and dependent childhood. In those days, our lives belonged to our adults, and we were suppressed by them. Only a few children had stable, fulfilling and bright lives filled with love and games.

This phenomenon continues and continues::: until this year, which is "Children's Year"; "Protecting Children is Our Responsibility"! It will soon cease to exist (?). I think.

Our current task is to protect working children! Those in hereditary wealthy and educated families do not need our protection.

Protecting working children: abolish child labor (those girls working in the cotton mills who are scalded with hot water on their heads and bodies if they are slightly inattentive at work, so that large and small blisters rise up, and they are ordered not to cry! Those students in shops who are routinely subjected to torture by the shop owners: beatings, branding, ::: those eldest daughters in mansions who are often scolded and beaten:::). Strictly prohibit the sale of children (those evil traffickers who kidnap children from Shanghai, Ningbo, etc., and take them to Xiamen and Shantou to sell them to those with money! Here, whoever has the most maidservants is the richest! The situation is like the attitude of some capitalists towards their slaves after the abolition of slavery in the United States...:::::::). Relieving suffering children (those who pick up garbage all the time, summer or winter, sunny or rainy days, suffering from urban pallor,:::::)

Seeking Happiness in Death and Showing Off in Death

— Zhu Renyi

"Death" is always a bit terrifying to the living. However, strangely enough, some people are now seeking happiness at the head of the word "death". Perhaps all the joys of the world have been exhausted, but people are determined to find new and strange joys to be happy about, so they have found death. What an interesting farce this is!

The people of the twentieth century have also had enough of showing off, from the air to the sea, from the battlefield to the ballroom, from going abroad to going to the countryside, from revolution to chanting Buddha: finally, they have turned to the head of the word "death". It is also showing off to die. What another interesting farce!

Just open any major newspaper and you will always find news of death published. Here are two examples:

A young couple died together because they were not free to love. Their method was to draw two flower lines from the electric light to the bed, tying each to one leg, and then turning the machine button to electrocute themselves.

There was also a person who died by first buying a coffin, suspending it in the air, opening a hole at the bottom, and placing a coal stove on the ground, aiming at the hole, and burning coal; then he climbed into the coffin, moved the lid, and let the coal gas poison him to death.

This is looking for fun in death!

A certain monk studied abroad in a certain country when he was young and obtained a doctoral degree. After returning to China, he successively held important military and political positions. Later, after seeing through the world, he concentrated on cultivating and chanting scriptures; he will now die in the next month. So, he summoned countless believers.

A certain gentleman lost his love in the love scene, owed a huge debt, and could no longer maintain his life. He was determined to "die" in frustration, and wrote a letter of suicide note, the general idea being: the people of the country are willing to degenerate, the violent sun is invading, and they are not resisting. I cannot bear to witness the demise of the motherland, so I committed suicide in order to awaken my compatriots to rise up and save the country together. So, the newspaper touted it loudly, and everyone praised it!

This is called showing off in death!

The living want to seek the happiness of dying and show off the limelight of dying. This is far-sighted! Don't you see...

The Voice of the City

— Yixiao

Shanghai, a large city, always evokes in those who have never been there the illusion of a "great, mysterious den of consumption". As soon as you step into this metropolis of Shanghai, you will feel that it is hiding some sadness, depravity, pain, ... constant cries!

Sleeping in bed in the early morning, you will hear:

"Little cabbage... green vegetables, turnips..."

This sound is always sad and earnest: it will give you a burst of discomfort invisibly, and a moment later another burst:

"Shenbao, News, Times, Current Affairs News!

..." rough sound.

At noon, the sounds gradually become complex, sad and mournful: heavy and light: sandy and broken, boiling on the streets and alleys. The kind of life shouting, you really can't let your brain settle down for a moment, even if you walk on the street for a walk, those beggars, sick old beggars, will follow behind you:

"Sir, young master... do something good! ..." a burst of shouting. Is it a little quieter at night? Indeed, it is indeed a little quieter--but soon that kind of cry will move your heartstrings again in the quiet night alley:

"Olives... sandalwood olives, buy olives..." This sound is always clear, tactful, more natural than any music, and soon you hear:

Shell... The hissing sound made by breaking bamboo, followed by: "Be careful of fire! ..." short and quick sand sounds, from far to near, from near to far...

Late at night, I was awakened by a sound again, and I heard sparsely:

"Ham dumplings,..."

"Pork fat, rice, five-spice tea eggs..."

I have lived in Shanghai for ten years, and I always wake up sadly, sleep sadly, and wake up sadly in the middle of the night!

"The voice of the city, the voice of the city! ..." When will you disappear from my ears?

Cleanliness and Squalor

— 19

Recently, I met an old friend whom I hadn’t seen in years. During the height of our drunken conversation, he spoke at length about cleanliness and squalor, causing my face to flush with shame, because I am also Chinese.

My friend lives on a certain road in Hongkou, Shanghai. Besides the Chinese, there are also many Japanese among his neighbors. He told me, "If you want to know which house in this area is occupied by Chinese, you only need to look at whether there is a pile of garbage at the back door." This statement alone made me, as a Chinese person, feel quite uncomfortable. He continued, "If you take a stroll down a lane, you will see that the glass windows of many houses are covered in dust, as if the house has been empty for a long time; you can be sure that these households are also Chinese. Furthermore, you can also tell the nationality of the occupants from the gaps in the curtains or the lampshades."

Following this, my friend spoke about bathing, something he does every day. According to him, the women of a certain large commercial port in a province renowned as a land of culture and civilization do not bathe year after year; moreover, they dare not even wash their lower parts. Because if the act of washing the lower parts becomes known, the washer will be unjustly accused of "prostitution." Who would want to bear such a terrible reputation? Therefore, they have no choice but to let their lower parts become more and more squalid day by day. After my friend finished speaking, he repeatedly shook his head in disapproval.

He also told me, "A Westerner, after traveling all over East Asia, including Japan, Korea, and China, expressed his feelings to others, roughly saying: Westerners are clean both inside and out, Japanese are squalid on the outside but clean on the inside, Koreans are clean on the outside but squalid on the inside, but only the Chinese are squalid both inside and out." The terms "inside" and "outside" refer to the body and clothing, respectively. Being "squalid on the inside" is naturally related to bathing.

Finally, my friend said to me, "From cleanliness and squalor, one can see the national character of a country." After listening to these words, my face turned red, and I could only stare blankly and think.

Four Company Commanders of the Northeast

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 24

Drinking and sharing food, wild revelry contains parting tears

Picking up the lamp to warm dreams, low singing passes the long night

Old Zhao stopped stroking his beard, puffed out his chest, and raised his voice, saying: "You've been a soldier for so long, how can you still be so sentimental? You know that these old bones of mine are very healthy. With me taking care of your mother-in-law and your wife, they will be even more comfortable than before. You don't need to worry about any of this, just go be a good company commander. Heroes are made of flesh and blood, and great things are also done by people, there are no immortals descending to help the people." At this point, he lowered his voice slightly and said: "Women's hearts are always soft, you have to put on an indifferent appearance to lift their spirits. If you yourself are so sad and gloomy, and they don't understand the things in the military camp, wouldn't they be even more anxious?" Zi Qiang smiled and said: "I'm not particularly anxious, it's just that I see that she seems to be very sad, and I don't know what to say to comfort her." Old Zhao said: "That's nonsense. When people are about to part, they are always sad. You should only use kind words to comfort her, saying that you will meet again soon, that's the right thing to do. If you are the same as her, wouldn't it be even harder to part?" These are just a few words from me, listen carefully and think about them." After Old Zhao finished speaking, he hurriedly returned to his own room, leaving Zi Qiang standing alone in the main room. He originally thought of going to the front yard to comfort his mother-in-law a few words. However, he didn't have that kind of courage, took a few steps forward, and then walked back again. He stood in the main room for a long time, afraid that his father would come out and lecture him, so he simply turned around and retreated into the bridal chamber. He sat alone on a chair, propping his head with his hands on the edge of the table. He sat there silently, not knowing how much time had passed, only hearing heavy footsteps as someone came in. He immediately straightened up and saw Gui Zhi walking into the room, smiling and skipping. Judging by her appearance, she was naturally extremely happy. (240)

Miscellaneous Notes on Suzhou Tea Affairs

— Zhang Yuming

(1) Tea Production in China. The most famous tea-producing areas include "Lu'an" in Anhui and "Wuyi" in Fujian. However, people rarely notice that "Dongting East Mountain" and "West Mountain" in Suzhou also produce excellent teas, known as "Biluochun." "Dengwei Mountain" in Guangfu also produces the so-called "Benshan Yuqian." The annual output of these two types of tea is about six to seven hundred dan. "Biluochun" tea accounts for about six or seven tenths of this amount and is a famous tea. Locals pick it and sell it to tea merchants, and the price is only about seven or eight jiao per catty, which can be considered extremely cheap. After being roasted, it is brewed with clear spring water, and the fragrance is pure and lasting, unlike ordinary teas. According to the traditions of Lu Yu and Lu Tong's friends, the "Biluochun" tea produced in Suzhou is no less fragrant, pure, and mellow than the so-called "Shifeng" and "Tieguanyin" famous teas.

(2) Tea Merchants Because Suzhou produces tea, the tea industry naturally occupies an important position in Suzhou's commerce. According to statistics, there are more than forty large-scale "tea firms," "tea warehouses," and "tea shops" in Suzhou. Among them, the most historic and financially strong are "Wu Xunji," "Bao Derun," "Wu Shimei," "Wang Ruiyu," and "Chou Zhenlong." "Wu Xunji's" tea is mostly sold in Shandong Province, such as in "Jining" and "Jinan." "Bao Derun's" products are best-selling in "Yizhou" and other places. "Wang Ruiyu" has an affiliated tasting room and relies on publicity, so it can also dominate the tea industry in Suzhou. "Chou Zhenlong's" tea also has considerable influence in the Suzhou market. The annual turnover of the above tea merchants can exceed 200,000 yuan.

(3) Scented Tea Suzhou's Tiger Hill, famous at home and abroad, has residents who mostly cultivate flowers and trees. "Citrus aurantium" is a specialty of the Tiger Hill scenic area. Citrus aurantium buds can be baked and used to make tea. If they are brewed with tea, they can enhance the flavor of the tea, making it rich and fragrant. Visitors who come to Tiger Hill know the great reputation of "Citrus aurantium tea." This kind of scented tea is sold to other places in large quantities every year, and Europeans and Americans especially like to buy it as a gift.

(4) Teahouses There are many teahouses in Suzhou. The more famous ones in the city include "Wu Yuan," "Pengying," "Sanwanchang," and "Wang Ruiyu." Outside the city, there are also "Changan" and "Fuan" teahouses. However, strangely, the tea drinkers have not been subjected to any formal restrictions, but they are very clearly divided automatically. For example, the customers of Wang Ruiyu's teahouse are mostly newspaper reporters and elementary school teachers. The customers of Wu Yuan's "Aizhu Ju" and "Huayu Lou" are mostly members of the Wu-area bourgeoisie. Outside the city, the "Fuan" and "Changan" teahouses attract merchants of all sizes and are veritable de facto exchanges in Suzhou that are divided into categories. In addition, the "East Pavilion" and "West Pavilion" of Suzhou Park are very prosperous in the hot summer months. Because the modern girls of Gusu have no dance halls or swimming pools to enjoy themselves, they often drink tea in the park to enjoy the cool breeze. A group of lecherous young men also often use drinking tea as a pretext to pursue their romantic endeavors. However, now that autumn has ended and winter has arrived, that group of customers has already changed course, and the "East Pavilion" and "West Pavilion" are hibernating like insects, waiting for the hot summer to come again to resume their activities. In addition, every year during the Lunar New Year, the Suzhou people who value auspiciousness like to go to "Changan" and "Fuan" in droves to drink tea. They believe that drinking "Changan" tea at the beginning of the year can bring lasting joy and peace, and going to Fuan Teahouse can bring blessings, health, and well-being. If the facts are as people wish, our government officials should also be invited to visit Suzhou's "Changan" and "Fuan" to taste the auspicious tea. Wouldn't that make our China prosperous and peaceful?

(5) Tea Talks There is a group of heroes who eat the sun during the day and eat the moon at night. They also learn from the politicians to establish factions and look down on all sides. If there are disputes, they are accustomed to using teahouses as places to comment on right and wrong. When they cannot reach an agreement, they may suddenly engage in hand-to-hand combat. This trend of "tea talks" is now rarely seen. Perhaps they have embraced pacifism and realized that they should no longer kill each other. As a result, the owners of Suzhou teahouses have reduced many unwarranted disasters!

Education News

Other Locations

Self-Funded Students Studying Abroad

Must Comply with Ministry Regulations

-Otherwise, Study Abroad Qualifications Will Not Be Recognized-

Students Studying in Japan Should Pay More Attention

(Nanjing, 6th) The Ministry of Education has issued an order to various departments stating: After reviewing the regulations, self-funded students studying abroad must have qualifications that meet the standards set by the Ministry's regulations for studying abroad, and their study abroad expenses must ensure their behavior. A study abroad certificate will be issued upon approval by the Ministry. After arriving in the country of study, the study abroad certificate must be submitted to the study abroad management agency in the country within two weeks for verification and registration. Recently, the Supervision Office for Students Studying in Japan reported that some self-funded students studying in Japan have gone abroad without a study abroad certificate, or have not registered with the office after obtaining a study abroad certificate. Recently, there have been cases where people have been detained upon arrival in Japan for lacking study abroad documents, or sent back to their country of origin by the original ship. This is detrimental to the national image. We sincerely request that measures be taken to prevent this situation. After investigation, it has been found that most of these students without study abroad certificates have either had their applications rejected by the Ministry due to unqualified qualifications or insufficient study abroad expenses, or intend to avoid the law and hope to obtain a study abroad certificate after going abroad. The Ministry has already strictly stipulated that the study abroad qualifications and academic qualifications of these students will not be recognized. Therefore, the Ministry hereby orders the department to earnestly guide the students in the affiliated schools who intend to study in Japan at their own expense, and ensure that they apply for a study abroad certificate before going abroad in accordance with the regulations, and register with the Supervision Office for Students Studying in Japan after going abroad, so as to respect the law and avoid abuses.

Current State of Education in Hankou City

A Total of 158 Public and Private Schools

Funding Is Extremely Difficult, and Existing Problems Need to Be Eliminated

Primary Education Is Underdeveloped, and 50,000 Children Are Out of School

Hankou Correspondence: Education in Hankou City has always been underdeveloped. Illiteracy accounts for more than eight tenths of the total population. There are only 158 public and private schools in total, and funding is difficult, with many existing problems. Expansion and rectification are truly urgent. According to Mayor Wu Guozhen's public statement, the city's educational institutions are divided into middle schools, primary schools, kindergartens, vocational schools, public education centers, and public libraries based on level, and based on nature, they are divided into (1) Municipal: one male middle school, one female middle school, one vocational school, ten complete primary schools, fifty junior primary middle schools, one public education center, and one public library. (2) Semi-public and semi-private: nineteen schools for children of industrial and commercial workers. (3) Private: fourteen middle schools and sixty-two primary schools. The content is roughly as follows:

Situation of Municipal Schools

The situation of municipal schools is the most complicated. (1) There is the issue of factions. In the past, each school had factions, and it was not easy to replace principals and teachers, even if they were incompetent, otherwise it would cause a disturbance. After the city government decided to correct this situation, the principals and teachers of each school must first apply to the city government for registration. After registration, the qualifications review committee will review and determine whether they are eligible to be employed. However, the abuses of party affiliation and favoritism have not been completely eliminated. Later, it was stipulated that the principal has no power to completely replace teachers. If a teacher is incompetent, the city government must be requested to investigate, and the successor must still be selected from among those who are registered and qualified. This implicitly provides teachers with protection, and the abuse of control can be slightly reduced. (2) There is the issue of funding. After the provincial government vigorously reduced funding, the funding for municipal schools has not been in arrears. However, the arrears for the first, second, third, seventh, eighth, and ninth months of the 21st year are difficult to repay. The internal funding of each school has already been handled by the principal, who is like a bureaucrat. Each principal can obtain hundreds of yuan in extra income. The city government is now organizing a "Permanent Goods Accounting" and establishing a "Purchasing Committee" to implement public funding in order to eliminate this abuse. (3) There is the issue of school buildings. The school buildings are either borrowed or forcibly occupied, and most are not suitable, which has a great impact. The city government plans to issue 400,000 yuan in treasury bonds to provide sufficient funds for the construction of school buildings. It is estimated that each primary school student will be charged one yuan, each middle school student will be charged one yuan and five jiao, and kindergarten students will not be charged. The school building fund management committee will be in charge of managing the funds. This plan has been submitted to the provincial government for transfer to the Ministry of Finance.

Situation of Private Schools

Although there are fourteen middle schools and sixty-two primary schools in private schools, most of them have simple equipment and unstable funding, and there are especially many with insufficient funds. Although the city government cannot supervise and improve teaching, it cannot solve the funding problem. It is now planned to provide some subsidies in the next semester, but it is unknown whether this can be realized.

Situation of Industrial and Commercial Schools

There are nineteen schools for children of industrial and commercial workers. The schools are run by the city government, and the funding is raised by industrial and commercial enterprises, so they are called semi-public and semi-private. The donors can form a "Funding Management Committee" and can also elect the principal. The managers are also not immune to the abuses of control or embezzlement. Now, a "Funding Supervision Office" has been established to formulate annual budget estimates and sort out the situation, which has been effective. The schools for children of the cart and ferry industries have all expanded their classes.

Problem of Children Out of School

In addition to the difficulty of funding and many existing problems, there is also a serious problem that has not been resolved for a long time, namely the problem of children out of school. At present, the city has more than 80,000 school-age children, but the existing public, private, and semi-public and semi-private schools can only accommodate 30,000 people. The remaining 50,000 children have no books to read. Even to enroll, each student must have a letter of recommendation from a military or political person, otherwise they will inevitably be turned away. Although it is ridiculous to view the school as an institution, it is also unavoidable. (February 2nd)

Jiangning

Development of Education in the Experimental County

Since Jiangning was changed to an autonomous experimental county, thanks to the hard work of County Magistrate Mei Siping and Education Section Chief Wang Guobin, the original 95 primary schools have been expanded to more than 195 primary schools in the county. It will not be long before more than 100 schools can be added, which is a new record in all counties in Jiangsu Province. It is said that the reason why it can develop so rapidly is that the county government authorities plan well, open the city and publicize it, cooperate with the county people, and encourage people in various townships to automatically set up township-run primary schools. The government provides appropriate guidance and subsidies, so many township-run primary schools have been established in the past six months. Local people are happy to support local education with local money. After the winter vacation, the county plans to promote more than ten primary schools, and six or seven schools have been added one after another. In order to popularize compulsory education, on the one hand, teachers are trained to meet the needs, and on the other hand, in order to seek advancement and meet the needs of modern rural society, Jiangning Primary School Teachers' Rotating Training Institute is opened to increase the necessary knowledge and skills about rural society. The staff, students, and school workers of the institute share the same hardships and develop the habit of diligence and hard work. The first and second phases of the institute enroll primary school teachers who are not currently employed in the institute for training (the first phase has just graduated, and the second phase is being recruited, and will start in March). After graduation, they will be sent to various schools to replace current teachers to make up the institute, and then rotate every three months to graduate, that is, continue to rotate, and all primary school teachers in the county can supplement their necessary knowledge and skills about rural society. The county feels that there is a lack of primary school teachers. In addition, a township-run primary school teacher training class is attached to the rotating training institute, enrolling 50 students, with a graduation period of six months. It is currently recruiting students and will start in March. The county provides subsidies to encourage primary schools in various districts and townships and to ensure that the primary schools in various townships have sufficient funds. The subsidy method is divided into five types (the maximum subsidy is 180 yuan per grade per year, and the minimum is 60 yuan), depending on the performance of the school and the amount of funds that the township itself can raise, as well as the grade of subsidies issued, etc.

Former Northeast Education Association President Wang Huayi

Talks About Education in the Northeast

Northeast Academy Now Changed to Northeast Middle School

Kong Xiangxi and Zhang Xueliang Both Agreed to Subsidize

Wang Huayi, the former president of the Northeast Education Association, came to Shanghai from Peiping some time ago specifically because of the funding problem of the Northeast Middle School in Peiping to meet with Finance Minister Kong Xiangxi and Zhang Xueliang, etc. and has had good results. A reporter from the Xin Sheng News Agency met with Mr. Wang at his residence yesterday, according to his conversation about the situation of education in the Northeast as follows:

Students Entering the Pass

According to Mr. Wang, since the Northeast was lost after the September 18th Incident, at that time, I was the Chairman of the Shenyang Education Association. I then organized a diplomatic association dedicated to resisting Japan. This caused deep jealousy from the Japanese. On the day after September 18th, both associations were sealed off. I also temporarily took refuge in Peiping. Later, the Japanese ordered the closure of all secondary schools and above in the Northeast and prohibited them from opening, in order to implement their cultural aggression. All primary schools used the Japanese as their spiritual guide. Therefore, middle school students flocked to within the Pass. Initially, I first established a Northeast College in Peiping, which was later renamed Northeast Middle School. I submitted it to the Ministry of Education for record. Currently, there are over one thousand middle school students and about eight hundred primary school students.

Implementing Military Affairs

In terms of teaching, we try to avoid unimportant courses and completely eliminate courses such as drawing, crafts, and singing. We added military education. We take drills and shooting very seriously every day. Apart from this, we pay attention to chemistry, mathematics, industry, and other subjects. In the past two years, graduates applying for further education, such as when applying to the Central Military Academy, twenty-four were admitted, and the first place was a student from Northeast Middle School. Those who applied to universities such as Peking University were all admitted. Some who sought employment, several students who studied papermaking, have also taken positions in Peiping paper mills.

School Funding

As for school funding, initially, we only solicited clothing and food from all parties, but this was not a long-term solution. Therefore, before Deputy Commander Zhang (Xueliang) went abroad, I requested assistance from Zhang Shinan. Zhang was also very concerned and contributed private funds as school funding once. Later, when Minister Song (Ziwent) went to Rehe, I paid a visit to request a subsidy plan. Song immediately agreed to find a way to allocate funds. However, Song then went abroad, and the matter was shelved again. With the assistance of various parties, the central government allocated funds from financial institutions in North China once, but it was still far from enough. The middle and primary school sections need 20,000 yuan for the middle school section and 8,000 yuan for the primary school section. After Song returned to China, he promised to allocate funds according to the plan, but it was not fulfilled due to his resignation.

Meeting Kong and Zhang

This time I came to Shanghai, I have met with Minister Kong and Committee Member Zhang (Xueliang) successively. Both of them promised to find ways to allocate funds for Northeast Middle School. Minister Kong, in particular, is very familiar with the situation of our school and is especially concerned.

Saving People's Hearts

He continued that the Japanese are now in the Northeast, still busy with politics and military affairs, so they have no time to take care of education. According to those who have left the Northeast, they have now used Chinese traitors to form an editorial committee to revise all books published by Commercial Press, Chung Hwa Book Company, and The World Book Company within the Pass. All historical content is deleted, leaving only irrelevant content, while gradually adding Japanese history and geography. Therefore, it is predicted that there will be further actions in the future. However, my feeling is that those who are puppets of the Japanese in the Northeast are all from Jinzhou. The reason is that Jinzhou has been influenced by Japan for decades, leading them to recognize the enemy as their father. At the same time, the recent strategy of the Japanese is that political and military affairs may only oppress temporarily or intimidate only for a short time. Therefore, their new policy has changed to a plan of attacking hearts as the priority. Therefore, we deeply feel that if we want to recover our territory, our military strength is far behind. We can only devote our efforts to education, so that our compatriots in the Northeast will not forget their ancestors. Then, whether it is thirty or forty years later, there will eventually be a day of recovery. Otherwise, nothing is more tragic than the death of the heart, and we are truly terrified.

China Educational Reconstruction Society

Actively Implementing Productive Education

Co-operating with Huangdu Rural Teachers School to Run a Chicken Farm

And Preparing to Hold a Chicken Raising Work-Study Class

The China Educational Reconstruction Society is organized by Sun Kangzeng, Xi Yangzhi, Cheng Kuanzheng, Zhang Zhonghuan and others in the educational field, with the aim of promoting the production of education. Later, the Society felt that the Chinese countryside was increasingly bankrupt, so last year it co-operated with Huangdu Rural Teachers School to run Huangdu Chicken Farm, in order to improve rural sideline occupations and practice productive education. It has hundreds of laying hens, and everything is managed according to scientific methods. It also hired experts as technicians for the farm. Therefore, the chickens are all strong and lovely. The Society is now preparing to hold a chicken raising work-study class and test raising Chinese chickens, in order to promote the chicken raising industry in nearby rural areas and increase farmers' production.

Municipal Primary and Secondary Schools

Deadline for Reporting Teacher Changes

The Municipal Education Bureau Issued Instructions to All Schools Yesterday

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau issued instructions to municipal primary and secondary schools yesterday, stating: "It has been found that the regulations for the appointment and dismissal of teachers in municipal secondary schools were revised and promulgated in September of the 22nd year and published in the 209th issue of the Education Weekly. The regulations for the appointment and dismissal of teachers in municipal primary schools were also revised in July of the 22nd year and stipulated the appointment procedures, which were also issued to all schools and published in the 200th issue of the Education Weekly. Now, it has been found that the second semester of the 22nd year has already started. Teachers in all schools should continue to serve according to the appointment period. Those who resign on their own or should be dismissed according to the regulations for appointment and dismissal must follow the prescribed procedures within two weeks after the start of the school year and submit them for approval. In addition to separate orders, this order is issued for compliance."

Xiangda Graduates Came to Shanghai for a Tour

A Group of Thirty-Nine People for a Week

Visited the Telephone Company and Glue Factory Yesterday

This year's graduates from the two colleges of science and engineering of Hunan University, a group of thirty-nine people, led by Dean Tang Ying of the College of Engineering, Professors Tong Kai, Yang Kaidong, etc., came to Shanghai from Nanjing yesterday morning for a tour. Details are as follows:

List of Team Members

The team includes thirty-six students. Ten from the Department of Electrical Engineering: Zhou Guangyan, Tang Shibo, Luo Zhinan, Wang Daochan, Li Yunchi, Zhan Jiazhi, Chen Nie, Gao Xianjian, etc. Nineteen from the Department of Civil Engineering: Tang Zuo, Tang Mingzhuo, He Wukan, Liu Shangheng, Liu Ganji, Zhu Tingyuan, Liu Shengru, Zou Shengyi, etc. Five from the Department of Chemistry: Yang Qionghua, Chen Deheng, Zheng Jiapei, Xu Guangjian, Yi Guohua, etc. Two from the Department of Mechanical Engineering: Li Binyuan, Lao Qishou, etc.

Tour Schedule

The tour group from the school departed from Changsha on January 30, visited Hankou for one day, visited Nanjing for two days, and took the night train to Shanghai on the 5th of this month. Yesterday, students from the Department of Electrical Engineering and the Department of Mechanical Engineering visited the Shanghai Telephone Company. Students from the Department of Civil Engineering and the Department of Chemistry visited the Chichang Glue Factory. The group will stay in Shanghai for about a week to visit the Electric Lamp Factory, the Electric Steam Company, the China Chemical Industry Society, the Tianyuan Electrochemical Factory, the Tianchu Flavoring Essence Factory, the Huasheng Electric Factory, the Aupu Ear Factory, the Water Company, and other great buildings. After a week, they will go to Hangzhou and Wuxi for a tour, and return to Hunan in two weeks. Students from the College of Liberal Arts will also come to Shanghai for a tour after the Lunar New Year.

School History

Hunan University is the highest institution of higher learning in Hunan Province, with a long history. It was founded in the Song Dynasty, originally named Yuelu Academy, where Zhu Xi and others lectured. It was later renamed Hunan Higher Industrial School and Higher Industrial College, specializing in engineering. It was not until the sixteenth year of the Republic of China that it was renamed its current name, with the establishment of the two colleges of science and engineering. Later, in accordance with the university regulations of the Ministry of Education, the College of Liberal Arts was added. Currently, there are about 500 students. The school's facilities, such as the science hall and library, are quite complete, and the scale is also very grand.

Contributions in Hunan

Graduates from the school have made many contributions while serving in Hunan. For example, almost all the officials and staff of the Hunan Highway Bureau are graduates from the Department of Civil Engineering of the school. The completion of the Hunan-Guangdong, Hunan-Sichuan, Hunan-Hubei, Hunan-Jiangxi, and Tanbao highways in Hunan Province are all due to the achievements of the students of the school. In addition, Huang Jianbai, a graduate from the Department of Mechanical Engineering of the school, is currently an engineer at the Hankou Jiji Water and Electricity Company. He has not studied abroad and recently invented a type of flying boat that can travel on both land and water, costing 200,000 yuan to build. Huang has already prepared one and is currently applying for registration with the government.

China Children's Education Society Invited to Join

International New Education Fellowship

The China Children's Education Society was invited to join the International New Education Fellowship, through the introduction of New Educationist Hua Xupeng from the United States. The Association had already sent letters to Chen Heqin and Dong Renjian to discuss everything. According to the Association, it was first organized in 1921 by new educators from various European countries, specifically to spread new ideas and methods of education and promote the implementation and improvement of general schools. Later, North America, South America, Japan, and other countries joined one after another, becoming an international organization for educational research. Figures such as Freinet of France, Kechstein of Germany, Decroly of Belgium, Montessori of Italy, and Dewey of the United States all participated. An annual meeting is held every year, and an annual report is published. Each member country also has its own journal. It is heard that the China Children's Education Society plans to make its Children's Education Monthly the educational journal of the Chinese branch of the Association.

The Raging Current Literary Society Initiates

The China Literary and Art Organizations Federation

Literary and Art Groups Across the Country Participate

Actively Proceeding with Establishment Soon

Reasons for Initiation

Recently, the Shanghai Raging Current Literary Society and many other famous literary and art groups in the country, in view of the lack of solid connections in the Chinese literary and art circles at the present stage, initiated the organization of the "China Literary and Art Organizations Federation" to unite literary and art groups across the country and jointly complete the Chinese new literary and art movement as its task. The association has been actively proceeding recently, and it is heard that literary and art groups from across the country, both domestic and overseas, as well as Nanyang and other places, have participated one after another and will soon be established, which will be a new phenomenon in the Chinese literary and art circles.

Declaration of the Association

The declaration of the association is as follows: "The mission of literature and art is to reflect the times and also to promote the times. However, the Chinese new literary and art movement has been sluggish in its development for more than ten years due to the turmoil of the entire social situation, which has formed an undeniable fact. Therefore, the Chinese literary circles at the present stage still remain in a state of chaos - and all feudal and anti-era literature and art can still prolong their lives. It is undoubtedly necessary for the Chinese new literary and art movement to accelerate its progress in order to eliminate the survival of feudal literature that hinders the times and lay the foundation for Chinese new literature and art. In order to accelerate the advancement of our new literary and art movement, in order to unite the Chinese literary and art circles to jointly shoulder the mission of completing the promotion of literature and art, it is of course urgently necessary to use the power of groups to promote this great task. Therefore, the "China Literary and Art Organizations Federation" was produced in response to the needs of this objective condition. We believe that many scattered literary and art groups in China have different environments and form different tendencies. However, we need to complete the Chinese new literary and art movement, need to shoulder the mission of the times, and move towards the bright road. This is completely consistent. Therefore, we understand our mission and deeply feel that Chinese literary and art groups need to work together. We welcome literary and art groups across the country to participate together, and we also hope that the literary and art organizations federations of countries around the world will enthusiastically respond to us in order to complete this great mission."

Recent Preparations

It is heard that the initiating group of the association, the Raging Current Literary Society, etc., has once convened a preparatory meeting by the persons in charge, Sheng Maliang, Shen Runliu, Zhao Liu, etc., to jointly plan the progress and decided to use the three major alliances of literature, drama, and fine arts to promote the organization of the China Literary and Art Organizations Federation. Furthermore, recently, in addition to the literary and art organizations federations of various countries around the world expressing their willingness to cooperate, they welcome groups across the country related to literature, drama, fine arts, etc. to participate and cooperate in order to promote China's new literary and art movement. The general preparatory office of the association is temporarily located at No. 5 Penglai Lane, Zhonghua Road, Ximen, Shanghai.

Sports

Tianjin Interport Football Team Tryout

-- 5-1 Great Victory over Fu Jen Catholic University --

The Tianjin Team's Offense and Defense Are Excellent, Making Their Strength Fearsome

Although Fu Jen Lost, Their Goalkeeping Performance Was Very Good

(Tianjin, 4th Dispatch) The Fu Jen Catholic University football team from Peiping has given the citizens of Tianjin an excellent impression since arriving in Tianjin on New Year's Day and achieving consecutive victories. The Tianjin team, which will participate in the Tianjin-Shanghai Interport Games, is about to depart, and specially invited the Fu Jen team to Tianjin to perform, so as to learn from each other. The team of fifteen arrived in Tianjin the night before last to prepare for the battle. Before 3 pm yesterday, they first went to the English field to try out their legs and take photos in time, and then lined up to start the game.

Tianjin Team Starts a Fierce Attack

The Tianjin team attacked from north to south, and the ball entered Fu Jen's territory, but was kicked back by Li Fenglou. The Tianjin team's rear was repeatedly threatened, but fortunately, the first defense fought hard to turn the danger into safety. The Tianjin team took the opportunity to launch a large-scale attack. Jones' header in front of Fu Jen's goal failed. In an instant, Johnson's foot failed. Before long, the Tianjin team launched another attack. Johnson and Aicher successively showed their skills, but they were easily passed out by Fu Jen goalkeeper Wang Yumin. Jones went up again on the edge, kicking a shot. Wang Yumin rushed out to save and slapped the ball out of the defense. After two or three rounds, the Fu Jen defense was in danger again.

Fu Jen's Goal Falls

Johnson dribbled forward, and Fenjie and Swiss also became ambitious. The Fu Jen goalkeeper received the ball and broke through the siege, crossing the difficult pass. Wu Youan got the ball and dribbled forward to continue the attack. Tianjin's McElroy did not neglect his duty, intercepted the ball and passed it forward. Fenjie and Swiss passed to the center forward again, and Aicher took advantage of the situation to head it to the dangerous corner of the goal. In an instant, Jones rushed over like the wind, and the ball rolled towards the goal. The goalkeeper ran out to catch the ball, but unfortunately fell, and the ball steadily spun into the net, and the record began. Fu Jen kicked off, and the Tianjin team was in danger again. Wang Jingxi dribbled the ball straight up, but kicked it out of bounds in front of the goal, missing the opportunity again. Tianjin midfielder Sun Sijing saw an opportunity and took a long shot. The ball fell towards Fu Jen's goal. Wang Yumin hurriedly patted it into a corner kick, and the first half ended at the same time.

Four More Goals Scored

After lemon time, the Tianjin team entered a dangerous situation. Fu Jen lost many goals due to the disorganization of their troops. Tianjin's Malcolm showed his heading skills. Another corner kick was formed next to Fu Jen's goal. Jiang Lu took the penalty. Wang Yumin jumped up and missed. Johnson rushed up and kicked it in, winning another goal. Five minutes later, Jiang Lu cleverly intercepted the ball. Johnson chased the ball straight up. Wang Yumin rushed out to save, opening the defense wide, and the ball entered the net again. During the re-battle, the Tianjin team attacked fiercely, and Ai succeeded in hitting the goal twice. Wang Yumin was injured and left the field, replaced by Cai Binxian. Tang Guobiao received the ball and passed it forward. Zhang Zhizhen lost his sock meeting again. Jiang Lu met the ball and restrained it back. Ai rushed straight up and broke into the new goal with his body. Cai Binxian was unable to save in time, resulting in a score of four to zero.

Fortunately Escaping Total Annihilation

The center kicked off again, and Lian Yanxun hurriedly passed it to Wang Jingxi. Wang dribbled the ball straight up. The Tianjin goal was forty yards away and the kick was off again. The ball slipped out in front of the goal. In an instant, the Tianjin team launched another attack. Ai knew the opportunity and took a long shot. The ball touched the goal post. Cai Bingxian was too late to return to save, and the ball lightly rushed in. After re-kicking off, not long after the fierce battle, Wang Jingxi moved on the edge again. After getting the ball, he rushed up alone. In front of the enemy's goal, he lured the tiger away from the mountain, and the ball was lightly pushed into the hole. Twenty seconds later, the bloody battle ended. The Fu Jen army was fortunate to avoid being shut out with a score of one to five.

Tianjin Team's Strength Is Impressive

In yesterday's battle, Fu Jen Catholic University, as a university team, fought against the essence of the Tianjin team, which is currently occupied by Western players. Although their strength is somewhat inferior, it is still impressive. Fu Jen's lineup was not tidy. The forwards' attack and shooting were weak, and there were very few opportunities. The defense was a time of trouble. The three defenders and two guards were rarely flawed. Danger was rampant in front of the goal, and Wang Yumin's contribution was the greatest in turning danger into safety. With the assistance of Fu Niu and Yang Puzhi, the left and right assistants complemented each other, so that the Interport star Johnson was not satisfied. The ball rotating and rolling in front of the goal was indeed unexpected. It is said that it is easy to dodge a spear in the open, but difficult to guard against an arrow in the dark. Interport player Heil performed the best, his bald head looked like iron, and he coped with ease. The defenders Da Silva and Della were steady and shrewd. The forward Johnson did not succeed at first, but after a few rushes to shoot, he was indeed extraordinary. Aicher was experienced and cunning, and his passing and picking were unique. Although Jiang Lu ran fast, his passes were difficult to use. Sun Sijing's performance yesterday was not brilliant, but his steadiness is still that of an old Huang Zhong. In short, Fu Jen's problem this time was that there was no one to respond. The ball saved by the defense was not responded to by the forwards for attack, and it was intercepted by the Interport team, resulting in a lack of opportunities to knock on the door. If the forwards were full of strength and added fierce shooting, the situation would be renewed. The fourth and fifth goals were officially scored after the goalkeeper was injured and left the field, and the substitutes were inexperienced and could not avoid negligence. Moreover, Interport players Johnson and Aicher are veteran shooters. In addition, the school's right winger and left forward Ye Delu and Zhao Xitian were unable to play due to illness, and their strength was not reduced.

Shanghai Basketball Association

Group A Is Not Worthy of Its Name

Three Games Last Night

Sea Dogs Defeat Gunners 73-24

Van Kings Defeat Jews 59-33

Macklings Defeat Datong 95-15

In this Shanghai Basketball Association, there were originally seventeen teams in Group A, divided into two divisions, one with nine teams and the other with eight. Standing Committee of the North China Games Preparatory Committee

(Central News Agency, Tianjin, 6th) The Preparatory Committee of the 18th North China Games, considering the large amount of cement and stone materials needed for the construction of the sports field and the considerable expense of telegrams to and from various provinces and cities, resolved during its regular meeting at the Provincial Government at noon on the 6th to separately request the Ministry of Railways and the Ministry of Communications to grant free transportation for cement, stone materials, and telegrams to and from them. The Skill of a Master Is Indeed Extraordinary

A Record of Smith's Performance on the First Day

▲ Cue Sports King Li Gongying is Energetic and Promising

▲ Today's Two Sessions Will Be Held at the Original Location

Willie Smith, the world-renowned professional cue sports master whom the Chinese and Western cue sports circles in Shanghai have been eagerly anticipating, demonstrated his skills at the United Chinese Association at No. 27 Beijing Road yesterday afternoon at 6:00 PM, with two sessions, one in the afternoon and one in the evening. More than two hundred spectators watched, and all were deeply impressed and amazed. Even Cue Sports King Li Gongying, in the face of such a formidable and unfathomable opponent, was able to bravely display his independent spirit, scoring 660 points in 40 shots, averaging 16.5 points per shot, a significant improvement over his previous performance. Today's two sessions will be held at the original location, the first session at 6:00 PM this afternoon, originally scheduled for Shen Lince. Mr. Shen is absent from Shanghai due to business, so Mr. Li will still take the stage. The second session will be at 9:15 PM this evening, and our country's rising star, Xu Shizhang, will take the stage to compete.

Coming from Behind

A total of three famous professional cue sports players have visited Shanghai: Faulkner, Gray, and this time Smith. Shanghai Cue Sports King Li Gongying is a student of Gray. It is conceivable that a famous teacher produces excellent students, and Gray's skills are excellent. However, according to those who have witnessed the skills of these three gentlemen, Smith's skills are even higher than the former. This is also a good phenomenon of progress in the professional cue sports world. Smith's past career has been mostly published in this newspaper yesterday and the day before, but there is still one thing that is worth supplementing. Smith once competed with Lindrum for the World Professional Championship, and they faced off five times. Smith lost by two to three, so the World Professional Championship is still in Lindrum's hands.

An All-Around Master

Smith has been proficient in this skill since he was a child, and he has been a professional in this field for 23 years. It is fitting that he is capable of all kinds of techniques on the six-pocket rectangular green table. His best skill is to attract the red ball and the opponent's ball to converge around the red ball spot, and then open, send the red, self-fall, and cycle endlessly, saving effort and being effective. After the two-person competition is over, the individual will make a special performance, like the after-show after the main drama. Techniques such as flying balls, circling, and hitting champagne baskets are novel and worth watching, and the methods of instructing how to hold the cue, hold the palm, and position the steps seem to be quite beneficial to newcomers.

Course of the Competition

The performance competition does not focus on winning or losing. Each person takes 40 shots. Smith scored 1950 points, and Li Gongying scored 660 points. Smith's last shot scored 333 points, which was the highest score of the day, followed by 276, 259, 181, 144, 130, 123, 106, averaging 48.7 points per shot. Li Gongying's large numbers were 100, 72, 42, 41, 30, etc., averaging 16.5 points per shot. However, Mr. Li missed a total of seven shots, while Smith missed as many as twelve times. This shows that Mr. Li's calmness is more evident.

Securities

Government Bonds Lack the Strength to Rise

All Prices Are Already at Their Peak

Yesterday, at the Chinese Securities Exchange, as the end of the year approached, the short forces' barrier gradually wavered, and the exchange and settlement transactions surged slightly, and the market price saw a strong rise. This was a reaction to the many days of hovering, seemingly not falling and seemingly not rising. Most people believed that shorting at this high market price was relatively less dangerous, but although there were many shorts, the bulls were very stable. After holding on for a long time, the shorts failed again. At the opening in the morning, covering suddenly rose, and No. 5 and No. 50 were bought quite a bit. No. 20 and No. 21 also had needs. The shorts on No. 75 also had exchanges, and the bond markets all rose sharply, gaining 1 to 2 jiao to 5 to 6 jiao. In the second round, there was still covering, and the disarmament surged 5 jiao, seeing a new high price of 69 yuan and 2 jiao. The other types also generally continued to rise slightly. The salt tax saw a new high price of 52 yuan, which was in line with the reporter's prediction. At the opening in the afternoon, some of the floating bulls came out, falling back by 1 to 3 jiao and a half. The closing prices were also mostly down by 1 to 2 jiao. This is the cause and effect of sudden rises and falls, and also the cycle of not being stupid and escaping. Because the market price still has the possibility of continuing to rise, it is actually already at its peak, and the strength to rise is more difficult than the rise from a lower price. Therefore, at this time, a rise of a slightly large amount will inevitably have a return of the wind, but it is not a fall immediately. The market price ultimately continued to rise by 1 to 2 jiao to 7 to 8 jiao. As a result, spot goods did not move, and futures rose by 2 to 5 points. Liverpool spot cotton rose by 21 points, and futures rose by 15 to 6 points. Egyptian cotton spot goods rose by 22 points. The Bombay cotton market initially rose because speculators and scattered Japanese merchants bought, and then fell back due to some European exporters selling. As a result, the flat price rose by 1.5 rupees, Aomura rose by 4 rupees and 7.5 jiao, and Bairuo Creek rose by 6 rupees. The original telegram is recorded on the left (5th telegram).

Grain

Factories Dump Forward Flour

- Drops of About 1.5 Cents Each Month -

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning, the market for each month showed a sluggish appearance again. The quoted price of foreign wheat also fluctuated uncertainly, such as Chicago up 1.10, Canada up 4/8, only the market sentiment, due to the factory's continued foreign wheat transaction the day before, for the far period flour, naturally took the opportunity to get out. So the market atmosphere was empty and soft, and the buying was very quiet. Until the afternoon opening, the market atmosphere for each month, generally hovering, although the factory wanted to dump, but very few buyers, just lacking counterparties. According to the current situation, the weak purchasing power is felt. Even if there are large bulls, it is not easy to support it. As a result, this month remained unchanged from the previous day, March and April fell 1.25 cents, May fell 1.5 cents, June fell 1.75 cents, July only opened at 5.5 cents in the morning, calculated a drop of 2.5 cents, and did not open in the afternoon.

Downriver Rice Prices Stabilized

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, only over twenty ships arrived from various gangs (over three thousand stones), of which only three or four were thick japonica, and the rest were late rice. However, although the retail and wholesale sales channels were prosperous, there were still many remaining goods, so the market showed a stable situation. For other goods such as Qingjiao, Songsi, and Xitang, the Northern Ocean gang continued to accept over two thousand packages, and the market prices did not fluctuate. For Chang Gang’s japonica from Sutong, Nangang, etc., store sales remained unbroken, and the market prices did not rise or fall. However, Du Yangjian continued to weaken by nearly a cent due to sluggish sales, and the supply of Bian Yin Yuan exceeded demand, so the market looked slightly bearish.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, twenty-one or two ships arrived from various places downriver. Sales in the market were sluggish and prices were cleverly adjusted. Market prices for white japonica and Yang Du, port customer tip prices, were down several cents. White Yuan and Yin Yuan were stable, and early thin rice prices were down by nearly a cent.

Foreign Ke Xian Rice Inventory in Shanghai at 560,000 Bags

100,000 Bags More Than the Same Period Last Year

Due to the cessation of acceptance and the stoppage, the total inventory of foreign Ke Xian rice reached 560,000 bags, 100,000 bags more than last year. However, last year's inventory included only 40,000 bags of domestic Ke Xian rice, while this year there are as many as 350,000 bags. Detailed numbers are as follows:

Miscellaneous Grains Inventory Survey

Starting yesterday, all miscellaneous grains except soybeans have been off the market. Soybean transactions were also minimal, with a total turnover of about three cars. During this closing period, the inventories of various grains are listed below: approximately 100,000 packages of various cartwheel beans, 40 cars of Dalian soybeans, 200,000 packages of Hankou beans, 1,600 packages of Andong beans, 1,000 packages of Pudong Du beans, 1,000 packages of Pinghu Du beans, 600 packages of Jiujiang Late beans, 1,200 packages of Jiujiang Mixed Green beans, 1,000 packages of Liuhe Mixed Green beans, 3,000 packages of Niuzhuang Black beans, 2,000 packages of Pinghu Black beans, 350 packages of Jiujiang Black beans, 3,000 packages of Chongming Red beans, 5 cars of Dalian Green beans, 40,000 packages of various Green beans, 2,500 packages of various Cowpeas, 62,000 packages of various Sesame seeds, 120,000 packages of various Raw kernels, 5,000 packages of various Peanuts, 2 cars of Niuzhuang Corn, 1,500 packages of Mingguang Red Grain, and 3 cars of Niuzhuang Red Grain.

Silk and Tea

Good Situation in Overseas Silk Market

(Yokohama Raw Silk Rises Sharply) Recently, the Yokohama raw silk market has seen sharp rises in silk prices due to the launch of silk sales in Europe and America. Both spot silk and futures silk have risen to over 680-690 yen, an increase of 30-40 yen compared to the middle of last month, and the exchange rate to Chinese currency has broken through the 600 yuan mark.

(Wuxi Factory Merchants Transport to Shanghai for Sale) Recently, due to the launch of spring sales in the Shanghai foreign firm silk market, European firms have started to purchase, and American sales have also gradually turned around. Therefore, Wuxi manufacturers are actively transporting stored silk to Shanghai for sale. In recent days, Jinji, Zhenyi, and other factories have shipped 120 packages of white factory silk with the "Golden Double Deer," "Double Deer," and "Moon Rabbit" brands, which have already been put on the shelves for sale.

(European and American Factory Orders Received) In the overseas raw silk market, due to active factory orders, most of the silk in the hands of general importers has been sold, and inventories are gradually thinning. New York Ang Li silk prices have continued to rise. New orders for yellow and white factory silk have continued to come from overseas. Unfortunately, the incoming price of New York white factory silk is still 40-50 yuan different from the cost of various factories, so negotiations are still difficult to conclude. Yesterday, French firms and others imported 40 packages of white factory silk and 20 packages of yellow factory silk, and prices were firm and rising.

Hardware

Horse Shoe Nail Sales Turning Active

Horse shoe nails have recently been inquired about by guest merchants, and embellishments in this street are also very prosperous. Therefore, even before the closing period, over three to four hundred boxes have been transacted. Prices are as follows: No. 5 opens at 16.5 yuan per box, No. 6 at 17 yuan, No. 7 at 17.25 yuan, and No. 8 at 17.35 yuan. Yesterday, incoming prices from overseas have increased, so the local market has a stable appearance.

Pig Lead Temporarily Shows No Signs of Improvement

The trend of pig lead has recently remained normal. Therefore, according to industry insiders, it is feared that there will be no signs of improvement within the old lunar year. The market situation shows no opportunity for progress. Although various colleagues feel the need to increase prices due to cost concerns, they ultimately have no way to make prices rise.
